## Callbacks

Define any of these in `main.lua`. All are optional.

```lua
  function lurek.load()                                    end  -- called once after script loads
  function lurek.update(dt)                                end  -- dt: number; called every frame before draw
  function lurek.draw()                                    end  -- called every frame; push draw commands here
  function lurek.keypressed(key, scancode, isrepeat)       end  -- key: string; isrepeat: bool
  function lurek.keyreleased(key, scancode)                end  -- key: string; scancode: string
  function lurek.textinput(text)                           end  -- text: string; Unicode character input
  function lurek.mousepressed(x, y, button)                end  -- button: 1=left 2=right 3=middle
  function lurek.mousereleased(x, y, button)               end  -- button: number
  function lurek.wheelmoved(x, y)                          end  -- x,y: scroll delta this frame
  function lurek.input.gamepadpressed(id, button)          end  -- id: number; button: string
  function lurek.input.gamepadreleased(id, button)         end  -- id: number; button: string
  function lurek.input.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)        end  -- value: -1.0 to 1.0
  function lurek.joystickadded(id)                         end  -- gamepad connected
  function lurek.joystickremoved(id)                       end  -- gamepad disconnected
  function lurek.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)  end  -- touch start
  function lurek.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)    end  -- touch move
  function lurek.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure) end  -- touch end
  function lurek.focus(focused)                            end  -- focused: bool; window focus changed
  function lurek.visible(visible)                          end  -- visible: bool; window hidden or shown
  function lurek.resize(w, h)                              end  -- w, h: new window dimensions
  function lurek.quit()                                    end  -- return true to cancel shutdown
  function lurek.errorhandler(msg)                         end  -- return replacement string or nil
```

## lurek.render {#render}

> Immediate-mode 2D rendering: images, shapes, text, canvas, shaders, blend modes, transforms.

```lua

  lurek.render.currentLayer( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the currently active named layer.

  lurek.render.isWireframe( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether wireframe mode is active.
  lurek.render.line( ... )  -> nil  -- Draws a line between two points.
  lurek.render.newCanvas( width, height )  -> LCanvas  -- Creates an off-screen render canvas.
  lurek.render.newDrawLayer( )  -> LDrawLayer  -- Creates a new z-ordered draw-call queue.

  lurek.render.setShader( [ud] )  -> nil  -- Sets the active shader, or clears it.
  lurek.render.setStencilMode( action, [compare], [value] )  -> nil  -- Sets the stencil buffer write/test mode.
  lurek.render.setStencilTest( [compare], [value] )  -> nil  -- Sets the stencil comparison test, or disables stencil testing.
  lurek.render.setWireframe( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables wireframe rendering.
  lurek.render.shear( kx, ky )  -> nil  -- Shears the coordinate system.
  lurek.render.stencil( [action], [value] )  -> nil  -- Begins stencil writing with the given action and value.
  lurek.render.translate( x, y )  -> nil  -- Translates the coordinate system.
  lurek.render.triangle( mode, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3 )  -> nil  -- Draws a filled or outlined triangle connecting three world-space vertices.
```

**`LCanvas`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to an off-screen render target stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LCanvas:getDimensions( )  -> integer  -- Returns width and height of this canvas.
  LCanvas:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the height of this canvas in pixels.
  LCanvas:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the width of this canvas in pixels.
  LCanvas:release( )  -> boolean  -- Releases GPU framebuffer memory for this canvas.
  LCanvas:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this canvas handle.
  LCanvas:typeOf( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this canvas object.
```

**`LDrawLayer`** methods:

> Lua-side z-ordered draw queue. Callbacks are sorted by z and called on `flush()`.

```lua
  LDrawLayer:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all queued callbacks without calling them.
  LDrawLayer:flush( )  -> nil  -- Sorts and calls all queued callbacks, then empties the queue.
  LDrawLayer:getCount( )  -> number  -- Returns the number of queued callbacks.
  LDrawLayer:queue( z, f )  -> nil  -- Queues a draw callback at the given z-order.
  LDrawLayer:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the string type identifier of this draw layer (for example `LDrawLayer`).
  LDrawLayer:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is an instance of the given type name.
```

**`LFont`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a loaded font stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LFont:getAscent( )  -> number  -- Returns the ascent of this font in pixels.
  LFont:getDescent( )  -> number  -- Returns the descent of this font in pixels.
  LFont:getHeight( )  -> number  -- Returns the line height of this font.
  LFont:getLineHeight( )  -> number  -- Returns the line height multiplier of this font.
  LFont:getWidth( text )  -> number  -- Returns the rendered width of the given text string.
  LFont:getWrap( text, limit )  -> table  -- Wraps text to the given width and returns the lines.
  LFont:release( )  -> boolean  -- Releases this font and frees its atlas memory.
  LFont:setLineHeight( height )  -> nil  -- Sets the line height multiplier for this font.
  LFont:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this font handle.
  LFont:typeOf( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this font object.
```

**`LImage`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a loaded GPU texture stored in the engine's texture pool.

```lua
  LImage:getDimensions( )  -> integer  -- Returns width and height of this image.
  LImage:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the height of this image in pixels.
  LImage:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the width of this image in pixels.
  LImage:release( )  -> boolean  -- Releases the GPU texture memory for this image.
  LImage:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this image handle.
  LImage:typeOf( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this image object.
```

**`LImageData`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a loaded texture stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LImageData:blit( src_ud, dst_x, dst_y )  -> nil  -- Blits another image buffer onto this image at the destination position.
  LImageData:diff( other_ud )  -> integer  -- Returns the summed per-channel difference between this image and another image.
  LImageData:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the pixel height of this image buffer.
  LImageData:getRegion( x, y, w, h )  -> LImageData  -- Returns a copy of a rectangular region from this image buffer.
  LImageData:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the pixel width of this image buffer.
  LImageData:mapPixels( callback )  -> nil  -- Applies a Lua callback to each pixel in this image buffer.
  LImageData:resize( w, h )  -> LImageData  -- Returns a resized copy of this image buffer.
  LImageData:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this image data object.
  LImageData:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this object matches a requested type name.
```

**`LMesh`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a mesh stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LMesh:getVertex( index )  -> number  -- Returns vertex data at the given 1-based index.
  LMesh:getVertexCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of vertices in this mesh.
  LMesh:release( )  -> boolean  -- Releases the GPU mesh resource, freeing VRAM immediately.
  LMesh:setTexture( [ud] )  -> nil  -- Assigns a texture to this mesh.
  LMesh:setVertex( index, data )  -> nil  -- Sets vertex data at the given 1-based index.
  LMesh:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this mesh handle.
  LMesh:typeOf( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this mesh object.
```

**`LNineSlice`** methods:

> Lua-side 9-slice descriptor.

```lua
  LNineSlice:getInsets( )  -> number  -- Returns the four inset values as (top, right, bottom, left).
  LNineSlice:getTextureSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the width and height of the source texture.

```

```lua
  LQuad:getTextureDimensions( )  -> number  -- Returns the reference texture dimensions.

  LQuad:setViewport( x, y, w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the quad viewport rectangle.

```

**`LShader`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a compiled shader stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LShader:hasUniform( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this shader has a uniform with the given name.
  LShader:release( )  -> boolean  -- Releases the compiled GPU shader, freeing VRAM and shader slots.
  LShader:send( name, value )  -> nil  -- Sends a uniform value to this shader.
  LShader:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this shader handle.
  LShader:typeOf( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this shader object.
```

**`LShape`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a [`CompoundShape`] stored in [`SharedState::shapes`].

```lua
  LShape:arc( )  -> nil  -- Queues a filled or outlined arc draw command onto this shape.
  LShape:circle( mode, x, y, r )  -> nil  -- Queues a filled or outlined circle draw command onto this shape.
  LShape:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all commands and resets the shape to empty.
  LShape:draw( )  -> nil  -- Queues this shape for drawing at the given position.
  LShape:ellipse( mode, x, y, rx, ry )  -> nil  -- Queues an ellipse command.
  LShape:getCommandCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of drawing commands currently stored.
  LShape:line( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> nil  -- Queues a line segment command.
  LShape:polygon( mode, coords )  -> nil  -- Queues a polygon command from variadic (x, y) coordinate pairs.
  LShape:polyline( )  -> nil  -- Queues a polyline command from variadic (x, y) coordinate pairs.
  LShape:rectangle( mode, x, y, w, h )  -> nil  -- Queues a rectangle command.
  LShape:roundedRectangle( mode, x, y, w, h, rx, [ry] )  -> nil  -- Queues a rounded rectangle command.
  LShape:setColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -> nil  -- Sets the drawing color for subsequent primitives.
  LShape:setLineWidth( w )  -> nil  -- Sets the stroke width for subsequent outlined primitives.
  LShape:triangle( mode, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3 )  -> nil  -- Queues a triangle command.
  LShape:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this shape handle.
  LShape:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this object matches a requested type name.
```

**`LSpriteBatch`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a sprite batch stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LSpriteBatch:add( )  -> integer  -- Adds a sprite entry to this batch.
  LSpriteBatch:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all sprites from this batch.
  LSpriteBatch:getBufferSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum capacity of this batch.
  LSpriteBatch:getCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of sprites in this batch.
  LSpriteBatch:release( )  -> boolean  -- Releases this sprite batch.
  LSpriteBatch:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this sprite batch handle.
  LSpriteBatch:typeOf( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name for this sprite batch object.
```

## lurek.audio {#audio}

> Sound playback: load audio files, play/pause/stop, volume, pitch, looping, panning.

```lua
  lurek.audio.add_effect( bus_name, effect_type_str, [params] )  -> integer  -- Adds a DSP effect to a bus.
  lurek.audio.applyBandpass( sd_ud, low_hz, high_hz )  -> nil  -- Applies a bandpass filter (high-pass then low-pass) to a SoundData in-place.
  lurek.audio.applyGain( sd_ud, gain )  -> nil  -- Scales every sample by gain (clamped to [-1, 1]).
  lurek.audio.applyHighpass( sd_ud, cutoff_hz )  -> nil  -- Applies a first-order IIR high-pass filter to a SoundData in-place.
  lurek.audio.applyLowpass( sd_ud, cutoff_hz )  -> nil  -- Applies a first-order IIR low-pass filter to a SoundData in-place.
  lurek.audio.clearFilter( id_val )  -> nil  -- Removes any active filter from a source.
  lurek.audio.clearMidiSoundFont( )  -> nil  -- Unloads the active SoundFont.
  lurek.audio.clearRandomPitch( src_ud )  -> nil  -- Clears any random pitch range on a source, restoring fixed pitch.
  lurek.audio.clone( id_val )  -> LSource  -- Creates an independent copy of a source.
  lurek.audio.create_bus( name, [parent_name] )  -> nil  -- Creates a bus by name (functional style).
  lurek.audio.crossfade( from_ud, to_ud, duration )  -> nil  -- Crossfades from one source to another over a duration.
  lurek.audio.fadeIn( id_val, dur )  -> nil  -- Fades a source in from silence over the given duration.
  lurek.audio.getActiveSourceCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of currently playing sources.
  lurek.audio.getBusPeak( bus_name )  -> number  -- Returns the peak signal level of the named bus (stub: always 0.0).
  lurek.audio.getBusRms( bus_name )  -> number  -- Returns the RMS signal level of the named bus (stub: always 0.0).
  lurek.audio.getDistanceModel( )  -> string  -- Returns the current distance model name.
  lurek.audio.getDopplerScale( )  -> number  -- Returns the current Doppler scale.
  lurek.audio.getDuration( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the total duration of a source in seconds.
  lurek.audio.getFadeIn( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the fade-in duration of a source.
  lurek.audio.getFreeBufferCount( qsource_id )  -> integer  -- Returns the free buffer slots in a queueable source.
  lurek.audio.getHighpass( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the high-pass filter cutoff of a source.

  lurek.audio.getListener2D( )  -> number  -- Returns the 2D listener position (x, y).
  lurek.audio.getLowpass( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the low-pass filter cutoff of a source.
  lurek.audio.getMasterVolume( )  -> number  -- Returns the global master volume.
  lurek.audio.getMaxSources( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum number of simultaneous sources.
  lurek.audio.getMeter( )  -> number  -- Returns the stored master peak meter level.
  lurek.audio.getOrientation( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the 6-component orientation of a source.
  lurek.audio.getPan( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the source stereo panning.
  lurek.audio.getPitch( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the source pitch multiplier.
  lurek.audio.getPlaybackDevice( )  -> string  -- Returns the current audio output device name.
  lurek.audio.getPlaybackDevices( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of available audio output device names.
  lurek.audio.getPosition( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the 3D position of a source (x, y, z).

  lurek.audio.getVelocity( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the velocity of a source (x, y, z).
  lurek.audio.getVolume( id_val )  -> number  -- Returns the source volume.
  lurek.audio.hasMidiSoundFont( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a SoundFont is loaded.
  lurek.audio.isLooping( id_val )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if looping is enabled.
  lurek.audio.isPaused( id_val )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the source is paused.
  lurek.audio.isPlaying( id_val )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the source is playing.
  lurek.audio.isStopped( id_val )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the source is stopped.
  lurek.audio.mixInto( dest_ud, src_ud )  -> nil  -- Additively mixes another SoundData into the destination in-place.
  lurek.audio.newBus( name )  -> LBus  -- Creates a named audio bus for grouping sources.

  lurek.audio.seek( id_val, pos )  -> nil  -- Seeks to a time position in seconds.
  lurek.audio.setDistanceModel( model )  -> nil  -- Sets the distance attenuation model.
  lurek.audio.setDopplerScale( scale )  -> nil  -- Sets the global Doppler effect scale.
  lurek.audio.setHighpass( id_val, cutoff_hz )  -> nil  -- Applies a high-pass filter to a source.
  lurek.audio.setListener( x, y, [z] )  -> nil  -- Sets the 3D listener position.
  lurek.audio.setListener2D( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the 2D listener position for spatial audio.
  lurek.audio.setLooping( id_val, looping )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables looping.
  lurek.audio.setLowpass( id_val, cutoff_hz )  -> nil  -- Applies a low-pass filter to a source.
  lurek.audio.setMasterVolume( vol )  -> nil  -- Sets the global master volume.

  lurek.audio.setPlaybackDevice( name )  -> nil  -- Selects an audio output device by name.
  lurek.audio.setPosition( id_val, x, y, [z] )  -> nil  -- Sets the 3D position of a source.
  lurek.audio.setRandomPitch( src_ud, min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets a random pitch range applied each time the source is played.
  lurek.audio.setSourceBus( id_val, bus_val )  -> nil  -- Assigns a source to a bus.
  lurek.audio.setStereoWidth( src_ud, width )  -> nil  -- Sets the stereo width multiplier for a source (1.0 = normal, 0.0 = mono).
  lurek.audio.setVelocity( id_val, x, y, [z] )  -> nil  -- Sets the velocity of a source for Doppler.
  lurek.audio.setVolume( id_val, vol )  -> nil  -- Sets source playback volume.

  lurek.audio.waveformToPng( input, output, width, height )  -> nil  -- Renders the waveform of a WAV file to a PNG image.
```

**`LBus`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for an audio bus resource.

```lua
  LBus:clearDuck( )  -> nil  -- Removes the ducking target from this bus.
  LBus:getName( )  -> string  -- Returns the unique name string assigned to this audio bus.
  LBus:getPeak( )  -> number  -- Returns the average peak amplitude of all sources on this bus.
  LBus:getPitch( )  -> number  -- Returns the bus pitch multiplier.
  LBus:getVolume( )  -> number  -- Returns the current volume multiplier applied to all sources on this bus.
  LBus:isPaused( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this bus is paused.
  LBus:pause( )  -> nil  -- Pauses all sources on this bus.
  LBus:resume( )  -> nil  -- Resumes all sources on this bus.
  LBus:setDuckTarget( target_name, duck_vol )  -> nil  -- Configures this bus to duck another bus while it has active sources.
  LBus:setPitch( pitch )  -> nil  -- Sets the pitch multiplier for all sources on this bus.
  LBus:setVolume( vol )  -> nil  -- Sets the volume for all sources on this bus.
  LBus:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LBus:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

> Lua-side wrapper for a streaming audio decoder.

```lua
  LDecoder:decode( )  -> SoundData  -- Decodes the next chunk of samples, or nil at EOF.
  LDecoder:getBitDepth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the per-sample bit depth of this decoded audio stream.
  LDecoder:getChannelCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of audio channels.
  LDecoder:getDuration( )  -> number  -- Returns the total duration in seconds.
  LDecoder:getSampleRate( )  -> integer  -- Returns the sample rate in Hz.
  LDecoder:isSeekable( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if seeking is supported.
  LDecoder:release( )  -> nil  -- Releases the decoder (no-op).
  LDecoder:rewind( )  -> nil  -- Rewinds to the beginning.
  LDecoder:seek( offset )  -> nil  -- Seeks to a time offset in seconds.
  LDecoder:tell( )  -> number  -- Returns the current position in seconds.
  LDecoder:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LDecoder:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LMidiPlayer`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for the MIDI player.

```lua
  LMidiPlayer:getBus( )  -> LBus  -- Returns the assigned bus, or nil.
  LMidiPlayer:getChannelCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of MIDI channels.
  LMidiPlayer:getChannelInstrument( ch )  -> integer  -- Returns the GM instrument for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:getChannelVolume( ch )  -> number  -- Returns the volume for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:getChannels( )  -> integer  -- Returns the PCM output channel count (1 = mono, 2 = stereo).

  LMidiPlayer:getFilePath( )  -> string  -- Returns the file path of the loaded MIDI, or nil.
  LMidiPlayer:getNoteCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total note count in the MIDI sequence.

  LMidiPlayer:getTempo( )  -> number  -- Returns the current tempo in BPM.
  LMidiPlayer:getTempoScale( )  -> number  -- Returns the current tempo scale factor.

  LMidiPlayer:getTrackCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of tracks in the MIDI sequence.

  LMidiPlayer:getVolume( )  -> number  -- Returns the current MIDI volume.
  LMidiPlayer:isChannelMuted( ch )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a MIDI channel is muted (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:isLoaded( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a MIDI sequence is loaded.
  LMidiPlayer:isLooping( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if looping is enabled.
  LMidiPlayer:isPaused( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if MIDI playback is paused.
  LMidiPlayer:isPlaying( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if MIDI is currently playing.
  LMidiPlayer:isTrackMuted( idx )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a track is muted (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:load( path )  -> boolean  -- Loads a MIDI file from the given path.
  LMidiPlayer:loadData( )  -> boolean  -- Loads MIDI data from a Lua string.
  LMidiPlayer:pause( )  -> nil  -- Pauses the MIDI sequence at the current position; resume with `play()`.
  LMidiPlayer:play( )  -> nil  -- Starts or resumes MIDI sequence playback from the current position.
  LMidiPlayer:seek( secs )  -> nil  -- Seeks to a time position in seconds.
  LMidiPlayer:setBus( bus_val )  -> nil  -- Routes MIDI output through a bus (or nil to clear).
  LMidiPlayer:setChannelInstrument( ch, inst )  -> nil  -- Sets the GM instrument for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:setChannelMuted( ch, muted )  -> nil  -- Mutes or unmutes a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:setChannelVolume( ch, vol )  -> nil  -- Sets volume for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:setChannels( channels )  -> nil  -- Sets the PCM output channel count (clamped 1-2).
  LMidiPlayer:setLooping( looping )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables looping.
  LMidiPlayer:setOnEnd( cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a playback-end callback (stub).
  LMidiPlayer:setOnNoteOff( cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a note-off callback (stub).
  LMidiPlayer:setOnNoteOn( cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a note-on callback (stub).
  LMidiPlayer:setSampleRate( rate )  -> nil  -- Sets the PCM output sample rate in Hz (clamped 8000-192000).
  LMidiPlayer:setSoundFont( path )  -> nil  -- Loads a SoundFont file into this player (stub).
  LMidiPlayer:setTempo( bpm )  -> nil  -- Sets playback tempo in BPM.
  LMidiPlayer:setTempoScale( scale )  -> nil  -- Sets the tempo scale factor (1.0 = original speed).
  LMidiPlayer:setTrackMuted( idx, muted )  -> nil  -- Mutes or unmutes a track (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:setVolume( vol )  -> nil  -- Sets MIDI playback volume.
  LMidiPlayer:soloChannel( ch )  -> nil  -- Solos a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  LMidiPlayer:stop( )  -> nil  -- Stops MIDI playback and resets the playhead to the beginning.
  LMidiPlayer:tell( )  -> number  -- Returns the current playback position in seconds.
  LMidiPlayer:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LMidiPlayer:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LMidiPlayer:unsoloAll( )  -> nil  -- Clears solo on all channels.
  LMidiPlayer:useDefaultSoundFont( )  -> nil  -- Reverts to the built-in default SoundFont (stub).
```

## lurek.timer {#timer}

> Frame timing: delta time, FPS, sleep, scheduled callbacks.

```lua
  lurek.timer.afterReal( delay, func )  -> nil  -- Schedules a one-shot callback that fires after `delay` wall-clock seconds, completely u...
  lurek.timer.chain( steps )  -> LScheduler  -- Creates a new Scheduler pre-loaded with a sequence of one-shot callbacks that fire in o...
  lurek.timer.getAverageDelta( )  -> number  -- Returns a rolling average of recent frame delta times in seconds.
  lurek.timer.getDelta( )  -> number  -- Returns the time elapsed since the previous frame in seconds.
  lurek.timer.getFPS( )  -> number  -- Returns the current instantaneous frames-per-second as measured by the engine clock.
  lurek.timer.getFrameCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of frames that have been rendered since the engine was initial...
  lurek.timer.getMicroTime( )  -> number  -- Returns the high-resolution (microsecond-precision) elapsed time since engine start in ...
  lurek.timer.getPhysicsDelta( )  -> number  -- Returns the fixed timestep interval used by the `process_physics` callback loop, in sec...
  lurek.timer.getPhysicsMaxSteps( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum number of physics simulation sub-steps that the engine will perform...
  lurek.timer.getSmoothedDelta( )  -> number  -- Returns the exponentially smoothed frame delta time in seconds.
  lurek.timer.getTime( )  -> number  -- Returns the total wall-clock time that has elapsed since the engine was initialised, in...
  lurek.timer.newScheduler( )  -> LScheduler  -- Creates and returns a new independent Scheduler userdata object for managing timed and ...
  lurek.timer.setPhysicsDelta( dt )  -> nil  -- Sets the fixed timestep interval for the `process_physics` callback loop, in seconds.
  lurek.timer.setPhysicsMaxSteps( n )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum number of physics simulation sub-steps allowed per frame.
  lurek.timer.setSmoothingFactor( alpha )  -> nil  -- Sets the exponential moving-average smoothing factor (alpha) used by `getSmoothedDelta`.
  lurek.timer.sleep( seconds )  -> nil  -- Blocks the current thread for the specified number of seconds using an OS-level sleep.
  lurek.timer.step( )  -> number  -- Manually advances the engine timer by one frame tick and returns the resulting delta time.
  lurek.timer.tickRealTimers( )  -> integer  -- Checks all registered real-time timers and fires any whose wall-clock deadline has passed.
  lurek.timer.tickWaits( )  -> integer  -- Resumes all coroutines waiting via `waitSeconds` or `waitFrames` whose deadline or fram...
  lurek.timer.waitFrames( frames )  -> nil  -- Yields the current Lua coroutine until at least `frames` engine frames have elapsed.
  lurek.timer.waitSeconds( seconds )  -> nil  -- Yields the current Lua coroutine for at least `seconds` wall-clock seconds.
```

**`LScheduler`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Scheduler`] with per-event callback storage.

```lua
  LScheduler:after( delay, func )  -> integer  -- Schedules a callback to fire once after a delay.
  LScheduler:afterFrames( n, func )  -> integer  -- Schedules a callback to fire once after `n` frames.
  LScheduler:afterNamed( name, delay, func )  -> integer  -- Schedules a named one-shot callback, replacing any existing event with the same name.
  LScheduler:cancel( id )  -> boolean  -- Cancels a scheduled event by its numeric ID.
  LScheduler:cancelAll( )  -> integer  -- Cancels all scheduled events and returns the count removed.
  LScheduler:cancelNamed( name )  -> boolean  -- Cancels and removes a previously scheduled event identified by its string name assigned...
  LScheduler:every( interval, func, [count] )  -> integer  -- Schedules a callback to fire repeatedly at the given interval.
  LScheduler:everyFrames( n, func, [count] )  -> integer  -- Schedules a callback to fire every `n` frames.
  LScheduler:everyNamed( name, interval, func, [count] )  -> integer  -- Schedules a named repeating callback, replacing any existing event with the same name.
  LScheduler:getCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of currently active (not yet completed or cancelled) events in...
  LScheduler:getInterval( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the event exists and its configured base interval in seconds.
  LScheduler:getRemaining( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the event exists and how many seconds remain until it fires next.
  LScheduler:getRepeatCount( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the event exists and its remaining repetition count.
  LScheduler:getTimeScale( )  -> number  -- Returns the current time-scale multiplier for this scheduler instance.
  LScheduler:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this scheduler has zero active events.
  LScheduler:isPaused( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given event is currently paused.
  LScheduler:isPausedNamed( name )  -> boolean  -- Checks whether the named scheduled event is currently in the paused state.
  LScheduler:pause( id )  -> boolean  -- Pauses a scheduled event by its ID.
  LScheduler:pauseNamed( name )  -> boolean  -- Temporarily suspends the named scheduled event so it stops accumulating time.
  LScheduler:resetEvent( id )  -> boolean  -- Resets the countdown for a scheduled event back to its full configured interval, as if ...
  LScheduler:resume( id )  -> boolean  -- Resumes a paused event by its ID.
  LScheduler:resumeNamed( name )  -> boolean  -- Resumes a previously paused named event so it continues accumulating time.
  LScheduler:setInterval( id, interval )  -> boolean  -- Modifies the repeat interval of an already-scheduled repeating event.
  LScheduler:setTimeScale( scale )  -> nil  -- Sets a time-scale multiplier that affects all events in this scheduler.
  LScheduler:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the string type name of this userdata object.
  LScheduler:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Checks whether this object matches the given type name.
  LScheduler:update( dt )  -> integer  -- Advances all time-based events in this scheduler by `dt` seconds (scaled by the schedul...
  LScheduler:updateFrames( )  -> integer  -- Advances all frame-based events by one frame tick.
```

## lurek.math {#math}

> Core math: vectors, random, interpolation, geometry utilities.

```lua
  lurek.math.Vec2( x, y )  -> LVec2  -- Compatibility alias for `vec2`.
  lurek.math.Vec3( x, y, z )  -> LVec3  -- Compatibility alias for `vec3`.
  lurek.math.aabbTree( )  -> LAabbTree  -- Creates a new empty AABB tree for efficient broad-phase overlap queries.
  lurek.math.abs( x )  -> number  -- Returns the absolute value of x.
  lurek.math.acos( x )  -> number  -- Returns the arccosine of x, in radians.
  lurek.math.angleBetween( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> number  -- Returns the angle in radians from (x1, y1) to (x2, y2).
  lurek.math.applyEasing( name, t )  -> number  -- Applies a named easing function to progress value t.
  lurek.math.asin( x )  -> number  -- Returns the arcsine of x, in radians.
  lurek.math.atan( y, [x] )  -> number  -- Returns the arctangent of x (or atan2(y, x) when two args given).
  lurek.math.atan2( y, x )  -> number  -- Returns atan(y/x) using the signs of both args to determine the quadrant.
  lurek.math.bresenham( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> table  -- Rasterizes a line from (x1,y1) to (x2,y2) using Bresenham's algorithm. Returns a table ...
  lurek.math.catmullRom( points )  -> LCatmullRom  -- Creates a Catmull-Rom spline through the given control points.
  lurek.math.ceil( x )  -> number  -- Returns the smallest integer ≥ x.
  lurek.math.circleContainsPoint( cx, cy, r, px, py )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the point (px, py) lies inside the circle.
  lurek.math.circleIntersectsCircle( x1, y1, r1, x2, y2, r2 )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if two circles overlap.
  lurek.math.circleIntersectsLine( cx, cy, r, lx1, ly1, lx2, ly2 )  -> boolean  -- Tests an infinite line against a circle. Returns hit, then two optional hit-point pairs.
  lurek.math.circleIntersectsSegment( cx, cy, r, sx1, sy1, sx2, sy2 )  -> boolean  -- Tests a line segment against a circle. Returns hit, then two optional hit-point pairs.
  lurek.math.clamp( v, min, max )  -> number  -- Clamps `v` between `min` and `max`.
  lurek.math.closestPointOnSegment( px, py, x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> number  -- Returns the closest point on segment (x1,y1)-(x2,y2) to point (px,py).
  lurek.math.convexHull( pts )  -> table  -- Computes the convex hull of a flat {x1,y1,...} point list. Returns a flat table.
  lurek.math.cos( x )  -> number  -- Returns the cosine of x (radians).
  lurek.math.deg( rad )  -> number  -- Converts radians to degrees.
  lurek.math.delaunayTriangulate( pts )  -> table  -- Delaunay triangulation of a flat {x1,y1,...} point list. Returns a table of flat 6-numb...
  lurek.math.distance( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> number  -- Returns the Euclidean distance between (x1,y1) and (x2,y2).
  lurek.math.distanceSq( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> number  -- Returns the squared Euclidean distance between (x1,y1) and (x2,y2) (avoids sqrt).
  lurek.math.exp( x )  -> number  -- Returns e raised to the power x.
  lurek.math.fbm( )  -> number  -- Returns fractal Brownian motion noise at (x, y).
  lurek.math.floor( x )  -> number  -- Returns the largest integer ≤ x.
  lurek.math.fmod( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the remainder of x / y (fmod).
  lurek.math.fromHex( hex )  -> number  -- Parses a hex color string (#RRGGBB or #RRGGBBAA) into (r, g, b, a) floats.
  lurek.math.gammaToLinear( c )  -> number  -- Converts a gamma-encoded sRGB value to linear space.
  lurek.math.hermite( p0x, p0y, p1x, p1y, m0x, m0y, m1x, m1y )  -> LHermite  -- Creates a Hermite spline defined by two endpoints and tangents.
  lurek.math.hslToRgb( h, s, l )  -> number  -- Converts HSL (h: 0-360, s: 0-1, l: 0-1) to RGBA (r, g, b, a) floats.
  lurek.math.inBack( t )  -> number  -- Back ease-in — overshoots slightly before settling at the target.
  lurek.math.inBounce( t )  -> number  -- Bounce ease-in — reverse bounce effect that accelerates into the motion.
  lurek.math.inCubic( t )  -> number  -- Cubic ease-in — acceleration starts slowly then increases sharply.
  lurek.math.inElastic( t )  -> number  -- Elastic ease-in — spring-like overshoot at the beginning of the motion.
  lurek.math.inExpo( t )  -> number  -- Exponential ease-in — very slow start that accelerates sharply near the end.
  lurek.math.inOutBack( t )  -> number  -- Back ease-in-out — overshoot on both ends.
  lurek.math.inOutBounce( t )  -> number  -- Bounce ease-in-out — bouncing motion on both ends.
  lurek.math.inOutCubic( t )  -> number  -- Cubic ease-in-out — slow start and end with fast cubic middle.
  lurek.math.inOutElastic( t )  -> number  -- Elastic ease-in-out — spring-like oscillation on both ends.
  lurek.math.inOutExpo( t )  -> number  -- Exponential ease-in-out — very slow start and end with an exponential surge.
  lurek.math.inOutQuad( t )  -> number  -- Quadratic ease-in-out — slow start, fast middle, slow end.
  lurek.math.inOutQuart( t )  -> number  -- Quartic ease-in-out — very slow start and end with a sharp middle peak.
  lurek.math.inOutSine( t )  -> number  -- Sinusoidal ease-in-out — smooth S-curve based on cosine interpolation.
  lurek.math.inQuad( t )  -> number  -- Quadratic ease-in — acceleration that starts at zero and increases.
  lurek.math.inQuart( t )  -> number  -- Quartic ease-in — strongly delayed acceleration using a power-of-4 curve.
  lurek.math.inSine( t )  -> number  -- Sinusoidal ease-in — gentle acceleration based on a sine curve.
  lurek.math.inverseLerp( a, b, v )  -> number  -- Returns the interpolation parameter t for `v` in [a, b].
  lurek.math.isConvex( pts )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the polygon (flat table {x1,y1,...}) is convex.
  lurek.math.lerp( a, b, t )  -> number  -- Linear interpolation between two numbers: a + (b - a) * t.
  lurek.math.lineIntersect( x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3, x4, y4 )  -> number  -- Infinite line intersection. Returns (x, y) or (nil, nil) if lines are parallel.
  lurek.math.linear( t )  -> number  -- Linear easing (identity).
  lurek.math.linearToGamma( c )  -> number  -- Converts a linear-space value to gamma-encoded sRGB.
  lurek.math.log( x, [b] )  -> number  -- Returns the natural log of x, or log base b if b is supplied.
  lurek.math.max( )  -> number  -- Returns the largest of the supplied numbers.
  lurek.math.min( )  -> number  -- Returns the smallest of the supplied numbers.
  lurek.math.newBezierCurve( points )  -> LBezierCurve  -- Creates a new BezierCurve from a flat table of coordinates {x1,y1, x2,y2, ...}.
  lurek.math.newCircle( x, y, radius )  -> LCircle  -- Creates a new Circle value type with the given centre and radius.
  lurek.math.newNoiseGenerator( [seed] )  -> LNoiseGenerator  -- Creates a new seeded noise generator.
  lurek.math.newRandomGenerator( [seed] )  -> LRandomGenerator  -- Creates a new random number generator with an optional seed.
  lurek.math.newSpatialHash( cell_size )  -> LSpatialHash  -- Creates a new SpatialHash with the given cell size.
  lurek.math.newTransform( )  -> LTransform  -- Creates a new Transform, optionally initialised from full parameters.
  lurek.math.newTween( duration, [easing_name] )  -> LTween  -- Creates a new Tween with the given duration and easing name.
  lurek.math.outBack( t )  -> number  -- Back ease-out — overshoots the target then snaps back into place.
  lurek.math.outBounce( t )  -> number  -- Bounce ease-out — simulates a ball bouncing against the target value.
  lurek.math.outCubic( t )  -> number  -- Cubic ease-out — rapid deceleration using a cubic power curve.
  lurek.math.outElastic( t )  -> number  -- Elastic ease-out — spring-like oscillation that settles at the target.
  lurek.math.outExpo( t )  -> number  -- Exponential ease-out — sharp initial speed that decelerates exponentially.
  lurek.math.outQuad( t )  -> number  -- Quadratic ease-out — deceleration that starts fast and ends at zero.
  lurek.math.outQuart( t )  -> number  -- Quartic ease-out — rapid deceleration using a power-of-4 curve.
  lurek.math.outSine( t )  -> number  -- Sinusoidal ease-out — gentle deceleration based on a cosine curve.
  lurek.math.perlin2d( x, y, [seed] )  -> number  -- Returns 2D Perlin noise at (x, y) with the given seed.
  lurek.math.perlin3d( x, y, z, [seed] )  -> number  -- Returns 3D Perlin noise at (x, y, z) with the given seed.
  lurek.math.pointInPolygon( pts, px, py )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if (px, py) is inside the polygon given as a flat {x1,y1,...} table.
  lurek.math.polygonArea( pts )  -> number  -- Returns the signed area of a polygon given as a flat {x1,y1,...} table.
  lurek.math.polygonCentroid( pts )  -> number  -- Returns the centroid (cx, cy) of a polygon given as a flat {x1,y1,...} table.
  lurek.math.polygonClip( pts, nx, ny, d )  -> table  -- Clips a polygon against a single half-plane using the Sutherland-Hodgman algorithm.
  lurek.math.polygonDifference( a, b )  -> table  -- Computes the approximate difference `A - B` for convex polygon inputs.
  lurek.math.polygonIntersection( a, b )  -> table  -- Computes the intersection of two convex polygons.
  lurek.math.polygonUnion( a, b )  -> table  -- Computes the approximate union of two convex polygons as a convex hull.
  lurek.math.pow( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns x raised to the power y.
  lurek.math.rad( deg )  -> number  -- Converts degrees to radians.
  lurek.math.random( [a], [b] )  -> number  -- Returns a pseudo-random number using Lua's built-in `math.random` behavior.
  lurek.math.randomInt( lo, hi )  -> integer  -- Returns a pseudo-random integer in [lo, hi] (inclusive).
  lurek.math.rectFromCenter( cx, cy, w, h )  -> number  -- Creates a rectangle centered at (cx, cy) with the given width and height.
  lurek.math.rectUnion( x1, y1, w1, h1, x2, y2, w2, h2 )  -> number  -- Returns the union (bounding box) of two rectangles.
  lurek.math.remap( v, in_min, in_max, out_min, out_max )  -> number  -- Remaps `v` from [in_min, in_max] to [out_min, out_max].
  lurek.math.rgbToHsl( r, g, b )  -> number  -- Converts RGBA floats to HSL (h: 0-360, s: 0-1, l: 0-1).
  lurek.math.round( x )  -> number  -- Returns x rounded to the nearest integer (half-up).
  lurek.math.segmentIntersectsSegment( x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3, x4, y4 )  -> boolean  -- Tests if two line segments intersect. Returns (hit, ix?, iy?).
  lurek.math.sign( v )  -> number  -- Returns -1, 0, or 1 depending on the sign of `v`.
  lurek.math.simplex2d( x, y, [seed] )  -> number  -- Returns 2D Simplex noise at (x, y) with the given seed.
  lurek.math.simplexNoise( x, y, [z] )  -> number  -- Returns a simplex noise value in [-1, 1] for 2D or 3D coordinates.
  lurek.math.sin( x )  -> number  -- Returns the sine of x (radians).
  lurek.math.smoothstep( edge0, edge1, x )  -> number  -- Hermite smoothstep between `edge0` and `edge1`.
  lurek.math.sqrt( x )  -> number  -- Returns the square root of x.
  lurek.math.tan( x )  -> number  -- Returns the tangent of x (radians).
  lurek.math.triangulate( pts )  -> table  -- Triangulates a simple polygon given as a flat table {x1,y1, x2,y2, ...}.
  lurek.math.vec2( x, y )  -> LVec2  -- Creates a 2D vector with x and y components.
```

**`LAabbTree`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`AabbTree`].

```lua
  LAabbTree:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all entries from the tree.
  LAabbTree:contains( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if an entry with the given id exists in the tree.
  LAabbTree:insert( id, min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -> nil  -- Inserts an entry with the given AABB into the tree.
  LAabbTree:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the tree contains no entries.
  LAabbTree:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of entries in the tree.
  LAabbTree:query( min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -> table  -- Returns the ids of all entries whose AABBs overlap the query rectangle.
  LAabbTree:queryPoint( x, y )  -> table  -- Returns the ids of all entries whose AABBs contain the given point.
  LAabbTree:remove( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes the entry with the given id.
  LAabbTree:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LAabbTree:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LAabbTree:update( id, min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -> boolean  -- Updates the AABB for an existing entry.
```

```lua
  LBezierCurve:removeControlPoint( index )  -> boolean  -- Removes a control point at 1-based index.

  LBezierCurve:scale( s, ox, oy )  -> nil  -- Scales all control points around a pivot by factor s.
  LBezierCurve:setControlPoint( index, x, y )  -> boolean  -- Sets the control point at 1-based index.
```

**`LTween`** methods:

```lua
  LTween:addValue( start, target )  -> integer  -- Adds a start/target value pair. Returns the 1-based index.
  LTween:getAllValues( )  -> table  -- Returns all interpolated values as a table.

  LTween:getDuration( )  -> number  -- Returns the tween duration in seconds.
  LTween:getEasingName( )  -> string  -- Returns the easing function name.
  LTween:getTime( )  -> number  -- Returns the current clock time.
  LTween:getValue( [index] )  -> number  -- Returns the interpolated value at 1-based index, or all values when no index is given.
  LTween:getValueCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of values in this tween.
  LTween:isComplete( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the tween has finished.
  LTween:reset( )  -> nil  -- Resets the tween elapsed time to zero, restarting the animation.
  LTween:set( t )  -> nil  -- Alias for setTime(). Sets the clock to t, clamped to [0, duration].
  LTween:setTime( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the clock to a specific time, clamped to [0, duration].
  LTween:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTween:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LTween:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the clock by dt seconds. Returns true when complete.
```

**`LVec2`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Vec2`] value type.

```lua
  LVec2:angle( )  -> number  -- Returns the angle of this vector in radians (atan2(y, x)).
  LVec2:cross( other )  -> number  -- Returns the 2D cross product (scalar) with another vector.
  LVec2:distance( other )  -> number  -- Returns the Euclidean distance from this vector to another.
  LVec2:dot( other )  -> number  -- Returns the dot product with another vector.
  LVec2:fromAngle( radians )  -> LVec2  -- Creates a unit vector from an angle in radians.
  LVec2:length( )  -> number  -- Returns the Euclidean length of the vector.
  LVec2:lengthSquared( )  -> number  -- Returns the squared length of the vector (faster than length).
  LVec2:lerp( other, t )  -> LVec2  -- Returns a linearly interpolated vector between this and other at parameter t.
  LVec2:normalize( )  -> LVec2  -- Returns a unit-length copy of this vector. Returns zero if length is zero.
  LVec2:normalized( )  -> LVec2  -- Compatibility alias for `normalize`.
  LVec2:perpendicular( )  -> LVec2  -- Returns the perpendicular vector (-y, x).
  LVec2:reflect( normal )  -> LVec2  -- Reflects this vector off a surface with the given normal.
  LVec2:rotate( angle )  -> LVec2  -- Returns a new vector rotated by the given angle in radians.
  LVec2:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LVec2:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LVec2:x( )  -> number  -- Returns the horizontal component of the vector.
  LVec2:y( )  -> number  -- Returns the vertical component of the vector.
```

**`LVec3`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Vec3`] value type.

```lua
  LVec3:add( other )  -> LVec3  -- Add another Vec3 and return the result.
  LVec3:cross( other )  -> LVec3  -- Cross product with another Vec3.
  LVec3:distance( other )  -> number  -- Euclidean distance to another Vec3.
  LVec3:dot( other )  -> number  -- Dot product with another Vec3.
  LVec3:length( )  -> number  -- Returns the Euclidean length of the vector.
  LVec3:lengthSquared( )  -> number  -- Returns the squared Euclidean length (avoids sqrt).
  LVec3:lerp( other, t )  -> LVec3  -- Linear interpolation towards another Vec3.
  LVec3:normalize( )  -> LVec3  -- Returns a unit-length version of this vector.
  LVec3:scale( s )  -> LVec3  -- Scale this vector by a scalar and return the result.
  LVec3:splat( v )  -> LVec3  -- Creates a Vec3 with all components set to `v`.
  LVec3:sub( other )  -> LVec3  -- Subtract another Vec3 and return the result.
  LVec3:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LVec3:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.physics {#physics}

> 2D physics simulation via rapier2d: bodies, colliders, joints, sensors, raycasts.

```lua
  lurek.physics.attachShape( body_ud, shape_ud )  -> nil  -- Attaches a standalone shape to a body as an additional fixture.
  lurek.physics.debugDraw( enable )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the physics debug overlay (AABB boxes and velocity vectors).
  lurek.physics.destroyWorld( world_ud )  -> nil  -- Marks a physics world for destruction.
  lurek.physics.drawDebugGpu( world_ud, config_val )  -> nil  -- Queues a GPU physics debug draw command for the current frame.
  lurek.physics.getBody( world_ud, body_ud )  -> number  -- Returns the position and velocity of a body (x, y, vx, vy).
  lurek.physics.getCollisions( world_ud )  -> table  -- Returns all collision events from the last simulation step.
  lurek.physics.isSleepingAllowed( world_ud, body_ud )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the body is allowed to sleep.
  lurek.physics.newBody( world_ud, x, y, bt )  -> LBody  -- Creates a new rectangular body in the given world.
  lurek.physics.newCellular( width, height )  -> LCellular  -- Creates a falling-sand cellular automaton grid.
  lurek.physics.newChainShape( closed, coords )  -> LPhysicsShape  -- Creates a chain shape userdata from flat variadic vertex pairs.
  lurek.physics.newCircleShape( r )  -> LPhysicsShape  -- Creates a circle shape userdata.
  lurek.physics.newEdgeShape( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> LPhysicsShape  -- Creates an edge (line segment) shape userdata.
  lurek.physics.newPolygonShape( )  -> LPhysicsShape  -- Creates a convex polygon shape userdata from flat variadic vertex pairs.
  lurek.physics.newRectangleShape( w, h )  -> LPhysicsShape  -- Creates a rectangle shape userdata.
  lurek.physics.newTerrain( width, height, cell_size, world_ud )  -> LTerrain  -- Creates a destructible terrain grid.
  lurek.physics.newWorld( gx, gy )  -> LWorld  -- Creates a new physics world with the given gravity vector.
  lurek.physics.setBodyVelocity( world_ud, body_ud, vx, vy )  -> nil  -- Sets the velocity of a body.
  lurek.physics.setSleepingAllowed( world_ud, body_ud, allowed )  -> nil  -- Sets whether the body is allowed to sleep.
  lurek.physics.step( world_ud, dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the physics world by dt seconds.
  lurek.physics.testAABB( ax, ay, aw, ah, bx, by, bw, bh )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when two axis-aligned bounding boxes overlap.
  lurek.physics.testCircleAABB( cx, cy, cr, ax, ay, aw, ah )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when a circle overlaps an AABB.
  lurek.physics.testCircles( ax, ay, ar, bx, by, br )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when two circles overlap.
  lurek.physics.testPoint( px, py, ax, ay, aw, ah )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when point (px, py) lies inside the AABB.
```

**`LBody`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a physics body accessed through its world.

```lua
  LBody:applyAngularImpulse( impulse )  -> nil  -- Applies an angular impulse.
  LBody:applyForce( fx, fy )  -> nil  -- Applies a continuous force to the body.
  LBody:applyForceAtPoint( fx, fy, px, py )  -> nil  -- Applies a force at a specific world-space point.
  LBody:applyImpulse( ix, iy )  -> nil  -- Applies a linear impulse to the body.
  LBody:applyTorque( torque )  -> nil  -- Applies a torque (rotational force).
  LBody:destroy( )  -> nil  -- Removes this body from the world.
  LBody:getAngle( )  -> number  -- Returns the body angle in radians.
  LBody:getAngularDamping( )  -> number  -- Returns the angular damping coefficient.
  LBody:getAngularVelocity( )  -> number  -- Returns the angular velocity in radians/s.
  LBody:getFriction( )  -> number  -- Returns the body friction coefficient.
  LBody:getGravityScale( )  -> number  -- Returns the per-body gravity multiplier.
  LBody:getHeight( )  -> number  -- Returns the height of this body's primary collider shape in world units.
  LBody:getId( )  -> integer  -- Returns the body's integer ID.
  LBody:getLayer( )  -> integer  -- Returns the collision layer bitmask.
  LBody:getLinearDamping( )  -> number  -- Returns the linear damping coefficient.
  LBody:getMask( )  -> integer  -- Returns the collision mask bitmask.
  LBody:getMass( )  -> number  -- Returns the body mass in kilograms used for force and impulse calculations.
  LBody:getPosition( )  -> number  -- Returns the body position (x, y).
  LBody:getRestitution( )  -> number  -- Returns the body restitution (bounciness).
  LBody:getType( )  -> string  -- Returns the body type as a string.
  LBody:getVelocity( )  -> number  -- Returns the body velocity (vx, vy).
  LBody:getWidth( )  -> number  -- Returns the width of this body's primary collider shape in world units.
  LBody:getX( )  -> number  -- Returns the body X position.
  LBody:getY( )  -> number  -- Returns the body Y position.
  LBody:isBullet( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether CCD is enabled.
  LBody:isFixedRotation( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether rotation is locked.
  LBody:isSleeping( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this body is currently sleeping (inactive).
  LBody:isSleepingAllowed( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the body can sleep.
  LBody:setAngle( angle )  -> nil  -- Sets the body angle in radians.
  LBody:setAngularDamping( damping )  -> nil  -- Sets the angular damping coefficient.
  LBody:setAngularVelocity( omega )  -> nil  -- Sets the angular velocity.
  LBody:setBullet( bullet )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables continuous collision detection (CCD) for fast-moving bodies.
  LBody:setFixedRotation( fixed )  -> nil  -- Locks or unlocks rotation.
  LBody:setFriction( friction )  -> nil  -- Sets the body friction coefficient.
  LBody:setGravityScale( scale )  -> nil  -- Sets the per-body gravity multiplier.
  LBody:setLayer( layer )  -> nil  -- Sets the collision layer bitmask.
  LBody:setLinearDamping( damping )  -> nil  -- Sets the linear damping coefficient.
  LBody:setMask( mask )  -> nil  -- Sets the collision mask bitmask.
  LBody:setMass( mass )  -> nil  -- Sets the body mass; affects how forces and impulses change velocity.
  LBody:setPosition( x, y )  -> nil  -- Teleports the body to the given world-space position, bypassing collision.
  LBody:setRestitution( restitution )  -> nil  -- Sets the body restitution (bounciness).
  LBody:setSleepingAllowed( allowed )  -> nil  -- Sets whether the body can sleep.
  LBody:setType( bt )  -> nil  -- Changes the body type: `"dynamic"`, `"static"`, or `"kinematic"`.
  LBody:setVelocity( vx, vy )  -> nil  -- Sets the body's linear velocity in world units per second.
  LBody:sleep( )  -> nil  -- Puts this body to sleep immediately.
  LBody:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LBody:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LBody:wakeUp( )  -> nil  -- Forcibly wakes up this body.
```

**`LCellular`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a falling-sand [`CellularWorld`].

```lua
  LCellular:countCells( t )  -> integer  -- Counts cells of the given material type.
  LCellular:fillCircle( cx, cy, r, t )  -> nil  -- Fills a circle of cells with the given material.
  LCellular:fillRect( cx0, cy0, cw, ch, t )  -> nil  -- Fills a rectangular region of cells with the given material.
  LCellular:findCells( t )  -> table  -- Returns positions of all cells of the given material as an array of `{x, y}` tables.
  LCellular:getCell( cx, cy )  -> integer  -- Returns the material at `(cx, cy)` as an integer constant.
  LCellular:loadFromBytes( data )  -> boolean  -- Loads grid data from bytes produced by `toBytes`.
  LCellular:setCell( cx, cy, t )  -> nil  -- Sets the material of a cell.
  LCellular:step( )  -> nil  -- Advances the simulation by one tick.
  LCellular:stepN( n )  -> nil  -- Advances the simulation by `n` ticks.
  LCellular:toBytes( )  -> string  -- Serialises the grid to a byte string.
  LCellular:toImageData( )  -> string  -- Returns the full grid as an RGBA byte string using the default colour palette.
  LCellular:toImageDataRegion( cx0, cy0, cw, ch )  -> string  -- Returns a sub-region as an RGBA byte string.
  LCellular:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LCellular:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LPhysicsShape`** methods:

> Lua-side standalone shape object (circle, rectangle, edge, polygon, chain).

```lua
  LPhysicsShape:destroy( )  -> nil  -- Releases this shape handle (GC handles cleanup).
  LPhysicsShape:getBoundingBox( )  -> number  -- Returns the axis-aligned bounding box (x1, y1, x2, y2).
  LPhysicsShape:getRadius( )  -> number  -- Returns the radius. Only valid for circle shapes.
  LPhysicsShape:getType( )  -> string  -- Returns the shape type string: "circle", "rectangle", "polygon", "edge", or "chain".
  LPhysicsShape:setDensity( density )  -> nil  -- Sets the density for this shape (used when attaching to a body).
  LPhysicsShape:setFriction( friction )  -> nil  -- Sets the friction coefficient.
  LPhysicsShape:setRestitution( restitution )  -> nil  -- Sets the restitution (bounciness) coefficient.
  LPhysicsShape:setSensor( sensor )  -> nil  -- Sets whether this shape is a sensor (non-colliding trigger).
  LPhysicsShape:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LPhysicsShape:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LTerrain`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a destructible [`TerrainMap`].

```lua
  LTerrain:collapseColumns( )  -> integer  -- Removes unsupported cells, returning the number of cells that fell.
  LTerrain:fillAll( solid )  -> nil  -- Sets every cell in the grid to `solid`.
  LTerrain:fillCircle( wx, wy, radius, solid )  -> nil  -- Fills a circle of cells centred at world position `(wx, wy)`.
  LTerrain:fillRect( wx, wy, w, h, solid )  -> nil  -- Fills a rectangular region of cells.
  LTerrain:flush( )  -> nil  -- Rebuilds physics bodies for all dirty chunks.
  LTerrain:getCell( cx, cy )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a cell is solid.
  LTerrain:isDirty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns `true` when at least one chunk needs flushing.
  LTerrain:loadFromBytes( data )  -> boolean  -- Loads terrain cell data from bytes produced by `toBytes`.
  LTerrain:setCell( cx, cy, solid )  -> nil  -- Sets a single terrain cell to solid or empty.
  LTerrain:solidPositions( )  -> table  -- Returns the world-space centres of all solid cells as an array of `{x, y}` tables.
  LTerrain:spawnDebris( positions, mass, restitution )  -> table  -- Spawns dynamic debris bodies at the given positions.
  LTerrain:toBytes( )  -> string  -- Serialises the terrain grid to a byte string for save/load.
  LTerrain:toImageData( sr, sg, sb, er, eg, eb )  -> string  -- Returns the terrain as an RGBA byte string.
  LTerrain:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTerrain:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LWorld`** methods:

> Lua-side handle wrapping a physics World.

```lua
  LWorld:addDistanceJoint( a, b, ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, len )  -> integer  -- Creates a distance joint between two bodies.
  LWorld:addFixture( )  -> integer  -- Adds an extra fixture (collider) to a body.
  LWorld:addFrictionJoint( a, b, ax, ay, max_f, max_t )  -> integer  -- Creates a friction joint that resists relative motion.
  LWorld:addGearJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -> integer  -- Creates a gear joint (stub - falls back to weld joint).
  LWorld:addMotorJoint( a, b, factor )  -> integer  -- Creates a motor joint that drives body_b toward body_a.
  LWorld:addMouseJoint( body_id, tx, ty, max_f )  -> integer  -- Creates a mouse joint connecting a body to a target point.
  LWorld:addPrismaticJoint( a, b, ax, ay, axis_x, axis_y )  -> integer  -- Creates a prismatic (slider) joint between two bodies.
  LWorld:addPulleyJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -> integer  -- Creates a pulley joint (stub - falls back to weld joint).
  LWorld:addRevoluteJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -> integer  -- Creates a revolute (pin) joint between two bodies.
  LWorld:addRopeJoint( a, b, ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, max )  -> integer  -- Creates a rope joint with a maximum distance.
  LWorld:addWeldJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -> integer  -- Creates a weld (rigid) joint between two bodies.
  LWorld:addWheelJoint( a, b, ax, ay, axis_x, axis_y )  -> integer  -- Creates a wheel joint (prismatic + rotation).
  LWorld:addZone( x, y, w, h )  -> LZone  -- Creates a rectangular gravity or damping zone.
  LWorld:clear( )  -> nil  -- Resets the world, removing all bodies and joints.
  LWorld:clearBeginContact( )  -> nil  -- Removes the begin-contact callback.
  LWorld:clearBodyData( id )  -> nil  -- Removes the Lua data attached to a body.
  LWorld:clearBodyOneWay( id )  -> nil  -- Removes the one-way platform flag from a body.
  LWorld:clearEndContact( )  -> nil  -- Removes the end-contact callback.
  LWorld:destroyBody( id )  -> nil  -- Removes a body from the world.
  LWorld:destroyJoint( jid )  -> nil  -- Removes a joint from the world.
  LWorld:drawDebug( )  -> nil  -- Draws physics objects into an image for debugging.
  LWorld:fixtureCount( body_id )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of fixtures on a body.
  LWorld:getBeginContactEvents( )  -> table  -- Returns begin-contact events from the last step.
  LWorld:getBodyAtPoint( x, y )  -> integer  -- Returns the body ID at a world-space point, or nil.
  LWorld:getBodyCCD( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether CCD is enabled for a body.
  LWorld:getBodyContacts( body_id )  -> table  -- Returns contacts involving a specific body.
  LWorld:getBodyCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of bodies in the world.
  LWorld:getBodyData( id )  -> any  -- Returns the Lua data previously attached to a body, or nil if none is set.
  LWorld:getBodyIds( )  -> table  -- Returns all body IDs in the world.
  LWorld:getBodyOneWay( id )  -> number  -- Returns the one-way normal for a body, or nil if not configured.
  LWorld:getBodyType( id )  -> string  -- Returns the body type as a string.
  LWorld:getCollisionEvents( )  -> table  -- Returns collision events from the last step.
  LWorld:getContacts( )  -> table  -- Returns all contact pairs from the narrow phase.
  LWorld:getEndContactEvents( )  -> table  -- Returns end-contact events from the last step.
  LWorld:getGravity( )  -> number  -- Returns the gravity vector (gx, gy).
  LWorld:getJointBodies( jid )  -> integer  -- Returns the two body IDs connected by a joint.
  LWorld:getJointBreakForce( jid )  -> number  -- Returns the break threshold for a joint, or nil if not set.
  LWorld:getJointIds( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of integer IDs for every joint attached to this world.
  LWorld:getJointLimits( jid )  -> number  -- Returns the angular limits on a joint.
  LWorld:getJointMotorSpeed( jid )  -> number  -- Returns the motor speed on a joint's angular axis.
  LWorld:getJointType( jid )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of a joint.
  LWorld:getMeter( )  -> number  -- Returns the pixels-per-meter scaling factor.
  LWorld:getSolverIterations( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current number of solver iterations per step.
  LWorld:getZoneEvents( )  -> table  -- Returns zone enter and leave events from the most recent step.
  LWorld:isBodySleeping( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a body is currently sleeping (inactive).
  LWorld:jointCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of joints.
  LWorld:newBodies( specs )  -> table  -- Creates multiple bodies in one call.
  LWorld:newBody( x, y, bt )  -> LBody  -- Creates a new rectangular body and adds it to the world.
  LWorld:newChainBody( x, y, tbl, closed, bt )  -> LBody  -- Creates a new chain body from a flat vertex table and adds it to the world.
  LWorld:newCircleBody( x, y, radius, bt )  -> LBody  -- Creates a new circular body and adds it to the world.
  LWorld:newEdgeBody( x, y, x1, y1, x2, y2, bt )  -> LBody  -- Creates a new edge (line segment) body and adds it to the world.
  LWorld:newPolygonBody( x, y, tbl, bt )  -> LBody  -- Creates a new polygon body from a flat vertex table and adds it to the world.
  LWorld:queryAABB( x, y, w, h )  -> table  -- Returns body IDs within an axis-aligned bounding box.
  LWorld:raycast( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> table  -- Casts a ray and returns the nearest hit, or nil.
  LWorld:raycastAll( x1, y1, dx, dy, max_dist )  -> table  -- Casts a ray and returns all hits.
  LWorld:raycastClosest( x1, y1, dx, dy, max_dist )  -> table  -- Casts a ray and returns the closest hit using the query pipeline.
  LWorld:setBeginContact( f )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback fired when two bodies begin touching.
  LWorld:setBodyCCD( id, enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables Continuous Collision Detection for a body.
  LWorld:setBodyData( id, value )  -> nil  -- Attaches arbitrary Lua data to a body for later retrieval.
  LWorld:setBodyOneWay( id, nx, ny )  -> nil  -- Marks a body as a one-way platform.
  LWorld:setBodyType( id, bt )  -> nil  -- Changes the simulation type of the body: `"dynamic"`, `"static"`, or `"kinematic"`.
  LWorld:setEndContact( f )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback fired when two bodies stop touching.
  LWorld:setFixtureFriction( body_id, fix_idx, friction )  -> nil  -- Sets friction on a fixture by index.
  LWorld:setFixtureRestitution( body_id, fix_idx, restitution )  -> nil  -- Sets restitution on a fixture by index.
  LWorld:setFixtureSensor( body_id, fix_idx, sensor )  -> nil  -- Sets whether a fixture is a sensor.
  LWorld:setGravity( gx, gy )  -> nil  -- Sets the world gravity vector; default is `(0, 9.81)` (downward).
  LWorld:setJointBreakForce( jid, f )  -> nil  -- Sets the relative-velocity threshold above which a joint breaks.
  LWorld:setJointLimits( jid, lower, upper )  -> nil  -- Sets the angular limits on a joint.
  LWorld:setJointLimitsEnabled( jid, enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables angular limits on a joint.
  LWorld:setJointMotorSpeed( jid, speed )  -> nil  -- Sets the motor speed on a joint's angular axis.
  LWorld:setMeter( ppm )  -> nil  -- Sets the pixels-per-meter scaling factor.
  LWorld:setMouseJointTarget( jid, x, y )  -> nil  -- Updates the target position of a mouse joint.
  LWorld:setSolverIterations( n )  -> nil  -- Sets the number of constraint solver iterations per step.
  LWorld:sleepBody( id )  -> nil  -- Puts a body to sleep immediately.
  LWorld:step( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the physics simulation by `dt` seconds.
  LWorld:stepFixed( accum, step_dt, max_steps )  -> number  -- Steps the world using a fixed sub-step size to consume accumulated time.
  LWorld:toPhysics( px )  -> number  -- Converts a pixel value to physics units.
  LWorld:toPixels( m )  -> number  -- Converts a physics-unit value to pixels.
  LWorld:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LWorld:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LWorld:wakeUpBody( id )  -> nil  -- Forcibly wakes up a sleeping body.
```

**`LZone`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a [`PhysicsZone`] living inside a [`World`].

```lua
  LZone:destroy( )  -> nil  -- Removes the zone from the world.
  LZone:getId( )  -> integer  -- Returns the zone's integer ID.
  LZone:setAngularDampingOverride( [value] )  -> nil  -- Sets an optional angular damping override for bodies inside the zone.
  LZone:setCircle( cx, cy, radius )  -> nil  -- Replaces the zone boundary with a circle.
  LZone:setEnabled( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the zone.
  LZone:setGravityDirectional( gx, gy )  -> nil  -- Sets directional gravity inside the zone.
  LZone:setGravityPoint( cx, cy, strength )  -> nil  -- Sets point-attractor gravity inside the zone.
  LZone:setGravityRepulsor( cx, cy, strength )  -> nil  -- Sets point-repulsor gravity inside the zone.
  LZone:setGravityZero( )  -> nil  -- Suppresses gravity inside the zone (zero-g pocket).
  LZone:setLayerMask( mask )  -> nil  -- Sets the layer bitmask; only bodies whose `layer & mask != 0` are affected.
  LZone:setLinearDampingOverride( [value] )  -> nil  -- Sets an optional linear damping override for bodies inside the zone.
  LZone:setPriority( priority )  -> nil  -- Sets the zone priority; higher values win over lower when zones overlap.
  LZone:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LZone:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.filesystem {#filesystem}

> Game filesystem: read/write files, directory listing, save paths, sandboxed I/O.

```lua
  lurek.filesystem.append( path, data )  -> nil  -- Opens the file in append mode and writes the given string at the end.
  lurek.filesystem.copy( src, dst )  -> nil  -- Copies a file within the sandbox from the game root into `save/`.
  lurek.filesystem.createDirectory( path )  -> nil  -- Creates a directory and any missing parent directories in the save area.
  lurek.filesystem.createTempFile( [prefix] )  -> string  -- Creates an empty temporary file in the `save/` sandbox and returns its relative path.
  lurek.filesystem.exists( path )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given file or directory exists.
  lurek.filesystem.getDirectoryItems( path )  -> table  -- Returns a table containing the names of every file and subdirectory in the given path.
  lurek.filesystem.getIdentity( )  -> string  -- Returns the identity string used to locate the game's save directory.
  lurek.filesystem.getInfo( path )  -> table  -- Returns a table of metadata for a path, or nil if the path does not exist.
  lurek.filesystem.getSaveDirectory( )  -> string  -- Returns the sandboxed save data directory path.
  lurek.filesystem.getSource( )  -> string  -- Returns the absolute path of the directory the game was loaded from.
  lurek.filesystem.getUserDirectory( )  -> string  -- Returns the current user's home directory path.
  lurek.filesystem.getWorkingDirectory( )  -> string  -- Returns the current working directory path.
  lurek.filesystem.glob( pattern )  -> table  -- Returns a sorted list of paths matching a simple wildcard pattern.
  lurek.filesystem.isDirectory( path )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given path is a directory.
  lurek.filesystem.isFile( path )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given path is a regular file.
  lurek.filesystem.lines( path )  -> function  -- Returns an iterator function over the lines of a text file.
  lurek.filesystem.listRecursive( path )  -> table  -- Returns a sorted list of all files under `path`, recursively.
  lurek.filesystem.load( path )  -> function  -- Loads and compiles a Lua file from the VFS, returning it as a callable function.
  lurek.filesystem.mkdir( path )  -> nil  -- Creates a directory and any missing parents relative to the game root.
  lurek.filesystem.mount( src, mp )  -> boolean  -- Mounts a directory at a virtual path inside the game filesystem.
  lurek.filesystem.mountZip( archive_path, prefix )  -> LZipMount  -- Mounts a ZIP archive at a virtual path prefix and returns a mount handle.
  lurek.filesystem.move( src, dst )  -> nil  -- Moves or renames a file within the `save/` directory.
  lurek.filesystem.newFileData( path )  -> LFileData  -- Loads a file from the VFS into a FileData buffer.
  lurek.filesystem.openFile( path, mode )  -> LFileHandle  -- Opens a file and returns a readable/writable file handle.
  lurek.filesystem.pollAsync( handle_id )  -> string  -- Polls an async load handle, returning status and optional data.
  lurek.filesystem.pollWatchers( )  -> table  -- Polls watched paths and returns the ones that changed since the last poll.
  lurek.filesystem.read( path )  -> string  -- Reads a text file and returns its contents as a string.
  lurek.filesystem.readAsync( path )  -> integer  -- Starts loading a file in the background and returns an opaque handle.
  lurek.filesystem.remove( path )  -> nil  -- Permanently deletes a file or empty directory from the save directory.
  lurek.filesystem.removeDir( path )  -> nil  -- Recursively deletes a directory and all its contents within `save/`.
  lurek.filesystem.setIdentity( name )  -> nil  -- Sets the identity string that names the game's sandboxed save-data directory.
  lurek.filesystem.stat( path )  -> table  -- Returns lightweight file statistics for the given path.
  lurek.filesystem.toAbsolutePath( path )  -> string  -- Resolves a relative game path to an absolute OS path string.
  lurek.filesystem.unmount( mp )  -> boolean  -- Removes a virtual mount layer by mountpoint.
  lurek.filesystem.unwatchPath( path )  -> nil  -- Removes `path` from the polled file-watch list.  No-op if not watched.
  lurek.filesystem.watchPath( path )  -> nil  -- Adds `path` to the polled file-watch list.
  lurek.filesystem.write( path, data )  -> nil  -- Writes a string to a file in the save directory.
```

**`LFileData`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`FileData`] buffer.

```lua
  LFileData:getFilename( )  -> string  -- Returns the virtual path this data was loaded from.
  LFileData:getSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the file size in bytes.
  LFileData:getString( )  -> string  -- Returns the file content as a Lua string.
  LFileData:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LFileData:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LFileHandle`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`FileHandle`] with interior mutability.

```lua
  LFileHandle:close( )  -> nil  -- Flushes any pending writes and closes the file handle.
  LFileHandle:flush( )  -> nil  -- Flushes all buffered writes to disk without closing the handle.
  LFileHandle:getMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the access mode the file was opened with.
  LFileHandle:getSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the size of the open file in bytes.
  LFileHandle:isEOF( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the read cursor has reached the end of the file.
  LFileHandle:read( [count] )  -> string  -- Reads bytes from the file, returning them as a string.
  LFileHandle:readLine( )  -> string  -- Reads the next line from the file without the trailing newline.
  LFileHandle:seek( pos )  -> integer  -- Seeks the file position to the given byte offset from the start.
  LFileHandle:tell( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current read/write byte offset from the start of the file.
  LFileHandle:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LFileHandle:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LFileHandle:write( data )  -> integer  -- Writes a string to the file and returns the number of bytes written.
```

**`LZipMount`** methods:

> Lua userdata wrapper around a [`ZipMount`].

```lua
  LZipMount:contains( virtual_path )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if `virtual_path` exists inside this ZIP mount.
  LZipMount:listFiles( )  -> table  -- Returns a sorted array of all virtual paths exposed by this ZIP mount.
  LZipMount:prefix( )  -> string  -- Returns the virtual path prefix this archive was mounted under.
  LZipMount:readFile( virtual_path )  -> string  -- Reads a file from the ZIP and returns it as a string of bytes.
  LZipMount:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LZipMount:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.event {#event}

> Event queue: push/poll custom events between systems.

```lua
  lurek.event.clear( )  -> nil  -- Discards every pending event in the engine event queue without processing them.
  lurek.event.clearHistory( )  -> nil  -- Clears all recorded event history entries from the ring buffer.
  lurek.event.enableHistory( capacity )  -> nil  -- Enables event history recording, keeping a ring buffer of the last `capacity` events pu...
  lurek.event.exit( [code] )  -> nil  -- Pushes an exit event onto the engine event queue, requesting a graceful shutdown at the...
  lurek.event.flushDeferred( )  -> integer  -- Moves all events from the deferred buffer into the main engine event queue and clears t...
  lurek.event.getHistory( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of recently pushed events as tables.
  lurek.event.newSignal( )  -> LSignal  -- Creates and returns a new independent Signal pub-sub dispatcher.
  lurek.event.poll( )  -> function  -- Returns an iterator function that pops events one at a time from the engine event queue.
  lurek.event.pump( )  -> nil  -- Synchronises OS-level windowing events into the engine event queue.
  lurek.event.push( ... )  -> nil  -- Pushes a custom named event onto the main engine event queue with optional payload argu...
  lurek.event.pushDeferred( ... )  -> nil  -- Pushes a named event into the deferred buffer instead of the main queue.
  lurek.event.quit( )  -> nil  -- Alias for `exit()` - requests the engine to stop gracefully at the end of the current f...
  lurek.event.restart( )  -> nil  -- Requests that the engine perform a full restart at the beginning of the next frame.
  lurek.event.wait( [timeout] )  -> boolean  -- Blocks the current thread until the next engine event arrives or the optional timeout e...
```

**`LSignal`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Signal`] with registry-stored callbacks.

```lua
  LSignal:clear( name )  -> integer  -- Removes every callback registered for the specified event name and releases their Lua r...
  LSignal:clearAll( )  -> integer  -- Removes every callback across all event names in this Signal instance, effectively rese...
  LSignal:connect( name, func )  -> integer  -- Subscribes to an event name or wildcard glob pattern and returns a handle.
  LSignal:emit( ... )  -> nil  -- Fires all callbacks registered for the named event, passing any extra arguments to each...
  LSignal:getCount( name )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of callbacks currently registered for the specified event name.
  LSignal:getTotalCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of callbacks registered across all event names in this Signal ...
  LSignal:once( name, callback )  -> integer  -- Registers a one-shot callback that fires at most once for the named event and then auto...
  LSignal:register( name, callback )  -> integer  -- Registers a Lua callback function for the named event and returns a numeric handle ID.
  LSignal:registerWithFilter( name, callback, filter )  -> integer  -- Registers a callback with an associated filter predicate function.
  LSignal:remove( handle )  -> boolean  -- Removes a previously registered subscription identified by its numeric handle.
  LSignal:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the string type name of this userdata object.
  LSignal:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the given type name matches this object's type or any parent type.
```

```lua
  lurek.system.getMemorySize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total amount of installed system RAM in megabytes.

  lurek.system.getOS( )  -> string  -- Returns the host operating system name ('Windows', 'Linux', 'macOS').
```
