```lua
  lurek.system.setDebugOverlay( enabled )  -> nil  -- Shows or hides the FPS/draw-call debug overlay.
  lurek.system.setLogLevel( level )  -> nil  -- Sets the minimum severity level for runtime log messages.
```

## lurek.thread {#thread}

> Background threads and inter-thread channels for Lua coroutines.

```lua
  lurek.thread.async( code, ... )  -> LPromise  -- Starts a one-shot background computation and returns a promise.
  lurek.thread.getChannel( name )  -> LChannel  -- Gets or creates a named global channel shared across threads.
  lurek.thread.newChannel( )  -> LChannel  -- Creates a new unnamed channel for inter-thread communication.
  lurek.thread.newPool( size, code )  -> LThreadPool  -- Creates a thread pool whose workers all run the same Lua code.
  lurek.thread.newThread( code )  -> LThread  -- Creates a new background thread from a Lua code string.
```

**`LChannel`** methods:

> A synchronized message queue for cross-VM communication.

```lua
  LChannel:clear( )  -> nil  -- Clears all items from the channel.
  LChannel:demand( [timeout] )  -> table  -- Waits for a value or until the timeout expires, then removes and returns it.
  LChannel:getCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items in the channel.
  LChannel:peek( )  -> table  -- Retrieves the next value from the channel without removing it.
  LChannel:pop( )  -> table  -- Retrieves and removes a value from the channel.
  LChannel:popBytes( )  -> string  -- Pops a bytes value from the channel and returns it as a Lua string.
  LChannel:popTable( )  -> table  -- Pops a value from the channel expecting a table.
  LChannel:push( value )  -> integer  -- Pushes a value to the channel.
  LChannel:pushBytes( data )  -> integer  -- Pushes raw binary data (a Lua string treated as a byte array) to the channel.
  LChannel:pushTable( value )  -> integer  -- Serializes a Lua table and pushes it to the channel.
  LChannel:supply( value )  -> nil  -- Blocks until the channel has space, then adds the value.
  LChannel:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LChannel:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
```

**`LPromise`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a one-shot [`Promise`].

```lua
  LPromise:getError( )  -> string  -- Returns the worker error string if the promise failed.
  LPromise:isDone( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the promise has completed.
  LPromise:result( )  -> table  -- Pops and returns the promise result.
  LPromise:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LPromise:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
```

**`LThread`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a background [`LuaThread`].

```lua
  LThread:getError( )  -> string  -- Returns the error message if the thread failed.
  LThread:isRunning( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the thread is currently executing.
  LThread:start( ... )  -> nil  -- Launches the background thread, passing optional varargs.
  LThread:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LThread:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
  LThread:wait( )  -> nil  -- Blocks the calling thread until the background thread finishes.
```

**`LThreadPool`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`ThreadPool`].

```lua
  LThreadPool:collect( )  -> table  -- Retrieves the next result from the pool's output channel.
  LThreadPool:getInputChannel( )  -> LChannel  -- Returns the shared input channel.
  LThreadPool:getOutputChannel( )  -> LChannel  -- Returns the shared output channel.
  LThreadPool:join( )  -> nil  -- Blocks until all workers in the pool have finished execution.
  LThreadPool:size( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of workers in this pool.
  LThreadPool:submit( value )  -> nil  -- Submits a value to the pool's input channel for processing by a worker.
  LThreadPool:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LThreadPool:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.particle {#particle}

> CPU particle system: emitters, modifiers, rendering.

```lua
  lurek.particle.fromTOML( path )  -> LParticleSystem  -- Creates a new particle system from a TOML config file.
  lurek.particle.newSystem( [config] )  -> LParticleSystem  -- Creates a new particle system and stores it in the engine pool.
  lurek.particle.newTrail( lifetime, start_width )  -> LTrail  -- Creates a new trail ribbon effect.
```

**`LParticleSystem`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a particle system stored in SharedState.

```lua
  LParticleSystem:addAttractor( x, y, strength, radius )  -> nil  -- Adds a gravity well that pulls (positive strength) or repels
  LParticleSystem:addSubEmitter( config_tbl, [burst_count] )  -> nil  -- Attaches a sub-emitter that bursts when a particle dies.
  LParticleSystem:addSubSystem( config_tbl )  -> index  -- Adds a child emitter that updates and renders with this system.
  LParticleSystem:clearAttractors( )  -> nil  -- Removes all attractors from this particle system.
  LParticleSystem:clearBounds( )  -> nil  -- Removes the bounding rectangle so particles can move freely.
  LParticleSystem:clone( )  -> LParticleSystem  -- Creates a copy of this particle system (config only, no live particles).
  LParticleSystem:count( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of living particles.
  LParticleSystem:drawToImage( w, h )  -> LImageData  -- Renders all live particles to a CPU ImageData.
  LParticleSystem:emit( count )  -> nil  -- Emits a burst of the given number of particles.
  LParticleSystem:getAttractorCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of attractors currently registered on this system.
  LParticleSystem:getBufferSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum particle count.
  LParticleSystem:getColors( )  -> table  -- Returns color keyframes as a table of {r,g,b,a} tables.
  LParticleSystem:getCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of living particles (alias for count).
  LParticleSystem:getDirection( )  -> number  -- Returns emission direction in radians.
  LParticleSystem:getEmissionArea( )  -> nil  -- Returns emission area: dist-string, w, h.
  LParticleSystem:getEmissionRate( )  -> number  -- Returns particles emitted per second.
  LParticleSystem:getEmitterLifetime( )  -> number  -- Returns the emitter lifetime.
  LParticleSystem:getFlipbook( )  -> nil  -- Returns the current flipbook configuration as `(cols, rows, fps)`, or `nil` if not set.
  LParticleSystem:getGravity( )  -> number  -- Returns the gravity acceleration applied to particles as two numbers `gx, gy`.
  LParticleSystem:getInsertMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the insert mode as a string.
  LParticleSystem:getLinearAcceleration( )  -> number  -- Returns linear acceleration range.
  LParticleSystem:getLinearDamping( )  -> number  -- Returns linear damping range.
  LParticleSystem:getOffset( )  -> number  -- Returns the render origin offset.
  LParticleSystem:getParticleLifetime( )  -> number  -- Returns min and max particle lifetime.
  LParticleSystem:getPosition( )  -> number  -- Returns the emitter world position.
  LParticleSystem:getRadialAcceleration( )  -> number  -- Returns radial acceleration range.
  LParticleSystem:getRotation( )  -> number  -- Returns initial rotation range.
  LParticleSystem:getShape( )  -> string  -- Returns the particle draw shape as a string.
  LParticleSystem:getSizeVariation( )  -> number  -- Returns the maximum random size variation applied to newly emitted particles.
  LParticleSystem:getSizes( )  -> table  -- Returns size keyframes as a Lua table.
  LParticleSystem:getSpeed( )  -> number  -- Returns min/max initial speed.
  LParticleSystem:getSpin( )  -> number  -- Returns angular velocity range.
  LParticleSystem:getSpinVariation( )  -> number  -- Returns the maximum random angular velocity variation for new particles.
  LParticleSystem:getSpread( )  -> number  -- Returns the half-angle spread in radians for the emission cone.
  LParticleSystem:getTangentialAcceleration( )  -> number  -- Returns tangential acceleration range.
  LParticleSystem:hasRelativeRotation( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether relative rotation is enabled.
  LParticleSystem:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the emitter is currently emitting or has live particles.
  LParticleSystem:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if there are no live particles.
  LParticleSystem:isFull( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the system has reached max_particles.
  LParticleSystem:isPaused( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the emitter is paused.
  LParticleSystem:isStopped( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the emitter is stopped.
  LParticleSystem:moveTo( x, y )  -> nil  -- Moves the emitter to the given world position.
  LParticleSystem:pause( )  -> nil  -- Pauses particle emission; existing particles continue to simulate.
  LParticleSystem:release( )  -> nil  -- Removes the particle system from the engine, freeing its slot.
  LParticleSystem:render( [ox], [oy] )  -> nil  -- Renders all live particles to the GPU command queue.
  LParticleSystem:reset( )  -> nil  -- Removes all particles and resets the emitter.
  LParticleSystem:resume( )  -> nil  -- Resumes a paused emitter.
  LParticleSystem:setBounds( xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, restitution )  -> nil  -- Constrains all particles to an axis-aligned bounding rectangle.
  LParticleSystem:setBufferSize( n )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum number of particles (resizes the pool).
  LParticleSystem:setColors( ... )  -> nil  -- Sets color keyframes. Each arg is a table {r, g, b, a}.
  LParticleSystem:setCustomEmissionShape( cb )  -> nil  -- Sets a Lua function that returns (offset_x, offset_y) for each newly spawned
  LParticleSystem:setDirection( dir )  -> nil  -- Sets emission direction in radians.
  LParticleSystem:setEmissionArea( dist, w, h, [angle], [dir_rel] )  -> nil  -- Sets emission area distribution and size.
  LParticleSystem:setEmissionRate( rate )  -> nil  -- Sets particles emitted per second.
  LParticleSystem:setEmitterLifetime( t )  -> nil  -- Sets how long the emitter runs before auto-stopping. Negative = infinite.
  LParticleSystem:setFlipbook( cols, rows, fps )  -> nil  -- Configures sprite-sheet flipbook animation by dividing the texture into a grid.
  LParticleSystem:setGravity( gx, gy )  -> nil  -- Sets the gravity acceleration applied to all active particles each frame.
  LParticleSystem:setInsertMode( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the insert mode: "top", "bottom", or "random".
  LParticleSystem:setLinearAcceleration( xmin, ymin, xmax, ymax )  -> nil  -- Sets linear acceleration range.
  LParticleSystem:setLinearDamping( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets linear damping range.
  LParticleSystem:setOffset( ox, oy )  -> nil  -- Sets the render origin offset.
  LParticleSystem:setOnDeathBatch( cb )  -> nil  -- Sets a Lua function called after each update() with all particles that died
  LParticleSystem:setParticleLifetime( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets min and max particle lifetime in seconds.
  LParticleSystem:setPosition( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the emitter world position.
  LParticleSystem:setRadialAcceleration( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets radial acceleration range.
  LParticleSystem:setRelativeRotation( v )  -> nil  -- Sets whether particle rotation follows velocity direction.
  LParticleSystem:setRotation( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets initial rotation range in radians.
  LParticleSystem:setShape( shape )  -> nil  -- Sets the particle draw shape.
  LParticleSystem:setSizeVariation( v )  -> nil  -- Sets size variation (0-1).
  LParticleSystem:setSizes( ... )  -> nil  -- Sets size keyframes (varargs: each number is one keyframe).
  LParticleSystem:setSpeed( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets min/max initial speed.
  LParticleSystem:setSpin( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets angular velocity range.
  LParticleSystem:setSpinVariation( v )  -> nil  -- Sets spin variation (0-1).
  LParticleSystem:setSpread( spread )  -> nil  -- Sets emission spread (half-angle cone) in radians.
  LParticleSystem:setTangentialAcceleration( min, max )  -> nil  -- Sets tangential acceleration range.
  LParticleSystem:start( )  -> nil  -- Starts or restarts particle emission.
  LParticleSystem:stop( )  -> nil  -- Stops particle emission immediately.
  LParticleSystem:subSystemCount( )  -> count  -- Returns the number of direct child sub-systems attached to this emitter.
  LParticleSystem:toImage( w, h )  -> LImageData  -- Alias for `drawToImage`. Renders all live particles to a CPU ImageData.
  LParticleSystem:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name "ParticleSystem".
  LParticleSystem:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this matches the given type name.
  LParticleSystem:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the particle simulation by dt seconds.
  LParticleSystem:warmUp( seconds )  -> nil  -- Pre-simulates the particle system for `seconds` so it appears fully
```

## lurek.scene {#scene}

> Depth-sorted scene management for 2D layers.

```lua
  lurek.scene.clear( )  -> nil  -- Clears all scenes from the stack, calling leave on each.
  lurek.scene.define( [def] )  -> function  -- Creates a reusable scene class - returns a zero-argument constructor function.
  lurek.scene.depth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of scenes on the stack; alias for `getStackSize`.
  lurek.scene.deserializeScene( snapshot )  -> nil  -- Restores scene data_refs from a snapshot produced by serializeScene().
  lurek.scene.draw( )  -> nil  -- Draws all scenes in the stack from bottom to top (legacy name; prefer `render`).
  lurek.scene.fade( [duration] )  -> table  -- Pre-built named transition factory functions.  Each function accepts optional
  lurek.scene.getActiveScenes( )  -> table  -- Returns a table array of all active scene tables.
  lurek.scene.getCurrent( )  -> table  -- Returns the current top scene table, or nil if the stack is empty.
  lurek.scene.getData( key )  -> table  -- Returns a value from the inter-scene data store, or nil if not found.
  lurek.scene.getRegistered( name )  -> table  -- Returns a registered scene table by name, or nil if not found.
  lurek.scene.getRegisteredNames( )  -> table  -- Returns a list of all registered scene names.
  lurek.scene.getStackSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of scenes on the stack.
  lurek.scene.getTransitionProgress( )  -> number  -- Returns the transition progress from 0.0 to 1.0.
  lurek.scene.getTransitionProgressEased( )  -> number  -- Returns the easing-adjusted transition progress from 0.0 to 1.0.
  lurek.scene.getTransitionTypes( )  -> table  -- Returns a table listing all supported transition type strings.
  lurek.scene.hasData( key )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the given key exists in the data store.
  lurek.scene.hasRegistered( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a scene is registered under the given name.
  lurek.scene.iris( [duration] )  -> table  -- Returns an iris in/out (circular reveal) transition config table.
  lurek.scene.isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the scene stack is empty.
  lurek.scene.isOverlay( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the current top scene was pushed as an overlay.
  lurek.scene.isPreloaded( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the named scene has been preloaded.
  lurek.scene.isTransitioning( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a scene transition is currently active.
  lurek.scene.new( [def] )  -> table  -- Creates a scene instance directly from a methods table.
  lurek.scene.newDepthSorter( )  -> DepthSorter  -- Creates a new DepthSorter for z-ordered draw batching.
  lurek.scene.newScene( [def] )  -> table  -- Alias for `lurek.scene.new`. Creates a scene instance from a methods table.
  lurek.scene.pop( [transition], [duration], [easing] )  -> nil  -- Pops the top scene from the stack with an optional transition and easing.
  lurek.scene.popTo( name )  -> boolean  -- Pops scenes until the named scene is on top, calling leave on each removed.
  lurek.scene.preload( name, loader )  -> nil  -- Registers a loader function for a named scene. The loader is called
  lurek.scene.process( dt )  -> nil  -- Calls `scene:ready(self)` once per scene on the first tick after enter,
  lurek.scene.processLate( dt )  -> nil  -- Calls `scene:process_late(dt)` on all active scenes (after process, before render).
  lurek.scene.processPhysics( dt )  -> nil  -- Calls `scene:process_physics(dt)` on all active scenes (fixed timestep).
  lurek.scene.push( )  -> nil  -- Pushes a scene table onto the stack with an optional transition and easing.
  lurek.scene.pushOverlay( )  -> nil  -- Pushes a scene as a non-pausing overlay over the current top scene.
  lurek.scene.pushPreloaded( )  -> nil  -- Pushes a registered scene by name, running its loader if not yet preloaded.
  lurek.scene.registerScene( name, scene )  -> nil  -- Registers a scene table by name for later retrieval.
  lurek.scene.removeData( key )  -> nil  -- Removes a value from the inter-scene data store by key.
  lurek.scene.render( )  -> nil  -- Draws all scenes in the stack from bottom to top.
  lurek.scene.renderUi( )  -> nil  -- Draws UI overlay for all scenes in the stack from bottom to top.
  lurek.scene.serializeScene( )  -> table  -- Returns a snapshot of the scene stack as a Lua table: { stack=[name...], data={key=val} }.
  lurek.scene.setData( key, value )  -> nil  -- Stores a value in the inter-scene data store under the given key.
  lurek.scene.slide( [direction], [duration] )  -> table  -- Returns a directional slide transition config table.
  lurek.scene.switchTo( )  -> nil  -- Replaces the top scene with a new one, calling leave and enter callbacks.
  lurek.scene.unregisterScene( name )  -> nil  -- Removes a scene from the registry by name.
  lurek.scene.update( dt )  -> nil  -- Updates the top scene and any active transition (legacy name; prefer `process`).
  lurek.scene.wipe( [duration] )  -> table  -- Returns a wipe/curtain transition config table.
```

**`LDepthSorter`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`DepthSorter`] with registry-stored callbacks.

```lua
  LDepthSorter:add( callback, depth )  -> nil  -- Registers a draw callback at the given depth layer.
  LDepthSorter:addObject( obj )  -> nil  -- Registers a table object with a draw method at the given depth.
  LDepthSorter:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all registered callbacks without calling them.
  LDepthSorter:flush( )  -> nil  -- Calls all draw callbacks in sorted depth order, then clears.
  LDepthSorter:getCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of registered draw entries.
  LDepthSorter:isStable( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if stable sort mode is enabled.
  LDepthSorter:setStable( stable )  -> nil  -- Sets whether equal-depth entries preserve insertion order.
  LDepthSorter:sort( )  -> nil  -- Sorts all registered callbacks by depth ascending.
  LDepthSorter:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LDepthSorter:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.ecs {#ecs}

> Lightweight entity/component system with universe, tags, and blueprints.

```lua
  lurek.ecs.newUniverse( )  -> LUniverse  -- Creates a new empty ECS universe.
```

**`LUniverse`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Universe`] ECS world.

```lua
  LUniverse:addRelation( from, name, to )  -> nil  -- Adds a directed named relationship from entity `from` to entity `to`, ignoring duplicates.
  LUniverse:addSystem( system, [opts] )  -> nil  -- Adds a system table to the universe with an optional priority (lower = earlier).
  LUniverse:addTag( id, tag )  -> nil  -- Attaches a string tag to an entity.
  LUniverse:bitmapTag( id, name )  -> nil  -- Adds a bitmap tag to an entity.
  LUniverse:bitmapUntag( id, name )  -> nil  -- Removes a bitmap tag from an entity.
  LUniverse:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all entities, components, tags, layers, and systems. Blueprints are preserved.
  LUniverse:clearRelations( from, name )  -> nil  -- Removes all directed named relationships of type `name` from entity `from`.
  LUniverse:defineBlueprint( name, components )  -> nil  -- Defines a blueprint from a component table.
  LUniverse:defineTag( name )  -> integer  -- Defines a bitmap tag name, returning its bit index.
  LUniverse:deserialize( snapshot )  -> nil  -- Restores entity state from a snapshot produced by serialize() while preserving blueprin...
  LUniverse:each( name, callback )  -> nil  -- Calls callback(id, value) for every entity with the named component.
  LUniverse:emit( ... )  -> nil  -- Emits a named event to all systems that implement the handler, in priority order.
  LUniverse:extendBlueprint( name, parent, overrides )  -> nil  -- Defines a blueprint by extending a parent with overrides.
  LUniverse:flushObservers( )  -> nil  -- Dispatches all pending component-add and component-remove events to registered callbacks.
  LUniverse:get( id, name )  -> table  -- Returns the component value for an entity, or nil if missing.
  LUniverse:getBitmapTagBit( name )  -> integer  -- Returns the bit index for a bitmap tag name, or nil if undefined.
  LUniverse:getBlueprintComponents( name )  -> table  -- Returns a deep copy of a blueprint's component table, or nil.
  LUniverse:getChildren( parent_id )  -> table  -- Returns all direct child entity IDs.
  LUniverse:getComponents( id )  -> table  -- Returns all component names for an entity.
  LUniverse:getEntities( )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entity IDs.
  LUniverse:getEntitiesByLayer( layer )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entities on a specific layer.
  LUniverse:getEntitiesByTag( tag )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entities with the given string tag.
  LUniverse:getEntitiesSorted( )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entities sorted by layer then ID.
  LUniverse:getEntityCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of alive entities.
  LUniverse:getLayer( id )  -> integer  -- Returns the layer for an entity, defaulting to zero.
  LUniverse:getParent( child_id )  -> integer  -- Returns the parent entity ID, or nil if unparented.
  LUniverse:getRelated( from, name )  -> table  -- Returns all entity IDs reachable from `from` via the named relationship.
  LUniverse:getSystemCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of registered systems.
  LUniverse:getTags( id )  -> table  -- Returns all string tags for an entity.
  LUniverse:has( id, name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the entity has the named component.
  LUniverse:hasBitmapTag( id, name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the entity has the given bitmap tag.
  LUniverse:hasBlueprint( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a blueprint with the given name exists.
  LUniverse:hasRelation( from, name, to )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a directed named relationship from `from` to `to` exists.
  LUniverse:hasTag( id, tag )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the entity carries the given tag.
  LUniverse:isAlive( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the entity ID is currently alive.
  LUniverse:kill( id )  -> nil  -- Destroys the entity with the given ID, freeing its slot for reuse.
  LUniverse:killRecursive( id )  -> nil  -- Kills an entity and all its descendants recursively.
  LUniverse:listBlueprints( )  -> table  -- Returns all defined blueprint names.
  LUniverse:onComponentAdded( name, cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback for component-added events that is dispatched by flushObservers().
  LUniverse:onComponentRemoved( name, cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback for component-removed events that is dispatched by flushObservers().
  LUniverse:query( ... )  -> table  -- Returns entity IDs that have all listed component names.
  LUniverse:queryBitmapAll( names )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entities with all of the listed bitmap tags.
  LUniverse:queryBitmapAny( names )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entities with any of the listed bitmap tags.
  LUniverse:queryBitmapTag( name )  -> table  -- Returns all alive entities with the given bitmap tag.
  LUniverse:queryNot( with_tbl, without_tbl )  -> table  -- Returns entity IDs that have all `with` components and none of the `without` components.
  LUniverse:release( )  -> nil  -- Releases all universe state, equivalent to clear.
  LUniverse:remove( id, name )  -> nil  -- Removes a component from an entity.
  LUniverse:removeBlueprint( name )  -> nil  -- Removes a blueprint definition.
  LUniverse:removeRelation( from, name, to )  -> nil  -- Removes the directed named relationship from entity `from` to entity `to`.
  LUniverse:removeSystem( system )  -> nil  -- Removes a system table from the universe.
  LUniverse:removeTag( id, tag )  -> nil  -- Removes a string tag from an entity.
  LUniverse:render( )  -> nil  -- Calls render(system, world) on each system in priority order and falls back to draw(sys...
  LUniverse:serialize( )  -> table  -- Serializes all alive entities to a Lua table snapshot.
  LUniverse:set( id, name, value )  -> nil  -- Sets a component value on an entity.
  LUniverse:setLayer( id, layer )  -> nil  -- Sets the layer for an entity.
  LUniverse:setParent( child_id, [parent_id] )  -> nil  -- Sets or clears the parent of an entity.
  LUniverse:spawn( )  -> integer  -- Creates a new entity and returns its packed ID.
  LUniverse:spawnBlueprint( name, [overrides] )  -> integer  -- Spawns an entity from a blueprint with optional overrides.
  LUniverse:spawnBulk( name, count, [overrides] )  -> table  -- Spawns `count` entities from a blueprint, returns an array of entity IDs.
  LUniverse:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LUniverse:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LUniverse:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Calls update(system, world, dt) on each registered system in priority order.
```

## lurek.pathfind {#pathfind}

> Grid-based A* and flow-field pathfinding.

```lua
  lurek.pathfind.getThreadCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the background pathfinding thread count (currently always 0).
  lurek.pathfind.newFlowField( grid_ud )  -> LFlowField  -- Creates a new FlowField backed by a NavGrid.
  lurek.pathfind.newHexGrid( width, height, [layout_str] )  -> LHexGrid  -- Creates a hex grid for pathfinding, LOS, FOV, and range queries.
  lurek.pathfind.newJpsGrid( width, height )  -> LJpsGrid  -- Creates a uniform-cost grid optimised for Jump Point Search (orthogonal + diagonal).
  lurek.pathfind.newNavGrid( width, height )  -> LNavGrid  -- Creates a new NavGrid with all cells walkable.
  lurek.pathfind.newNavGridFromTileMap( tm_ud, layer_index, blocked_table )  -> LNavGrid  -- Builds a NavGrid from a TileMap layer, treating specified GIDs as blocked (unwalkable).
  lurek.pathfind.newPathFlowField( grid_ud )  -> LAIFlowField  -- Creates a new BFS flow field from a PathGrid.
  lurek.pathfind.newPathGrid( w, h, cell_size )  -> LPathGrid  -- Creates a new PathGrid with per-cell cost and walkability.
  lurek.pathfind.newPathfinder( grid_ud )  -> LUnitPathfinder  -- Creates a new UnitPathfinder backed by a NavGrid.
  lurek.pathfind.rangeMap( opts )  -> table  -- Computes a Dijkstra range-of-movement map from an origin within a movement budget.
  lurek.pathfind.setThreadCount( count )  -> nil  -- Sets the background pathfinding thread count (currently a no-op).
```

**`LAIFlowField`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a PathGrid-based [`AiFlowField`].

```lua
  LAIFlowField:getDirection( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the normalised direction toward the goal (1-based coordinates).
  LAIFlowField:getDistance( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the BFS distance to the goal (1-based coordinates).
  LAIFlowField:getGoal( )  -> integer  -- Returns the goal cell (1-based coordinates) or nil if unset.
  LAIFlowField:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the flow field grid height in cells.
  LAIFlowField:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the flow field grid width in cells.
  LAIFlowField:hasGoal( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a goal has been set.
  LAIFlowField:setGoal( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the goal cell and triggers BFS recomputation (1-based coordinates).
  LAIFlowField:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LAIFlowField:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LFlowField`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`FlowField`].

```lua
  LFlowField:calculate( tx, ty, [unit_size] )  -> nil  -- Computes the flow field toward a single target (1-based coordinates).
  LFlowField:calculateMulti( targets, [unit_size] )  -> nil  -- Computes the flow field toward multiple targets (1-based coordinates).
  LFlowField:getCostToTarget( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the integrated cost to the nearest target (1-based coordinates).
  LFlowField:getDirection( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the normalised direction vector at a cell (1-based coordinates).
  LFlowField:getDirectionAngle( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the flow direction as an angle in radians (1-based coordinates).
  LFlowField:getTargets( )  -> table  -- Returns the target cells from the most recent computation (1-based coordinates).
  LFlowField:isCalculated( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the flow field has been computed at least once.
  LFlowField:steer( wx, wy, speed, tw, th )  -> number  -- Converts a world-space position into a velocity vector via the flow field.
  LFlowField:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LFlowField:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LHexGrid`** methods:

```lua
  LHexGrid:distance( c1, r1, c2, r2 )  -> integer  -- Hex-distance between two cells.
```

**`LNavGrid`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`NavGrid`] with optional HPA★ abstract graph.

```lua
  LNavGrid:clearDirty( )  -> nil  -- Clears all pending dirty rectangles.
  LNavGrid:fill( cost )  -> nil  -- Sets every cell to the given cost.
  LNavGrid:fillRect( x, y, w, h, cost )  -> nil  -- Sets all cells in a rectangle to the given cost (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:getChunkSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current HPA★ chunk size.
  LNavGrid:getCost( x, y )  -> integer  -- Returns the traversal cost of a cell (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:getDiagonalMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the current diagonal movement mode as a string.
  LNavGrid:getDimensions( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid dimensions as width, height.
  LNavGrid:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid height in cells.
  LNavGrid:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid width in cells.
  LNavGrid:isBlocked( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the cell is blocked (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:isWalkable( x, y, [unit_size] )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a unit footprint is fully walkable (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:loadFromString( data )  -> nil  -- Overwrites the grid from a raw byte string (row-major, one byte per cell).
  LNavGrid:rebuildAbstract( )  -> nil  -- Rebuilds the HPA★ abstract graph from the current grid state.
  LNavGrid:saveToString( )  -> string  -- Exports the cost grid as a byte string (row-major, one byte per cell).
  LNavGrid:setBlocked( x, y, blocked )  -> nil  -- Marks a cell as blocked or unblocked (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:setChunkSize( size )  -> nil  -- Sets the HPA★ chunk size.
  LNavGrid:setCost( x, y, cost )  -> nil  -- Sets the traversal cost of a cell (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:setDiagonalMode( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the diagonal movement mode.
  LNavGrid:setDirty( x, y, w, h )  -> nil  -- Records a dirty rectangle for incremental HPA★ updates (1-based coordinates).
  LNavGrid:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LNavGrid:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LPathGrid`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`PathGrid`] (A★ weighted grid with per-cell cost).

```lua
  LPathGrid:findPath( sx, sy, gx, gy )  -> table  -- Finds an A★ path returning world-space waypoints (1-based coordinates).
  LPathGrid:findPathSmoothed( sx, sy, gx, gy )  -> table  -- Finds a smoothed A★ path with string-pulling (1-based coordinates).
  LPathGrid:getCellSize( )  -> number  -- Returns the world-space size of each cell.
  LPathGrid:getCost( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the cost multiplier for a cell (1-based coordinates).
  LPathGrid:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid height in cells.
  LPathGrid:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid width in cells.
  LPathGrid:isWalkable( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a cell is walkable (1-based coordinates).
  LPathGrid:setCost( x, y, cost )  -> nil  -- Sets the cost multiplier for a cell (1-based coordinates).
  LPathGrid:setWalkable( x, y, w )  -> nil  -- Sets the walkability of a cell (1-based coordinates).
  LPathGrid:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LPathGrid:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

```lua
  LUnitPathfinder:clearCache( )  -> nil  -- Removes all cached path results.
  LUnitPathfinder:findNearestWalkable( x, y, max_radius, [unit_size] )  -> integer  -- Finds the nearest walkable cell within a radius (1-based coordinates).
  LUnitPathfinder:findPartialPath( )  -> table  -- Finds a partial path with a node expansion limit (1-based coordinates).
  LUnitPathfinder:findPath( x1, y1, x2, y2, [unit_size] )  -> table  -- Finds an A★ path between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  LUnitPathfinder:findPathBidirectional( )  -> table  -- Finds a path with bidirectional A★ between two cells.
  LUnitPathfinder:findPathSmooth( x1, y1, x2, y2, [unit_size] )  -> table  -- Finds a Theta★ smoothed path between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  LUnitPathfinder:getCacheSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of entries in the path cache.
  LUnitPathfinder:getPathCost( path )  -> number  -- Returns the sum of grid traversal costs along a path.
  LUnitPathfinder:getPathLength( path )  -> number  -- Returns the euclidean length of a path table.
  LUnitPathfinder:heuristicDistance( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> number  -- Returns the octile heuristic distance between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  LUnitPathfinder:isCacheEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if path result caching is enabled.

  LUnitPathfinder:setCacheEnabled( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables path result caching.
  LUnitPathfinder:setCacheMaxSize( n )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum number of cached path entries.
```

## lurek.ai {#ai}

> AI subsystems: FSM, behavior tree, steering, Q-learning, squad, utility AI, GOAP.

```lua
  lurek.ai.newAIDirector( )  -> LAIDirector  -- Creates a new AI pacing director with default config.
  lurek.ai.newAILod( )  -> LAILod  -- Creates a new AI LOD controller with default 3-tier config.
  lurek.ai.newAction( callback )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT action leaf with a Lua callback.
  lurek.ai.newBandit( arm_count, strategy, epsilon, seed )  -> LBandit  -- Creates a new multi-armed bandit.
  lurek.ai.newBehaviorTree( )  -> LBehaviorTree  -- Creates a new behavior tree.
  lurek.ai.newBlackboard( )  -> LAIBlackboard  -- Creates a new standalone blackboard.
  lurek.ai.newCommandQueue( )  -> LCommandQueue  -- Creates an RTS-style command queue.
  lurek.ai.newCondition( callback )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT condition leaf with a Lua predicate.
  lurek.ai.newContextSteering( slots )  -> LContextSteering  -- Creates a new context steering controller.
  lurek.ai.newEmotionModel( )  -> LEmotionModel  -- Creates a new affective emotion model.
  lurek.ai.newGOAPPlanner( )  -> LGOAPPlanner  -- Creates a new GOAP planning solver.
  lurek.ai.newGeneticAlgorithm( pop_size, gene_count, seed )  -> LGeneticAlgorithm  -- Creates a new genetic algorithm.
  lurek.ai.newGuard( predicate, child_ud )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT guard decorator.
  lurek.ai.newHTNDomain( )  -> LHTNDomain  -- Creates a new Hierarchical Task Network domain.
  lurek.ai.newInfluenceMap( w, h, cs )  -> LInfluenceMap  -- Creates a multi-layer influence map grid.
  lurek.ai.newInverter( )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT inverter decorator.
  lurek.ai.newMCTSEngine( iters, uct_c, depth, seed )  -> LMCTSEngine  -- Creates a new Monte Carlo Tree Search engine.
  lurek.ai.newNeedSystem( )  -> LNeedSystem  -- Creates a new motivational need system.
  lurek.ai.newNeuralNet( )  -> LNeuralNet  -- Creates a new feedforward neural network (inference only).
  lurek.ai.newNeuroevolution( layer_spec, pop_size, seed )  -> LNeuroevolution  -- Creates a neuroevolution trainer (GA for neural network weights).
  lurek.ai.newORCASolver( time_horizon )  -> LORCASolver  -- Creates a new ORCA crowd avoidance solver.
  lurek.ai.newParallel( [sp], [fp] )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT parallel node with optional policies.
  lurek.ai.newQLearner( sc, ac )  -> LQLearner  -- Creates a tabular Q-learner.
  lurek.ai.newRepeater( [count] )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT repeater decorator.
  lurek.ai.newSelector( )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT selector node.
  lurek.ai.newSequence( )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT sequence node.
  lurek.ai.newSquad( name )  -> LSquad  -- Creates a named squad for formation positioning.
  lurek.ai.newStateMachine( )  -> LStateMachine  -- Creates a new finite state machine.
  lurek.ai.newSteeringManager( )  -> LSteeringManager  -- Creates a new steering behavior manager.
  lurek.ai.newStimulusWorld( )  -> LStimulusWorld  -- Creates a new stimulus perception world.
  lurek.ai.newStrategyAI( update_interval )  -> LStrategyAI  -- Creates a new throttled strategy AI.
  lurek.ai.newSucceeder( )  -> LBTNode  -- Creates a BT succeeder decorator.
  lurek.ai.newTraitProfile( )  -> LTraitProfile  -- Creates a new personality trait profile.
  lurek.ai.newUtilityAI( )  -> LUtilityAI  -- Creates a new utility AI evaluator.
  lurek.ai.newWorld( )  -> LAIWorld  -- Creates a new AI world container.
```

```lua

  LSteeringManager:addWander( )  -> nil  -- Adds a Wander behavior for random meandering.

  LSteeringManager:calculate( px, py, vx, vy, max_speed, max_force, dt )  -> number  -- Computes the combined steering force for the given agent state.
  LSteeringManager:enableSpatialHash( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables spatial-hash bucketing for neighbourhood queries.
  LSteeringManager:getBehaviorCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of active behaviors.
  LSteeringManager:getCombineMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the current combination mode.
  LSteeringManager:getLastSteering( )  -> number  -- Returns the last computed steering force.
  LSteeringManager:setCombineMode( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the force combination mode.
  LSteeringManager:setSpatialHashCellSize( size )  -> nil  -- Sets the cell size used by the spatial-hash neighborhood search.
  LSteeringManager:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LSteeringManager:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.data {#data}

> Data utilities: TOML/JSON parsing, encoding, hashing, compression.

```lua
  lurek.data.compress( format_str, raw_data, [level] )  -> string  -- Compresses data using the given algorithm (deflate, gzip, lz4).
  lurek.data.crc32( raw_data )  -> integer  -- Returns the CRC-32 checksum of the input data as an integer.
  lurek.data.decode( format_str, encoded )  -> string  -- Decodes encoded text back to binary (base64, hex).
  lurek.data.decompress( format_str, compressed )  -> string  -- Decompresses data using the given algorithm (deflate, gzip, lz4).
  lurek.data.encode( format_str, raw_data )  -> string  -- Encodes binary data using the given format (base64, hex).
  lurek.data.encodeToml( tbl )  -> string  -- Encodes a Lua table into a TOML string.
  lurek.data.fromMsgPack( bytes )  -> any  -- Deserializes a MessagePack binary string back into a Lua value.
  lurek.data.getPackedSize( fmt, ... )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of bytes the given format and values would occupy.
  lurek.data.hash( algo_str, raw_data )  -> string  -- Returns the cryptographic hash of the input (md5, sha1, sha256, sha512).
  lurek.data.newByteData( value )  -> ByteData  -- Instantiates a raw byte data container object.
  lurek.data.newDataView( raw, [offset], [size] )  -> LDataView  -- Creates a read-only windowed view into a byte string.
  lurek.data.newRingBuffer( capacity )  -> LRingBuffer  -- Creates a fixed-capacity ring buffer that can store any Lua value.
  lurek.data.newWriter( )  -> LDataWriter  -- Creates a new write-cursor for building binary data.
  lurek.data.pack( fmt, ... )  -> string  -- Packs values into a binary byte string using the format string.
  lurek.data.parseToml( text )  -> table  -- Parses a TOML string into a Lua table.
  lurek.data.read( fmt, raw, [offset] )  -> any  -- Reads values using the Lurek2D Binary Pack Format.
  lurek.data.size( fmt )  -> integer  -- Returns the byte size of a Lurek2D Binary Pack Format string.
  lurek.data.toMsgPack( value )  -> string  -- Serializes a Lua value (table, string, number, boolean, or nil) to MessagePack binary.
  lurek.data.unpack( fmt, raw, [offset] )  -> any  -- Unpacks values from a binary byte string, returning values followed by next offset.
  lurek.data.write( fmt, ... )  -> string  -- Writes values using the Lurek2D Binary Pack Format.
```

**`LByteData`** methods:

> Raw byte buffer for binary I/O; addressable by byte or bit offset.

```lua
  LByteData:clone( )  -> ByteData  -- Creates an independent copy of this byte buffer with identical contents.
  LByteData:getBit( byte_offset, bit_offset )  -> boolean  -- Returns the value of a single bit within the buffer.
  LByteData:getByte( offset )  -> integer  -- Get a byte at the specified offset.
  LByteData:getSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total byte length of this buffer.
  LByteData:getString( )  -> string  -- Get the string representation.
  LByteData:readBits( byte_offset, bit_offset, count )  -> integer  -- Reads consecutive bits and packs them into a 32-bit integer.
  LByteData:setBit( byte_offset, bit_offset, value )  -> nil  -- Sets or clears a single bit within the buffer.
  LByteData:setByte( offset, value )  -> nil  -- Set a byte at the specified offset.
```

**`LDataView`** methods:

> Access structured binary data efficiently without copying.

```lua
  LDataView:getDouble( offset )  -> number  -- Reads a 64-bit float at the given offset.
  LDataView:getFloat( offset )  -> number  -- Reads a 32-bit float at the given offset.
  LDataView:getInt16( offset )  -> integer  -- Reads a signed 16-bit integer at the given offset.
  LDataView:getInt32( offset )  -> integer  -- Reads a signed 32-bit integer at the given offset.
  LDataView:getInt8( offset )  -> integer  -- Reads a signed 8-bit integer at the given offset.
  LDataView:getSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the size of this view in bytes.
  LDataView:getUInt16( offset )  -> integer  -- Reads an unsigned 16-bit integer at the given offset.
  LDataView:getUInt32( offset )  -> integer  -- Reads an unsigned 32-bit integer at the given offset.
  LDataView:getUInt8( offset )  -> integer  -- Reads an unsigned 8-bit integer at the given offset.
  LDataView:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LDataView:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LDataWriter`** methods:

> Write-cursor wrapper for the `lurek.data` module.

```lua
  LDataWriter:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total buffer length.
  LDataWriter:seek( pos )  -> nil  -- Moves the write cursor to the given position.
  LDataWriter:tell( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current write cursor position.
  LDataWriter:toBytes( )  -> string  -- Returns the buffer contents as a Lua string.
  LDataWriter:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LDataWriter:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LDataWriter:writeBytes( )  -> nil  -- Writes raw bytes from a Lua string.
  LDataWriter:writeF32LE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes a 32-bit LE float.
  LDataWriter:writeF64LE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes a 64-bit LE float.
  LDataWriter:writeI16LE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes a signed 16-bit LE integer.
  LDataWriter:writeI32LE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes a signed 32-bit LE integer.
  LDataWriter:writeI8( v )  -> nil  -- Writes a signed 8-bit integer.
  LDataWriter:writeString( s )  -> nil  -- Writes a length-prefixed UTF-8 string (4-byte LE length + bytes).
  LDataWriter:writeU16BE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes an unsigned 16-bit BE integer.
  LDataWriter:writeU16LE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes an unsigned 16-bit LE integer.
  LDataWriter:writeU32LE( v )  -> nil  -- Writes an unsigned 32-bit LE integer.
  LDataWriter:writeU8( v )  -> nil  -- Writes an unsigned 8-bit integer.
```

**`LRingBuffer`** methods:

> Lua-side fixed-capacity ring buffer that holds any Lua value.

```lua
  LRingBuffer:capacity( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum number of elements the buffer can hold.
  LRingBuffer:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all elements from the buffer, releasing their registry entries.
  LRingBuffer:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the buffer contains no elements.
  LRingBuffer:isFull( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the buffer has reached its capacity.
  LRingBuffer:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of elements currently in the buffer.
  LRingBuffer:peek( )  -> any  -- Returns the oldest element without removing it, or nil if empty.
  LRingBuffer:peekNewest( )  -> any  -- Returns the newest element without removing it, or nil if empty.
  LRingBuffer:pop( )  -> any  -- Removes and returns the oldest element, or nil if the buffer is empty.
  LRingBuffer:push( value )  -> boolean  -- Pushes a value onto the ring buffer.
  LRingBuffer:toTable( )  -> table  -- Returns all elements as an array table ordered oldest-first.
  LRingBuffer:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LRingBuffer:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.compute {#compute}

> Dense NdArray numerical computing: element ops, reductions, convolutions.

```lua
  lurek.compute.affine2d( tx, ty, angle_rad, sx, sy )  -> Array  -- Creates a 3Ă-3 homogeneous affine matrix.
  lurek.compute.fft( samples )  -> table  -- Computes the discrete Fourier transform of a 1D real-valued sample array.
  lurek.compute.fftMagnitude( samples )  -> table  -- Returns the magnitude spectrum `|X[k]|` of a real-valued sample array.
  lurek.compute.fromTable( data, [shape], [dtype] )  -> Array  -- Creates an array from a Lua table of numbers with optional shape and dtype.
  lurek.compute.gaussianKernel( size, sigma )  -> Array  -- Creates a sizeĂ-size Gaussian kernel array.
  lurek.compute.ifft( freqs )  -> table  -- Computes the inverse discrete Fourier transform.
  lurek.compute.newArray( shape, [dtype] )  -> Array  -- Creates a zero-initialized array with the given shape and optional dtype.
  lurek.compute.ones( shape, [dtype] )  -> Array  -- Creates a one-filled array with the given shape and optional dtype.
  lurek.compute.range( start, stop, [step], [dtype] )  -> Array  -- Creates a 1D array from start to stop with optional step and dtype.
  lurek.compute.rotate2dMatrix( angle_rad )  -> Array  -- Creates a 2Ă-2 rotation matrix for the given angle in radians.
  lurek.compute.zeros( shape, [dtype] )  -> Array  -- Creates a zero-filled array with the given shape and optional dtype.
```

**`LArray`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`NdArray`].

```lua
  LArray:abs( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise absolute value.
  LArray:add( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise addition with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:all( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if all elements are nonzero.
  LArray:any( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if any element is nonzero.
  LArray:argmax( )  -> integer  -- Returns the 1-based flat index of the maximum element.
  LArray:argmin( )  -> integer  -- Returns the 1-based flat index of the minimum element.
  LArray:bitwiseAnd( other )  -> Array  -- Bitwise AND of two Int32 arrays.
  LArray:bitwiseLShift( amount )  -> Array  -- Bitwise left shift of an Int32 array.
  LArray:bitwiseNot( )  -> Array  -- Bitwise NOT of an Int32 array.
  LArray:bitwiseOr( other )  -> Array  -- Bitwise OR of two Int32 arrays.
  LArray:bitwiseRShift( amount )  -> Array  -- Bitwise right shift of an Int32 array.
  LArray:bitwiseXor( other )  -> Array  -- Bitwise XOR of two Int32 arrays.
  LArray:clamp( min, max )  -> Array  -- Clamps each element to the given range.
  LArray:clone( )  -> Array  -- Returns a deep copy of this array.
  LArray:convolve1d( kernel )  -> Array  -- 1D convolution with a kernel array (full output).
  LArray:convolve2D( kernel )  -> Array  -- 2D convolution with zero-padding.
  LArray:correlate1d( template )  -> Array  -- 1D cross-correlation with a template array (valid output).
  LArray:countNonZero( )  -> integer  -- Returns the count of nonzero elements.
  LArray:covariance( other )  -> number  -- Population covariance with another 1D array.
  LArray:cross2d( other )  -> number  -- Signed 2D cross product with another length-2 array.
  LArray:cumsum( )  -> Array  -- Cumulative sum of all elements (flattened).
  LArray:diff( [order] )  -> Array  -- Discrete difference applied `order` times.
  LArray:dilate( radius )  -> Array  -- Morphological dilation with a diamond structuring element.
  LArray:div( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise division with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:dot( other )  -> number  -- Dot product of two 1D arrays.
  LArray:eigenPower( [max_iter], [tol] )  -> table  -- Computes the dominant eigenvalue and its eigenvector using power iteration.
  LArray:eq( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise equality with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:erode( radius )  -> Array  -- Morphological erosion with a diamond structuring element.
  LArray:eval( expr )  -> Array  -- Evaluate a Lua expression string element-wise, returning a new Array.
  LArray:fill( val )  -> nil  -- Fills all elements with the given value in-place.
  LArray:floodFill( row, col, val )  -> Array  -- Flood fill from a 1-based (row, col) with a new value.
  LArray:get( ... )  -> number  -- Returns the element at the given 1-based indices.
  LArray:getDataType( )  -> string  -- Returns the element data type name.
  LArray:getDimensions( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of dimensions.
  LArray:getRegion( row, col, rows, cols )  -> Array  -- Extracts a rectangular sub-region (1-based row, col).
  LArray:getShape( )  -> table  -- Returns the shape as a table of dimension sizes.
  LArray:getSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of elements.
  LArray:gt( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise greater-than with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:gte( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise greater-or-equal with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:histogram( bins, [lo], [hi] )  -> table  -- Compute a histogram. Returns a table of {lo, hi, count} tables.
  LArray:isOnGPU( )  -> boolean  -- Returns false (CPU arrays only).
  LArray:linsolve( b )  -> Array  -- Solve A*x = b where this array is A (square [n,n]) and b is a 1D vector.
  LArray:lt( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise less-than with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:lte( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise less-or-equal with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:luDecompose( )  -> table  -- Decomposes this square matrix into L and U factors with partial pivoting.
  LArray:map( func )  -> Array  -- Apply a Lua callback element-wise, returning a new Array of the same shape.
  LArray:matmul( other )  -> Array  -- Matrix multiplication of two 2D arrays.
  LArray:max( [axis] )  -> Array  -- Maximum of all elements, or along an axis (1-based).
  LArray:mean( [axis] )  -> Array  -- Mean of all elements, or along an axis (1-based).
  LArray:min( [axis] )  -> Array  -- Minimum of all elements, or along an axis (1-based).
  LArray:mul( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise multiplication with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:neg( )  -> Array  -- Returns a new Array with every element negated (multiplied by -1).
  LArray:neq( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise not-equal with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:normalizeRange( lo, hi )  -> Array  -- Linearly rescale values to [out_min, out_max].
  LArray:normalizeVec( )  -> Array  -- L2-normalise a 1D vector.
  LArray:outer( other )  -> Array  -- Outer product of two 1D vectors -> 2D array [m, n].
  LArray:pearsonCorr( other )  -> number  -- Pearson correlation coefficient with another 1D array.
  LArray:percentile( p )  -> number  -- Compute the p-th percentile (0-100).
  LArray:pow( exp )  -> Array  -- Raises each element to a scalar exponent.
  LArray:reduce( func, init )  -> number  -- Fold the array left-to-right with an accumulator.
  LArray:reshape( shape )  -> Array  -- Returns a new array with the given shape and the same data.
  LArray:scan( func, init )  -> Array  -- Running accumulation - like reduce but returns every intermediate result.
  LArray:set( ... )  -> nil  -- Sets the element at the given 1-based indices to a value.
  LArray:setRegion( row, col, source )  -> nil  -- Copies a source array into this array at the given 1-based position.
  LArray:sobel( )  -> table  -- Apply Sobel edge detection to a 2D array. Returns {gx=Array, gy=Array}.
  LArray:sqrt( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise square root.
  LArray:sub( )  -> Array  -- Element-wise subtraction with an Array or scalar.
  LArray:sum( [axis] )  -> Array  -- Sum of all elements, or along an axis (1-based).
  LArray:threshold( val )  -> Array  -- Returns a mask array with 1.0 where elements >= val, else 0.0.
  LArray:toTable( )  -> table  -- Returns all elements as a flat table of numbers.
  LArray:transformPoints( pts )  -> Array  -- Apply this 2Ă-2 or 3Ă-3 matrix to an [N,2] points array.
  LArray:transpose( )  -> Array  -- Returns the transposed 2D array.
  LArray:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name "Array".
  LArray:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the given name matches "Array" or a parent type.
  LArray:where( mask, other )  -> Array  -- Selects elements from this where mask is nonzero, else from other.
  LArray:zscore( )  -> Array  -- Standardise values to zero mean and unit variance.
```

## lurek.dataframe {#dataframe}

> Tabular data: DataFrame construction, column ops, filtering, CSV.

```lua
  lurek.dataframe.fromBinary( s )  -> LDataFrame  -- Deserializes a binary LVDF string into a DataFrame.
  lurek.dataframe.fromCSV( s )  -> LDataFrame  -- Parses a CSV string into a DataFrame.
  lurek.dataframe.fromJSON( s )  -> LDataFrame  -- Parses a JSON string into a DataFrame.
  lurek.dataframe.fromTable( rows )  -> LDataFrame  -- Creates a DataFrame from an array of row tables.
  lurek.dataframe.fromVec( vf )  -> LDataFrame  -- Converts a VecFrame back to a DataFrame.
  lurek.dataframe.newDataFrame( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Creates a new empty DataFrame.
  lurek.dataframe.newDatabase( )  -> LDatabase  -- Creates a new empty Database.
  lurek.dataframe.random( defs_tbl, n, [seed] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Generates a DataFrame with random data from column definitions.
  lurek.dataframe.toVec( df )  -> LVecFrame  -- Converts a DataFrame to a VecFrame for vectorized column operations.
```

**`LDataFrame`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a shared [`DataFrame`].

```lua
  LDataFrame:addColumn( name, [default] )  -> nil  -- Adds a new column with an optional default value.
  LDataFrame:addRow( [row_tbl] )  -> integer  -- Adds a row from an optional table of name-value pairs, returns 1-based index.
  LDataFrame:addRowBatch( rows )  -> nil  -- Add multiple rows at once from a table of row tables.
  LDataFrame:apply( col_val, func )  -> nil  -- Applies a function to each value in a column, replacing cells with results.
  LDataFrame:clone( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns a deep copy of this DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:columns( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of column names.
  LDataFrame:corr( col_a, col_b )  -> number  -- Pearson correlation coefficient between two numeric columns.
  LDataFrame:correlationMatrix( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Compute a correlation matrix for all numeric columns.
  LDataFrame:count( )  -> integer  -- Returns the row count (alias for nrows).
  LDataFrame:countBy( col )  -> LDataFrame  -- Counts distinct values in a column, returns a DataFrame with value and count columns.
  LDataFrame:describe( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns descriptive statistics for all numeric columns.
  LDataFrame:dropNil( col )  -> LDataFrame  -- Removes rows where the given column is nil, returns a new DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:entropy( col )  -> number  -- Shannon entropy (bits) of the value distribution in a column.
  LDataFrame:fillNil( col, val )  -> nil  -- Replaces nil values in a column with the given value.
  LDataFrame:filter( col, op, val )  -> LDataFrame  -- Filters rows where column matches a condition, returns a new DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:getColumn( col )  -> table  -- Returns all values in a column as a table.
  LDataFrame:getColumnAsF64( col )  -> table  -- Return a numeric column as a Lua array of numbers (nils -> 0/nan).
  LDataFrame:getRow( row )  -> table  -- Returns a row as a table of name-value pairs.
  LDataFrame:getValue( row, col )  -> table  -- Returns a single cell value.
  LDataFrame:groupAgg( group_col, agg_col, fn_name )  -> LDataFrame  -- Aggregate agg_col grouped by group_col using the named function.
  LDataFrame:groupBy( col )  -> table  -- Groups rows by column value, returns a table of DataFrames keyed by value.
  LDataFrame:groupByObj( col )  -> LGroupedFrame  -- Groups rows by column value, returns a GroupedFrame object supporting aggregate().
  LDataFrame:head( [n] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns the first n rows (default 5).
  LDataFrame:join( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Joins with another DataFrame on matching columns.
  LDataFrame:max( col )  -> number  -- Returns the maximum numeric value in a column.
  LDataFrame:mean( col )  -> number  -- Returns the mean of numeric values in a column.
  LDataFrame:median( col )  -> number  -- Returns the median of numeric values in a column.
  LDataFrame:merge( other )  -> nil  -- Appends rows from another DataFrame in-place.
  LDataFrame:min( col )  -> number  -- Returns the minimum numeric value in a column.
  LDataFrame:modeVal( col )  -> table  -- Return the most frequent value in a column (nil if empty).
  LDataFrame:ncols( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of columns.
  LDataFrame:normalizeCol( col, out_min, out_max, name )  -> nil  -- Add a min-max normalized column scaled to [out_min, out_max].
  LDataFrame:nrows( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of rows.
  LDataFrame:outliers( col, [threshold] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Return a new DataFrame with only outlier rows (|z-score| > threshold).
  LDataFrame:pivot( row_col, col_col, val_col )  -> LDataFrame  -- Creates a wide pivot table by reshaping rows into columns.
  LDataFrame:pivotTable( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Reshapes a long-format DataFrame into wide format.
  LDataFrame:query( sql_str )  -> LDataFrame  -- Executes a SQL query against this DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:rank( col, [order], [result_col] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with a dense-rank column appended.
  LDataFrame:removeColumn( col )  -> nil  -- Removes a column by name or index.
  LDataFrame:removeRow( row )  -> nil  -- Removes a row by 1-based index.
  LDataFrame:rename( col, new_name )  -> nil  -- Renames the column `old_name` to `new_name` in this DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:rollingMean( col, window, [result_col] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with a rolling mean column appended.
  LDataFrame:rollingSum( col, window, [result_col] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with a rolling sum column appended.
  LDataFrame:sample( n, [seed] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns a random sample of n rows.
  LDataFrame:select( ... )  -> LDataFrame  -- Selects a subset of columns, returns a new DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:setColumnFromF64( col, values )  -> nil  -- Set a numeric column from a Lua array of numbers.
  LDataFrame:setValue( row, col, val )  -> nil  -- Sets a single cell value.
  LDataFrame:slice( start, end )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns rows from start to end (1-based, inclusive).
  LDataFrame:sort( col, [ascending] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Sorts by column, returns a new DataFrame.
  LDataFrame:stddev( col )  -> number  -- Returns the population standard deviation of numeric values in a column.
  LDataFrame:sum( col )  -> number  -- Returns the sum of numeric values in a column.
  LDataFrame:tail( [n] )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns the last n rows (default 5).
  LDataFrame:toBinary( )  -> string  -- Serializes this DataFrame to a binary LVDF string.
  LDataFrame:toCSV( )  -> string  -- Serializes this DataFrame to a CSV string.
  LDataFrame:toJSON( )  -> string  -- Serializes this DataFrame to a JSON string.
  LDataFrame:toString( )  -> string  -- Returns a formatted string table representation.
  LDataFrame:toTable( )  -> table  -- Converts this DataFrame to a Lua table of row tables.
  LDataFrame:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LDataFrame:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LDataFrame:unique( col )  -> table  -- Returns unique values in a column as a table.
  LDataFrame:variance( col )  -> number  -- Returns the population variance of numeric values in a column.
  LDataFrame:withCumsum( col, name )  -> nil  -- Add a cumulative-sum column.
  LDataFrame:withEval( col_name, expr )  -> LDataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with an additional computed column named `col_name`.
  LDataFrame:withPctChange( col, name )  -> nil  -- Add a percent-change-from-previous-row column.
  LDataFrame:withRank( col, [asc], name )  -> nil  -- Add a rank column (1-based, ties averaged).
  LDataFrame:withRollingMax( col, window, name )  -> nil  -- Add a rolling maximum column.
  LDataFrame:withRollingMean( col, window, name )  -> nil  -- Add a rolling mean column. Rows with insufficient history get nil.
  LDataFrame:withRollingMin( col, window, name )  -> nil  -- Add a rolling minimum column.
  LDataFrame:withRollingSum( col, window, name )  -> nil  -- Add a rolling sum column.
  LDataFrame:zscoreCol( col, name )  -> nil  -- Add a z-score column for the given numeric column.
```

**`LDatabase`** methods:

```lua
  LDatabase:addTable( name, df_ud )  -> nil  -- Adds or replaces a table by cloning the given DataFrame.

  LDatabase:hasTable( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a table with the given name exists.

  LDatabase:merge( other )  -> nil  -- Merges all tables from another Database into this one.
  LDatabase:query( sql_str )  -> LDataFrame  -- Executes a SQL query against the database tables.
  LDatabase:removeTable( name )  -> nil  -- Drops the named table from this in-memory database if it exists.
  LDatabase:tableCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of tables.
  LDatabase:toJSON( )  -> string  -- Serializes all tables to a JSON object string.
  LDatabase:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LDatabase:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

```lua
  LGroupedFrame:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```
