
**`LVecFrame`** methods:

> Thin Lua wrapper around a [`VecFrame`]: typed-column vectorized DataFrame.

```lua
  LVecFrame:applyMask( mask_tbl )  -> LVecFrame  -- Return a new VecFrame containing only the rows where mask[i] is true.
  LVecFrame:colAbs( col )  -> nil  -- Apply absolute value to every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colAdd( col, val )  -> nil  -- Add a scalar to every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colCast( col, dtype )  -> nil  -- Cast a column to a new dtype: "float64", "int64", or "text".
  LVecFrame:colCeil( col )  -> nil  -- Apply ceiling to every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colClamp( col, min_val, max_val )  -> nil  -- Clamp every element of a Float64 column to [min, max].
  LVecFrame:colDiv( col, val )  -> nil  -- Divide every element of a Float64 column by a scalar.
  LVecFrame:colFloor( col )  -> nil  -- Apply floor to every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colMul( col, val )  -> nil  -- Multiply every element of a Float64 column by a scalar.
  LVecFrame:colNeg( col )  -> nil  -- Negate every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colOp( out_col, left_col, op, right_col )  -> nil  -- Compute out[i] = left[i] op right[i] for every row.
  LVecFrame:colSqrt( col )  -> nil  -- Apply square root to every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colSub( col, val )  -> nil  -- Subtract a scalar from every element of a Float64 column.
  LVecFrame:colType( col )  -> string  -- Return the dtype name of a column: "float64", "int64", "bool", or "text".
  LVecFrame:columns( )  -> table  -- Return a table of column names.
  LVecFrame:filterMask( col, cmp_op, val )  -> table  -- Build a boolean row mask: mask[i] = col[i] cmp_op val.
  LVecFrame:ncols( )  -> integer  -- Return the number of columns.
  LVecFrame:nrows( )  -> integer  -- Return the number of rows.
  LVecFrame:parReduce( cols_tbl, op )  -> table  -- Reduce multiple columns in parallel, returning {col -> value} table.
  LVecFrame:parScalarOp( cols_tbl, op, val )  -> nil  -- Apply a scalar op in parallel to multiple Float64 columns.
  LVecFrame:reduce( col, op )  -> number  -- Reduce an entire numeric column to a single value.
  LVecFrame:toDataFrame( )  -> LDataFrame  -- Convert this VecFrame back to a DataFrame.
  LVecFrame:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LVecFrame:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.graph {#graph}

> Directed graph: nodes, edges, item flow, Dijkstra pathfinding.

```lua
  lurek.graph.newGraph( )  -> Graph  -- Creates a new empty directed graph for item flow simulation.
```

**`LGraph`** methods:

> Lua wrapper around a directed `Graph` with event callback registry.

```lua
  LGraph:addEdge( from_ud, to_ud, [edge_type] )  -> Edge  -- Adds a directed edge between two nodes and returns its handle.
  LGraph:addItem( item_ud, node_ud )  -> boolean  -- Places an item at a node.
  LGraph:addNode( [node_type], [capacity] )  -> Node  -- Adds a node and returns its handle.
  LGraph:astar( from_node, to_node )  -> table  -- Finds the shortest path between two nodes using A*.
  LGraph:colorGraph( )  -> table  -- Assigns each node the smallest non-negative integer colour not shared with any
  LGraph:createItem( [item_type], [decay_time] )  -> GraphItem  -- Creates a new unplaced item and returns its handle.
  LGraph:findPath( from_ud, to_ud )  -> table  -- Finds the shortest path between two nodes using Dijkstra.
  LGraph:findPathForItem( item_ud, from_ud, to_ud )  -> table  -- Finds the shortest path for a specific item, filtering by item type.
  LGraph:getComponents( )  -> table  -- Returns weakly connected components as a table of tables of Node handles.
  LGraph:getDistance( from_ud, to_ud )  -> number  -- Returns the shortest path distance, or nil if unreachable.
  LGraph:getEdgeBetween( from_ud, to_ud )  -> Edge  -- Returns the edge between two nodes, or nil if none exists.
  LGraph:getEdgeCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of edges in the graph.
  LGraph:getEdges( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of all Edge handles.
  LGraph:getItemCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items in the graph.
  LGraph:getItems( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of all GraphItem handles.
  LGraph:getNeighbors( node_ud )  -> table  -- Returns a table of direct neighbor Node handles.
  LGraph:getNodeCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of nodes in the graph.
  LGraph:getNodes( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of all Node handles.
  LGraph:getReachable( from_ud, [max_dist] )  -> table  -- Returns a table of Node handles reachable from the given node.
  LGraph:getStats( )  -> table  -- Returns a statistics snapshot table.
  LGraph:hasCycle( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the graph contains a directed cycle.
  LGraph:hasEdge( edge_ud )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the edge exists in the graph.
  LGraph:hasItem( item_ud )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the item exists in the graph.
  LGraph:hasNode( node_ud )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the node exists in the graph.
  LGraph:isBipartite( )  -> boolean  -- Returns `true` when the graph can be 2-coloured (bipartite check via BFS).
  LGraph:mst( )  -> table  -- Returns edge IDs forming a minimum spanning tree (Kruskal, undirected view).
  LGraph:on( event_name, func )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback for a graph simulation event.
  LGraph:processDemand( )  -> nil  -- Processes all supply/demand declarations and fires event callbacks.
  LGraph:removeEdge( edge_ud )  -> boolean  -- Removes an edge from the graph.
  LGraph:removeItem( item_ud )  -> boolean  -- Removes an item from the graph entirely.
  LGraph:removeNode( node_ud )  -> boolean  -- Removes a node from the graph.
  LGraph:sendItem( item_ud, edge_ud )  -> boolean  -- Sends an item onto an edge to begin transit.
  LGraph:step( )  -> nil  -- Runs one discrete simulation step and fires event callbacks.
  LGraph:tickParallel( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances simulation by dt seconds using a parallelised decay phase.
  LGraph:topologicalSort( )  -> table  -- Returns a topologically sorted table of Node handles, or nil if a cycle exists.
  LGraph:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LGraph:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LGraph:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances simulation by dt seconds and fires event callbacks.
```

**`LGraphEdge`** methods:

> Lua handle for an edge inside a `Graph`.

```lua
  LGraphEdge:addAllowedType( t )  -> nil  -- Adds an item type to the edge allow-list.
  LGraphEdge:clearAllowedTypes( )  -> nil  -- Clears the edge allow-list so all item types are permitted.
  LGraphEdge:getCapacity( )  -> integer  -- Returns the edge capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  LGraphEdge:getCooldown( )  -> number  -- Returns the cooldown duration in seconds.
  LGraphEdge:getFrom( )  -> Node  -- Returns the source node handle.
  LGraphEdge:getItemsInTransit( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of GraphItem handles currently in transit on this edge.
  LGraphEdge:getSpeedModifier( )  -> number  -- Returns the speed modifier applied to items in transit.
  LGraphEdge:getThroughput( )  -> number  -- Returns items per second this edge can transfer.
  LGraphEdge:getTo( )  -> Node  -- Returns the destination node handle.
  LGraphEdge:getTravelTime( )  -> number  -- Returns the travel time in seconds for items on this edge.
  LGraphEdge:getType( )  -> string  -- Returns the edge type string.
  LGraphEdge:getWeight( )  -> number  -- Returns the pathfinding weight of this edge.
  LGraphEdge:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the edge is active.
  LGraphEdge:isBidirectional( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if items can travel the edge in either direction.
  LGraphEdge:isItemTypeAllowed( t )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the given item type is allowed on this edge.
  LGraphEdge:isOnCooldown( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the edge is currently on cooldown.
  LGraphEdge:removeAllowedType( t )  -> boolean  -- Removes an item type from the edge allow-list.
  LGraphEdge:setActive( a )  -> nil  -- Sets the active state of this edge.
  LGraphEdge:setBidirectional( b )  -> nil  -- Sets whether items can travel the edge in either direction.
  LGraphEdge:setCapacity( c )  -> nil  -- Sets the edge capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  LGraphEdge:setCooldown( c )  -> nil  -- Sets the cooldown duration in seconds.
  LGraphEdge:setSpeedModifier( m )  -> nil  -- Sets the speed modifier applied to items in transit.
  LGraphEdge:setThroughput( t )  -> nil  -- Sets items per second this edge can transfer.
  LGraphEdge:setTravelTime( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the travel time in seconds for items on this edge.
  LGraphEdge:setType( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the edge type string.
  LGraphEdge:setWeight( w )  -> nil  -- Sets the pathfinding weight of this edge.
  LGraphEdge:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name "GraphEdge".
  LGraphEdge:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the given name matches "GraphEdge" or a parent type.
```

**`LGraphItem`** methods:

> Lua handle for a graph item (typed item) inside a `Graph`.

```lua
  LGraphItem:getDecayTime( )  -> number  -- Returns the decay time in seconds (-1 = immortal).
  LGraphItem:getPosition( )  -> nil  -- Returns the item position: node userdata if at a node, (edge, progress)
  LGraphItem:getPriority( )  -> integer  -- Returns the item priority.
  LGraphItem:getRemainingLife( )  -> number  -- Returns the remaining life in seconds.
  LGraphItem:getType( )  -> string  -- Returns the item type string.
  LGraphItem:isAlive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the item is alive.
  LGraphItem:kill( )  -> nil  -- Marks this graph item as dead so it is removed on the next cleanup pass.
  LGraphItem:setDecayTime( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the decay time in seconds (-1 = immortal).
  LGraphItem:setPriority( p )  -> nil  -- Sets the scheduling priority; higher values are processed before lower ones.
  LGraphItem:setType( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the item type string.
  LGraphItem:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LGraphItem:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LGraphNode`** methods:

> Lua handle for a node inside a `Graph`.

```lua
  LGraphNode:addDemand( item_type, quantity, [priority] )  -> nil  -- Declares a demand for the given item type, quantity, and priority.
  LGraphNode:addSupply( item_type, quantity )  -> nil  -- Declares a supply of the given item type and quantity at this node.
  LGraphNode:addTag( tag )  -> nil  -- Attaches a string tag to this node for fast group queries.
  LGraphNode:clearAllConversions( )  -> nil  -- Removes all conversion rules from this node.
  LGraphNode:clearConversion( in_type )  -> nil  -- Removes the conversion rule for the given input type.
  LGraphNode:clearDemands( )  -> nil  -- Removes all demand declarations from this node.
  LGraphNode:clearSupplies( )  -> nil  -- Removes all supply declarations from this node.
  LGraphNode:clearTags( )  -> nil  -- Removes all tags from this node.
  LGraphNode:dequeue( )  -> nil  -- Pops the next item from the node queue, or nil if empty.
  LGraphNode:enqueue( item_ud )  -> boolean  -- Pushes an item into the node queue.
  LGraphNode:getCapacity( )  -> integer  -- Returns the node capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  LGraphNode:getEdges( [dir] )  -> table  -- Returns a table of Edge handles connected to this node.
  LGraphNode:getFlowMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the flow mode as a string.
  LGraphNode:getItemCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items currently at this node.
  LGraphNode:getItems( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of GraphItem handles at this node.
  LGraphNode:getOverflowPolicy( )  -> string  -- Returns the overflow policy as a string.
  LGraphNode:getProcessTime( )  -> number  -- Returns the processing time in seconds.
  LGraphNode:getPullFilter( )  -> string  -- Returns the pull filter string, or nil if unset.
  LGraphNode:getPullRate( )  -> number  -- Returns items per second this node pulls.
  LGraphNode:getPushFilter( )  -> string  -- Returns the push filter string, or nil if unset.
  LGraphNode:getPushRate( )  -> number  -- Returns items per second this node pushes.
  LGraphNode:getQueueCapacity( )  -> integer  -- Returns the queue capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  LGraphNode:getQueueSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items currently in the queue.
  LGraphNode:getTags( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of tag strings on this node.
  LGraphNode:getType( )  -> string  -- Returns the node type string.
  LGraphNode:hasTag( tag )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this node has the given tag.
  LGraphNode:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the node is active.
  LGraphNode:isFull( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the node has reached its capacity.
  LGraphNode:isQueueEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the node queue is enabled.
  LGraphNode:removeDemand( item_type )  -> boolean  -- Removes the demand declaration for the given item type.
  LGraphNode:removeSupply( item_type )  -> boolean  -- Removes the supply declaration for the given item type.
  LGraphNode:removeTag( tag )  -> boolean  -- Removes a tag from this node.
  LGraphNode:setActive( a )  -> nil  -- Sets the active state of this node.
  LGraphNode:setCapacity( c )  -> nil  -- Sets the node capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  LGraphNode:setConversion( )  -> nil  -- Adds or replaces a conversion rule on this node.
  LGraphNode:setFlowMode( m )  -> nil  -- Sets the flow mode from a string.
  LGraphNode:setOverflowPolicy( p )  -> nil  -- Sets the overflow policy from a string.
  LGraphNode:setProcessTime( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the processing time in seconds.
  LGraphNode:setPullFilter( [f] )  -> nil  -- Sets the pull filter string, or nil to clear.
  LGraphNode:setPullRate( r )  -> nil  -- Sets items per second this node pulls.
  LGraphNode:setPushFilter( [f] )  -> nil  -- Sets the push filter string, or nil to clear.
  LGraphNode:setPushRate( r )  -> nil  -- Sets items per second this node pushes.
  LGraphNode:setQueueCapacity( c )  -> nil  -- Sets the queue capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  LGraphNode:setQueueEnabled( e )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the node queue.
  LGraphNode:setType( t )  -> nil  -- Sets the node type string.
  LGraphNode:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name "GraphNode".
  LGraphNode:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the given name matches "GraphNode" or a parent type.
```

## lurek.minimap {#minimap}

> Minimap rendering from tile data.

```lua
  lurek.minimap.newMinimap( grid_w, grid_h, [display_w], [display_h] )  -> Minimap  -- Creates a new grid-based minimap.
```

**`LMinimap`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Minimap`].

```lua
  LMinimap:addMarker( )  -> integer  -- Adds a persistent marker and returns its auto-assigned ID.
  LMinimap:addObjectType( name, r, g, b, [a] )  -> integer  -- Registers a new object type and returns its 1-based index.
  LMinimap:addPing( )  -> nil  -- Adds an animated ping at grid coordinates with a duration and optional color.
  LMinimap:clearMarkerAnimation( id )  -> nil  -- Removes the animation from a marker, reverting it to static.
  LMinimap:clearObjects( )  -> nil  -- Removes all tracked objects.
  LMinimap:clearOverlay( )  -> nil  -- Removes all custom geometry from the minimap overlay.
  LMinimap:clearPath( [id] )  -> nil  -- Removes a displayed path. If id is nil, all paths are removed.
  LMinimap:clearViewportRect( )  -> nil  -- Clears the viewport rectangle overlay.
  LMinimap:drawLine( x1, y1, x2, y2, color_tbl )  -> nil  -- Draws a custom line segment on the minimap overlay.
  LMinimap:drawRect( x, y, w, h, color_tbl )  -> nil  -- Draws a custom rectangle on the minimap overlay.
  LMinimap:drawToImage( pixel_size )  -> ImageData  -- Renders the minimap grid to a CPU ImageData.
  LMinimap:getCenter( )  -> number  -- Returns the center coordinates as x, y.
  LMinimap:getCenterX( )  -> number  -- Returns the center X coordinate.
  LMinimap:getCenterY( )  -> number  -- Returns the center Y coordinate.
  LMinimap:getColorMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the current color mode as a string.
  LMinimap:getDisplayHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the display height in pixels.
  LMinimap:getDisplaySize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the display width and height as two values.
  LMinimap:getDisplayWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the display width in pixels.
  LMinimap:getFogColor( )  -> number  -- Returns the fog overlay color as r, g, b, a.
  LMinimap:getFogLevel( x, y )  -> integer  -- Returns the fog level at a 1-based grid position (0=hidden, 1=explored, 2=visible).
  LMinimap:getGridHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid height in cells.
  LMinimap:getGridSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid width and height as two values.
  LMinimap:getGridWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid width in cells.
  LMinimap:getHoverInfo( sx, sy, mx, my )  -> string  -- Returns hover tooltip text for the element under screen coordinates, or nil.
  LMinimap:getLayer( )  -> integer  -- Returns the index of the currently active render layer.
  LMinimap:getMarkerCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of markers.
  LMinimap:getMarkerDescription( id )  -> string  -- Returns the description of a marker, or nil.
  LMinimap:getObjectCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of tracked objects.
  LMinimap:getObjectTypeCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of registered object types.
  LMinimap:getOwnerColor( owner )  -> number  -- Returns the display color for an owner/faction as r, g, b, a.
  LMinimap:getPingCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of active pings.
  LMinimap:getTerrain( x, y )  -> integer  -- Returns the terrain type at a 1-based grid position.
  LMinimap:getTerrainColor( terrain_type )  -> number  -- Returns the display color for a terrain type as r, g, b, a.
  LMinimap:getTileDescription( type_id )  -> string  -- Returns the hover tooltip string for a terrain type ID, or nil.
  LMinimap:getViewportColor( )  -> number  -- Returns the viewport rectangle color as r, g, b, a.
  LMinimap:getViewportRect( )  -> nil  -- Returns the viewport rectangle as x, y, w, h or nil if not set.
  LMinimap:getZoom( )  -> number  -- Returns the current zoom level.
  LMinimap:gridToScreen( gx, gy, mx, my )  -> number  -- Converts grid coordinates to screen coordinates.
  LMinimap:hasMarker( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a marker with the given ID exists.
  LMinimap:isAntiAlias( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether anti-aliasing is enabled.
  LMinimap:isClickable( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this minimap responds to click hit-testing.
  LMinimap:isFogEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether fog of war is enabled.
  LMinimap:isObjectTypeVisible( type_idx )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether an object type (1-based index) is visible.
  LMinimap:isViewportVisible( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the viewport rectangle is visible.
  LMinimap:removeMarker( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes the minimap marker with the given integer ID, if present.
  LMinimap:removeObject( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a tracked object by ID.
  LMinimap:render( [x], [y] )  -> nil  -- Renders the minimap to the screen at the given position.
  LMinimap:screenToGrid( sx, sy, mx, my )  -> number  -- Converts screen coordinates to grid coordinates.
  LMinimap:setAntiAlias( enabled )  -> nil  -- Sets whether anti-aliasing is enabled.
  LMinimap:setCenter( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the center of the minimap view in grid coordinates.
  LMinimap:setClickable( enabled )  -> nil  -- Sets whether this minimap responds to click hit-testing.
  LMinimap:setColorMode( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the color mode ("terrain" or "political").
  LMinimap:setDisplaySize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the display size in pixels.
  LMinimap:setFogColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -> nil  -- Sets the fog overlay color.
  LMinimap:setFogData( data )  -> nil  -- Sets the entire fog grid from a flat 1-based table (0=hidden, 1=explored, 2=visible).
  LMinimap:setFogEnabled( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables fog of war.
  LMinimap:setFogLevel( x, y, level )  -> nil  -- Sets the fog level at a 1-based grid position (0=hidden, 1=explored, 2=visible).
  LMinimap:setLayer( layer )  -> nil  -- Switches the minimap's active render layer (0-based index).
  LMinimap:setLayerData( layer, data_tbl )  -> nil  -- Stores tile data for a specific layer index.
  LMinimap:setMarkerAnimation( id, anim_type, speed )  -> nil  -- Attaches an animation to a marker. Does nothing if the ID does not exist.
  LMinimap:setObject( id, x, y, type_idx, [owner] )  -> nil  -- Sets or updates a tracked object on the minimap.
  LMinimap:setObjectTypeVisible( type_idx, visible )  -> nil  -- Sets whether an object type (1-based index) is visible.
  LMinimap:setOwnerColor( owner, r, g, b, [a] )  -> nil  -- Sets the display color for an owner/faction.
  LMinimap:setTerrain( x, y, terrain_type )  -> nil  -- Sets the terrain type at a 1-based grid position.
  LMinimap:setTerrainColor( terrain_type, r, g, b, [a] )  -> nil  -- Sets the display color for a terrain type.
  LMinimap:setTerrainData( data )  -> nil  -- Sets terrain types from a flat 1-based Lua table of integers (row-major).
  LMinimap:setTileDescription( type_id, desc )  -> nil  -- Sets a hover tooltip string for a terrain type ID.
  LMinimap:setViewportColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -> nil  -- Sets the viewport rectangle color.
  LMinimap:setViewportRect( x, y, w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the viewport rectangle overlay in grid coordinates.
  LMinimap:setViewportVisible( visible )  -> nil  -- Sets whether the viewport rectangle is visible.
  LMinimap:setZoom( zoom )  -> nil  -- Sets the zoom level (minimum 0.1).
  LMinimap:showPath( points_tbl, color_tbl )  -> nil  -- Displays a pathfinding route on the minimap and returns its path ID.
  LMinimap:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LMinimap:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LMinimap:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances time-based effects by dt seconds (expires pings).
```

## lurek.save {#save}

> Save/load game state: named slots, versioned tables, autosave.

```lua
  lurek.save.newSaveManager( )  -> LSaveManager  -- Creates a new SaveManager for slot-based save/load operations.
```

**`LSaveManager`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`SaveManager`] with per-module callback storage.

```lua
  LSaveManager:addMigration( from_ver, func )  -> nil  -- Registers a migration function for upgrading from a schema version.
  LSaveManager:collect( )  -> table  -- Collects data from all registered collectors into a table with metadata.
  LSaveManager:delete( slot )  -> nil  -- Deletes a save file for the given slot.
  LSaveManager:disableAutoSave( )  -> nil  -- Disables automatic periodic saving; manual `write()` calls still work.
  LSaveManager:enableAutoSave( interval, slot )  -> nil  -- Enables auto-save with a given interval and target slot.
  LSaveManager:exists( slot )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a save file exists for the given slot.
  LSaveManager:getSchemaVersion( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current schema version.
  LSaveManager:getSlotInfo( slot )  -> table  -- Returns metadata for a single slot, or nil if not found.
  LSaveManager:getSlots( )  -> table  -- Returns a list of all save slots with metadata.
  LSaveManager:getSummary( )  -> string  -- Returns the current summary string.
  LSaveManager:isCompressed( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether compression is currently enabled.
  LSaveManager:isDirty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether data has been modified since the last save or load.
  LSaveManager:load( slot )  -> boolean  -- Loads data from a slot file, applies migrations, and restores.
  LSaveManager:markDirty( )  -> nil  -- Marks data as modified since the last save or load.
  LSaveManager:onAfterLoad( func )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback that fires after every successful load operation.
  LSaveManager:onBeforeSave( func )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback that fires before every save operation.
  LSaveManager:register( name, collect_fn, restore_fn )  -> nil  -- Registers a named module with collector and restorer callbacks.
  LSaveManager:reset( )  -> nil  -- Resets all state, removing callbacks and clearing the manager.
  LSaveManager:restore( data )  -> nil  -- Restores data from a table, applying migrations and calling restorers.
  LSaveManager:save( slot )  -> nil  -- Collects data and writes it to a slot file.
  LSaveManager:setCompress( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables LZ4 compression for saved data.
  LSaveManager:setSchemaVersion( version )  -> nil  -- Sets the current schema version for new saves.
  LSaveManager:setSummary( summary )  -> nil  -- Sets the summary string included in save metadata.
  LSaveManager:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LSaveManager:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LSaveManager:unregister( name )  -> nil  -- Removes a named module and its callbacks.
  LSaveManager:update( dt )  -> string  -- Advances the auto-save timer and returns the slot name when a save should trigger.
```

```lua
  lurek.log.addSink( config )  -> integer  -- Creates and registers a new log output sink from the given configuration table.
  lurek.log.clearSinks( )  -> nil  -- Removes every registered log sink, returning the logging system to its default state wh...
  lurek.log.debug( message, [tag] )  -> nil  -- Emits a message at debug severity to the engine log and all registered sinks.
  lurek.log.debug_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -> nil  -- Emits a structured log message at debug severity with key-value metadata.
  lurek.log.error( message, [tag] )  -> nil  -- Emits a message at error severity to the engine log and all registered sinks.
  lurek.log.error_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -> nil  -- Emits a structured log message at error severity with key-value metadata.
  lurek.log.flushFile( id )  -> nil  -- Forces the operating system to write any buffered data for a file-type sink to disk.
  lurek.log.getLevel( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the current global minimum severity threshold as a lowercase string...
  lurek.log.info( message, [tag] )  -> nil  -- Emits a message at info severity to the engine log and all registered sinks.
  lurek.log.info_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -> nil  -- Emits a structured log message at info severity with key-value metadata.
  lurek.log.listSinks( )  -> table  -- Returns an array-like table where each entry is a table describing one registered sink.
  lurek.log.print( level, message, [tag] )  -> nil  -- Emits a log message at an arbitrary severity level specified as a string.
  lurek.log.readMemory( id, [drain] )  -> table  -- Reads log entries stored in a memory-type sink.
  lurek.log.removeSink( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a previously registered log sink by its numeric identifier.
  lurek.log.setLevel( level )  -> nil  -- Sets the global minimum severity threshold for the engine log backend.
  lurek.log.struct( level_str, message, fields_tbl )  -> nil  -- Emits a structured log message that includes arbitrary key-value metadata alongside the...
  lurek.log.warn( message, [tag] )  -> nil  -- Emits a message at warning severity to the engine log and all registered sinks.
  lurek.log.warn_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -> nil  -- Emits a structured log message at warning severity with key-value metadata.
```

## lurek.mods {#mods}

> Mod loading: folder scanning, dependency resolution, hot-reload.

```lua
  lurek.mods.checkApiVersion( mod_ud, host_version )  -> boolean  -- Checks whether a mod's required `api_version` is compatible with the given `host_version`.
  lurek.mods.newMod( info )  -> LMod  -- Creates a new Mod from an info table with at least an `id` field.
  lurek.mods.newModManager( )  -> LModManager  -- Creates a new empty ModManager.
  lurek.mods.newRegistry( )  -> LContentRegistry  -- Creates a new empty ContentRegistry for mod-contributed assets.
```

**`LContentRegistry`** methods:

> A typed content registry for mod-contributed assets and objects.

```lua
  LContentRegistry:get( type_name, id )  -> table  -- Retrieves a content entry.
  LContentRegistry:getAll( type_name )  -> table  -- Returns all entries for a type.
  LContentRegistry:getTypes( )  -> table  -- Returns all registered type names.
  LContentRegistry:register( type_name, id, obj )  -> nil  -- Registers a content entry.
  LContentRegistry:registerType( type_name )  -> nil  -- Registers a new content type.
  LContentRegistry:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LContentRegistry:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LMod`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`ModInfo`] with per-mod hook and config storage.

```lua
  LMod:getApiVersion( )  -> string  -- Returns the required engine API version string when one is set.
  LMod:getAuthor( )  -> string  -- Returns the author name string from this mod's metadata manifest.
  LMod:getCapabilities( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of declared capability flags.
  LMod:getConfig( )  -> table  -- Returns the stored config value.
  LMod:getConfigSchema( )  -> table  -- Returns the config schema as an array of `{key, type, default}` tables.
  LMod:getDependencies( )  -> table  -- Returns the list of required mod IDs.
  LMod:getDescription( )  -> string  -- Returns the mod description.
  LMod:getHook( name )  -> function  -- Returns the hook function for the given name.
  LMod:getHookNames( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of registered hook names.
  LMod:getId( )  -> string  -- Returns the unique mod identifier.
  LMod:getName( )  -> string  -- Returns the localized or human-readable display name of the mod.
  LMod:getPriority( )  -> integer  -- Returns the load-order priority.
  LMod:getVersion( )  -> string  -- Returns the version string.
  LMod:hasHook( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a hook with the given name exists.
  LMod:isEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the mod is enabled.
  LMod:isLoaded( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the mod has been loaded.
  LMod:releaseRefs( )  -> nil  -- Releases all hook and config registry references.
  LMod:setApiVersion( api_version )  -> nil  -- Sets the required engine API version string.
  LMod:setCapabilities( caps )  -> nil  -- Replaces the capability list with the given array of strings.
  LMod:setConfig( value )  -> nil  -- Stores an arbitrary config value for this mod.
  LMod:setConfigSchema( schema )  -> nil  -- Replaces the config schema with the given array of `{key, type, default}` tables.
  LMod:setEnabled( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables this mod.
  LMod:setHook( name, func )  -> nil  -- Registers a named hook callback, replacing any existing one.
  LMod:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LMod:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LModManager`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`ModManager`].

```lua
  LModManager:clearLoadOrder( )  -> nil  -- Clears the custom load order.
  LModManager:clearReloadQueue( )  -> nil  -- Clears the reload queue without reloading.
  LModManager:getAllMods( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of info tables for all registered mods.
  LModManager:getLoadOrder( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of info tables in effective load order.
  LModManager:getModCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of registered mods.
  LModManager:getModPath( mod_id )  -> string  -- Returns the filesystem path of a registered mod.
  LModManager:getReloadQueue( )  -> table  -- Returns the array of mod IDs pending hot-reload.
  LModManager:hasCircularDependencies( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether any circular dependency cycles exist.
  LModManager:hasMod( mod_id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a mod with the given ID is registered.
  LModManager:markForReload( mod_id )  -> boolean  -- Marks a registered mod for hot-reload.
  LModManager:registerMod( ud )  -> nil  -- Registers a mod from its mod userdata.
  LModManager:scanFolder( path )  -> table  -- Scans a directory for mods with `mod.toml` and registers them.
  LModManager:setLoadOrder( order_table )  -> nil  -- Sets an explicit load order from an array of mod ID strings.
  LModManager:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LModManager:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LModManager:unregisterMod( mod_id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a mod by ID and returns whether it was found.
  LModManager:validateDependencies( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of mod IDs with missing dependencies.
```

## lurek.i18n {#i18n}

> Localisation: string lookup, locale switching, plural forms.

```lua
  lurek.i18n.buildIndex( )  -> table  -- Builds an inverted word index for the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.categories( )  -> table  -- Returns unique first-path-segment category prefixes for all active locale keys.
  lurek.i18n.formatDate( timestamp, [fmt] )  -> string  -- Formats a Unix timestamp according to the active locale's date order.
  lurek.i18n.formatNumber( n, [opts] )  -> string  -- Formats a number with locale-aware decimal and thousands separators.
  lurek.i18n.getAvailableLanguages( )  -> table  -- Returns all loaded locale codes.
  lurek.i18n.getBase( )  -> string  -- Returns the base fallback language.
  lurek.i18n.getFallbacks( )  -> table  -- Returns the current fallback locale array.
  lurek.i18n.getKeys( )  -> table  -- Returns all known keys for the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.getLanguage( )  -> string  -- Returns the currently active locale code.
  lurek.i18n.getLanguages( )  -> table  -- Returns all loaded locale codes.
  lurek.i18n.getLoadedLocales( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of all currently loaded locale codes.
  lurek.i18n.hasKey( key )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a key exists in the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.hasLanguage( locale )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a locale has been loaded.
  lurek.i18n.interpolate( template, vars )  -> string  -- Interpolates `{name}` placeholders in a template string.
  lurek.i18n.keyCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of keys loaded in the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.keysInCategory( category )  -> table  -- Returns all keys in the active locale whose first path segment matches the category.
  lurek.i18n.loadTable( locale, tbl )  -> nil  -- Loads a language table under the given locale code.
  lurek.i18n.mergeLocale( locale, entries )  -> nil  -- Merges a flat key-value table into an existing locale without replacing the whole table.
  lurek.i18n.offChange( )  -> nil  -- Unregisters all language-change callbacks.
  lurek.i18n.onChange( cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback invoked when `setLanguage()` is called.
  lurek.i18n.onLanguageChange( cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback invoked when `setLanguage()` is called.
  lurek.i18n.pluralFor( n )  -> string  -- Returns the CLDR plural category for a number.
  lurek.i18n.search( query, [limit] )  -> table  -- Searches active locale values for a case-insensitive substring query.
  lurek.i18n.searchIndexed( index, query, [limit] )  -> table  -- Searches the provided pre-built index for entries matching all words in the query.
  lurek.i18n.setBase( locale )  -> nil  -- Sets the base fallback language.
  lurek.i18n.setFallbacks( locales )  -> nil  -- Sets the ordered list of fallback locale codes tried when a key is missing.
  lurek.i18n.setKey( locale, key, value )  -> nil  -- Inserts or overwrites a single key in the given locale.
  lurek.i18n.setLanguage( locale )  -> nil  -- Sets the active translation language.
  lurek.i18n.t( key, [vars], [count] )  -> string  -- Translates a key against the active locale with optional interpolation and pluralization.
  lurek.i18n.tGender( key, gender, [vars] )  -> string  -- Looks up a translation key augmented with a gender suffix.
  lurek.i18n.unloadTable( locale )  -> boolean  -- Unloads a locale from the catalog.
```

## lurek.input {#input}

> Unified input helper: combined keyboard + gamepad queries.

```lua
  lurek.input.advancePlayback( )  -> table  -- Advances playback by one frame and returns that frame's input events.
  lurek.input.bind( action, keys )  -> nil  -- Maps an action name to one or more key or button names.
  lurek.input.clearBindings( )  -> nil  -- Removes all action bindings.
  lurek.input.getAxis( id, axis )  -> number  -- Returns the current value (-1 to 1) of a gamepad analog axis.
  lurek.input.getAxisCount( id )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of analog axes on the gamepad.
  lurek.input.getBackgroundEvents( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether background gamepad events are enabled.
  lurek.input.getBindings( )  -> table  -- Returns a table mapping each action name to its bound keys.
  lurek.input.getButtonCount( id )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of buttons on the gamepad.
  lurek.input.getCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of connected gamepads.
  lurek.input.getCursor( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the currently active system cursor.
  lurek.input.getGUID( id )  -> string  -- Returns the hardware GUID string of the gamepad.
  lurek.input.getGamepadMappingString( guid )  -> string  -- Returns the stored mapping string for the given GUID, or nil.
  lurek.input.getHat( id, hat )  -> string  -- Returns the direction string of a hat switch on the gamepad.
  lurek.input.getJoystickCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of tracked gamepad slots.
  lurek.input.getJoysticks( )  -> table  -- Returns a list of connected gamepad IDs.
  lurek.input.getKeyFromScancode( scancode )  -> string  -- Returns the key name for the given hardware scancode.
  lurek.input.getName( id )  -> string  -- Returns the human-readable name of a gamepad.
  lurek.input.getPlaybackFrame( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current playback frame index.
  lurek.input.getPosition( )  -> number  -- Returns the current cursor position as (x, y).
  lurek.input.getPosition( id )  -> number  -- Returns the position (x, y) of the touch with the given ID.
  lurek.input.getPressure( id )  -> number  -- Returns the pressure (0-1) of the touch with the given ID.
  lurek.input.getRelativeMode( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether relative mouse mode is active.
  lurek.input.getScancodeFromKey( key )  -> string  -- Returns the hardware scancode for the given key name.
  lurek.input.getSystemCursor( name )  -> LCursor  -- Returns a system cursor object for the named cursor shape.
  lurek.input.getTouchCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of currently active touch points.
  lurek.input.getTouches( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of active touch points with id, x, y, and pressure fields.
  lurek.input.getWheelDelta( )  -> number  -- Returns the mouse scroll wheel delta (dx, dy) since last frame.
  lurek.input.getX( )  -> number  -- Returns the current mouse X position in window coordinates.
  lurek.input.getY( )  -> number  -- Returns the current mouse Y position in window coordinates.
  lurek.input.hasKeyRepeat( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether key-repeat is currently enabled.
  lurek.input.hasTextInput( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether text input mode is currently active.
  lurek.input.isActionDown( action )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if any key bound to the action is currently held down.
  lurek.input.isConnected( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the gamepad with the given ID is connected.
  lurek.input.isCursorSupported( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether cursor customisation is supported on this platform.
  lurek.input.isDown( args )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if any of the given keys is currently held down.
  lurek.input.isDown( button )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given mouse button is currently held down.
  lurek.input.isDown( id, button )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given button on the gamepad is currently held.
  lurek.input.isGamepad( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the joystick at the given slot is a recognized gamepad.
  lurek.input.isGrabbed( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the mouse cursor is locked to the window.
  lurek.input.isModifierActive( modifier )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the named modifier key is currently held.
  lurek.input.isPlayingBack( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if input playback is currently active.
  lurek.input.isRecording( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if input recording is currently active.
  lurek.input.isScancodeDown( scancode )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the key with the given scancode is held.
  lurek.input.isVibrationSupported( id )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the gamepad supports haptic vibration.
  lurek.input.isVisible( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the mouse cursor is currently visible.
  lurek.input.loadGamepadMappings( path )  -> integer  -- Loads SDL2 GameControllerDB-format mappings from a file.
  lurek.input.loadRecording( json )  -> nil  -- Loads a JSON-encoded recording string for playback.
  lurek.input.newCombo( steps_val, [opts] )  -> LCombo  -- Creates a new combo detector from an ordered list of steps.
  lurek.input.newCursor( )  -> LCursor  -- Creates a custom mouse cursor from RGBA pixel data.
  lurek.input.saveGamepadMappings( path )  -> nil  -- Saves all stored gamepad mappings to a plain-text file.
  lurek.input.setBackgroundEvents( enable )  -> nil  -- Enable or disable receiving gamepad events when the window is not focused.
  lurek.input.setCursor( cursor_val )  -> nil  -- Sets the active mouse cursor from a Cursor handle, name string, or nil to reset.
  lurek.input.setGamepadMapping( guid, mapping )  -> nil  -- Stores or replaces the SDL2 GameControllerDB mapping string for the given GUID.
  lurek.input.setGrabbed( grabbed )  -> nil  -- Locks or unlocks the mouse cursor to the window.
  lurek.input.setKeyRepeat( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables key-repeat events.
  lurek.input.setPosition( x, y )  -> nil  -- Moves the mouse cursor to the given window-space position.
  lurek.input.setRelativeMode( relative )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables raw relative mouse motion mode.
  lurek.input.setTextInput( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables Unicode text input mode.
  lurek.input.setVibration( ... )  -> boolean  -- Triggers haptic rumble (currently a no-op stub).
  lurek.input.setVisible( visible )  -> nil  -- Shows or hides the operating-system mouse cursor.
  lurek.input.startPlayback( )  -> nil  -- Starts playback from the beginning of the loaded recording.
  lurek.input.startRecording( )  -> nil  -- Starts capturing input events frame by frame.
  lurek.input.stopPlayback( )  -> nil  -- Stops playback immediately.
  lurek.input.stopRecording( )  -> LInputRecording  -- Stops recording and returns the captured recording handle.
  lurek.input.unbind( action )  -> boolean  -- Removes all key bindings for the given action name.
  lurek.input.vibrate( id, low_freq, high_freq, duration_ms )  -> boolean  -- Requests haptic vibration on a gamepad.
  lurek.input.wasActionPressed( action )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if any key bound to the action was pressed this frame.
  lurek.input.wasActionPressedWithin( action, frames )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the action was pressed within the last frame window.
  lurek.input.wasActionReleased( action )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if any key bound to the action was released this frame.
```

**`LCombo`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for a [`ComboDetector`] with an integrated millisecond clock.

```lua
  LCombo:feed( key )  -> string  -- Feeds a key-press event into the combo detector.
  LCombo:getStep( index )  -> table  -- Returns the step at the given 1-based index as `{key=..., gap_ms=...}`.
  LCombo:isInProgress( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the detector is currently mid-sequence.
  LCombo:progress( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of steps matched so far (0 when idle).
  LCombo:reset( )  -> nil  -- Reset the detector to its initial idle state, cancelling any in-progress sequence.
  LCombo:tick( dt )  -> string  -- Advances the combo clock and checks for timeouts.
  LCombo:totalSteps( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of steps in the combo sequence.
  LCombo:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LCombo:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LCursor`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a mouse cursor handle.

```lua
  LCursor:getType( )  -> string  -- Returns the cursor type as "system" or "custom".
  LCursor:release( )  -> nil  -- Releases the cursor resource (no-op on desktop).
  LCursor:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LCursor:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LInputRecording`** methods:

> Lua userdata wrapper for a completed [`crate::input::recorder::InputRecording`].

```lua
  LInputRecording:frameCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of sparse event frames stored in this recording.
  LInputRecording:toJson( )  -> string  -- Serializes this recording to a JSON string for saving to disk.
  LInputRecording:totalFrames( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total frame count when recording was stopped.
  LInputRecording:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LInputRecording:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.animation {#animation}

> `lurek.animation` - Sprite animation with named clips, blending, state machines, and Aseprite import.

```lua
  lurek.animation.fromAseprite( json_str )  -> Animation  -- Parses an Aseprite JSON export string and builds an animation.
  lurek.animation.new( )  -> Animation  -- Creates a new, empty Animation controller.
  lurek.animation.newBlendLayerSet( )  -> BlendLayerSet  -- Creates a new empty blend layer set for compositing multiple animation clips.
  lurek.animation.newCurve( )  -> AnimCurve  -- Creates a new empty animation curve with linear interpolation.
  lurek.animation.newStateMachine( anim_ud, initial )  -> AnimStateMachine  -- Creates an animation FSM from an Animation controller and an initial state name.
  lurek.animation.newSyncGroup( )  -> AnimSyncGroup  -- Creates a new empty animation sync group.
```

**`LAnimCurve`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`AnimCurve`].

```lua
  LAnimCurve:addKeyframe( t, v )  -> nil  -- Inserts or replaces a keyframe at the given time.
  LAnimCurve:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all keyframes from this animation curve, resetting it to empty.
  LAnimCurve:eval( t )  -> number  -- Returns the interpolated curve value at the given time.
  LAnimCurve:keyframeCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of keyframes currently stored.
  LAnimCurve:setCustomEasing( func )  -> nil  -- Sets or clears a custom Lua easing function for this curve.
  LAnimCurve:setEasing( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the easing kind applied between all keyframe segments.
  LAnimCurve:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LAnimCurve:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LAnimStateMachine`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`AnimStateMachine`] FSM controller.

```lua
  LAnimStateMachine:addState( name, clip, looping )  -> nil  -- Registers a new named state that plays a clip from the embedded animation.
  LAnimStateMachine:addTransition( from_state, to_state, condition )  -> nil  -- Adds a conditional transition between two states using a condition string like "speed >...
  LAnimStateMachine:forceState( name )  -> boolean  -- Immediately jumps to the named state, bypassing transition conditions.
  LAnimStateMachine:getQuad( )  -> table  -- Returns the source quad for the current animation frame.
  LAnimStateMachine:getState( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the currently active state.
  LAnimStateMachine:setParam( name, value )  -> nil  -- Sets an FSM parameter value (number, boolean, or integer supported).
  LAnimStateMachine:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LAnimStateMachine:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LAnimStateMachine:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the FSM by `dt` seconds, evaluating transitions.
```

**`LAnimSyncGroup`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`AnimSyncGroup`].

```lua
  LAnimSyncGroup:add( handle )  -> nil  -- Adds an animation handle to the group.
  LAnimSyncGroup:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all animation handles from the group.
  LAnimSyncGroup:memberCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of animations currently in the group.
  LAnimSyncGroup:remove( handle )  -> nil  -- Removes an animation handle from the group.
  LAnimSyncGroup:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LAnimSyncGroup:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LAnimation`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`Animation`] controller.

```lua
  LAnimation:addClip( name, indices_tbl, fps, looping )  -> nil  -- Adds a named clip from explicit frame indices.
  LAnimation:addClipFromGrid( )  -> nil  -- Adds a named clip sliced from a sprite-sheet grid.
  LAnimation:addFrame( x, y, w, h )  -> integer  -- Adds a single frame to the frame pool by source rectangle.
  LAnimation:addFramesFromGrid( tw, th, fw, fh, start, count )  -> integer  -- Slices a sprite-sheet grid into frames and appends them.
  LAnimation:crossfade( clip_name, duration )  -> boolean  -- Begins a smooth crossfade from the current clip to a new named clip.
  LAnimation:drawToImage( w, h )  -> ImageData  -- Renders the current animation frame into a new ImageData (white bg, blue frame rect).
  LAnimation:getBlendState( )  -> table  -- Returns the active crossfade state.
  LAnimation:getClip( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the currently playing clip.
  LAnimation:getClipCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of registered clips.
  LAnimation:getCurrentFrame( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current position within the active clip (0-based).
  LAnimation:getFrameCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of frames in the frame pool.
  LAnimation:getQuad( )  -> table  -- Returns the source quad for the current frame.
  LAnimation:getSpeed( )  -> number  -- Returns the playback speed multiplier.
  LAnimation:isLooping( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the current clip is set to loop.
  LAnimation:isPlaying( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a clip is currently playing.
  LAnimation:pause( )  -> nil  -- Pauses playback at the current frame.
  LAnimation:play( name )  -> boolean  -- Starts playback of the named clip.
  LAnimation:pollEvents( )  -> table  -- Drains and returns all pending animation events as a table.
  LAnimation:resume( )  -> nil  -- Resumes playback from the current frame.
  LAnimation:setFrame( index )  -> nil  -- Sets the playback position within the current clip.
  LAnimation:setSpeed( speed )  -> nil  -- Sets the playback speed multiplier.
  LAnimation:stop( )  -> nil  -- Stops playback and resets to frame 0.
  LAnimation:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LAnimation:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LAnimation:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the animation by dt seconds.
```

**`LBlendLayerSet`** methods:

```lua
  LBlendLayerSet:addLayer( name, clip_name, weight, [bones] )  -> boolean  -- Appends a new blend layer.
  LBlendLayerSet:getWeight( name )  -> number  -- Returns the blend weight of a named layer.
  LBlendLayerSet:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of blend layers.
  LBlendLayerSet:listLayers( )  -> table  -- Returns an ordered array of layer info tables: {name, clip_name, weight, bones}.
  LBlendLayerSet:removeLayer( name )  -> boolean  -- Removes a blend layer by name.
  LBlendLayerSet:setMask( name, bones )  -> boolean  -- Replaces the bone mask of a layer.
  LBlendLayerSet:setWeight( name, weight )  -> boolean  -- Sets the blend weight of a named layer (clamped to [0, 1]).
  LBlendLayerSet:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LBlendLayerSet:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.automation {#automation}

> `lurek.automation` - Automated input simulation via timed step scripts.

```lua
  lurek.automation.getCurrentScript( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the active script.
  lurek.automation.getCurrentStep( )  -> integer  -- Returns the index of the next step to be dispatched.
  lurek.automation.getElapsedTime( )  -> number  -- Returns seconds elapsed since playback started.
  lurek.automation.getPlaybackSpeed( )  -> number  -- Returns the current playback speed multiplier (default 1.0).
  lurek.automation.getScripts( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of all registered script names.
  lurek.automation.getStepCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of steps in the active script.
  lurek.automation.getStepLimit( name )  -> integer  -- Returns the step limit for the named script.
  lurek.automation.hasMacro( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a macro with the given name has been saved.
  lurek.automation.hasScript( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a script with the given name is registered.
  lurek.automation.isComplete( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if all steps in the active script have been dispatched.
  lurek.automation.isHighlightMode( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the highlight overlay hint is active.
  lurek.automation.isPaused( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if playback is currently paused.
  lurek.automation.isRunning( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the simulator is actively playing a script.
  lurek.automation.listMacros( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of all saved macro names.
  lurek.automation.load( name, data )  -> nil  -- Loads a named script from a Lua data table containing a steps array.
  lurek.automation.loadFromToml( name, toml_str )  -> nil  -- Parses a TOML string and registers it as a named script.
  lurek.automation.pause( )  -> nil  -- Pauses playback at the current step position.
  lurek.automation.playMacro( name )  -> nil  -- Loads and starts playback of a previously saved macro.
  lurek.automation.resume( )  -> nil  -- Resumes playback from a paused position.
  lurek.automation.saveMacro( macro_name, script_name )  -> nil  -- Saves a loaded script under a macro name for fast replay.
  lurek.automation.setHighlightMode( enable )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the highlight overlay hint.
  lurek.automation.setPlaybackSpeed( factor )  -> nil  -- Sets the playback speed multiplier.
  lurek.automation.setStepLimit( name, n )  -> boolean  -- Sets the step limit for the named script.
  lurek.automation.start( name )  -> nil  -- Starts playback of the named script from the beginning.
  lurek.automation.stop( )  -> nil  -- Stops playback and resets the simulator to idle.
  lurek.automation.unload( name )  -> boolean  -- Removes a loaded script by name, returning true if it existed.
  lurek.automation.update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the playback clock by `dt` seconds.
  lurek.automation.waitUntil( predicate, timeout )  -> nil  -- Pauses playback advancement until a predicate returns true or a timeout expires.
```

## lurek.debugbridge {#debugbridge}

> `lurek.debugbridge` - TCP debug server bindings for runtime inspection and control.

```lua
  lurek.debugbridge.broadcast( event, json_data )  -> nil  -- Broadcasts a JSON event to all connected clients.
  lurek.debugbridge.capturePrint( msg, [source], [line] )  -> nil  -- Captures a print message and broadcasts it to connected clients.
  lurek.debugbridge.clearPrintHistory( )  -> nil  -- Clears the print history.
  lurek.debugbridge.getClientCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of connected TCP clients.
  lurek.debugbridge.getPerformance( )  -> table  -- Returns performance statistics.
  lurek.debugbridge.getPort( )  -> integer  -- Returns the server port (0 if not running).
  lurek.debugbridge.getPrintHistory( [count] )  -> table  -- Returns the print history.
  lurek.debugbridge.isRunning( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the server is currently running.
  lurek.debugbridge.isScreenshotRequested( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a screenshot is currently requested.
  lurek.debugbridge.poll( )  -> nil  -- Poll for pending Lua-dependent requests from TCP clients.
  lurek.debugbridge.requestScreenshot( [scale] )  -> nil  -- Flags a screenshot request for the next frame.
  lurek.debugbridge.setMaxPrintHistory( max )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum print history size.
  lurek.debugbridge.start( [port] )  -> boolean  -- Start the TCP debug server on 127.0.0.1:port.
  lurek.debugbridge.stop( )  -> nil  -- Stop the TCP debug server and close all connections.
```

## lurek.devtools {#devtools}

> `lurek.devtools` - Runtime diagnostics and developer tools.

```lua
  lurek.devtools.clearLog( )  -> nil  -- Discards all accumulated log entries from the in-memory devtools log buffer.
  lurek.devtools.clearWatches( )  -> nil  -- Clears all watched paths.
  lurek.devtools.debug( message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at DEBUG level.
  lurek.devtools.error( message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at ERROR level.
  lurek.devtools.eval( code )  -> boolean  -- Evaluates a Lua string and returns (success, results...).
  lurek.devtools.exposeWatch( name, getter, [category] )  -> integer  -- Registers a named live watch. The getter function is called on demand to sample a value.
  lurek.devtools.fatal( message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at FATAL level.
  lurek.devtools.getCallStack( [max_depth] )  -> table  -- Returns the Lua call stack as a table of frames.
  lurek.devtools.getFrameHistory( )  -> table  -- Returns the raw frame-time sample array.
  lurek.devtools.getFrameHistorySize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the current frame-history buffer capacity.
  lurek.devtools.getFrameStats( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of computed frame statistics.
  lurek.devtools.getLogConsole( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether console log output is enabled.
  lurek.devtools.getLogFile( )  -> string  -- Returns the current log file path.
  lurek.devtools.getLogHistory( [count] )  -> table  -- Returns recent log entries as an array of tables.
  lurek.devtools.getLogLevel( )  -> string  -- Returns the current minimum log level.
  lurek.devtools.getProfileData( [frame] )  -> table  -- Returns zone data table for a specific frame (0 or nil = most recent).
  lurek.devtools.getProfileFrameCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of retained profile frames.
  lurek.devtools.getWatchInterval( )  -> number  -- Returns the file watch poll interval in seconds.
  lurek.devtools.getWatchedPaths( )  -> table  -- Returns an array of all watched paths.
  lurek.devtools.getWatches( )  -> table  -- Calls all registered watch getters and returns a table of {name, category, value} records.
  lurek.devtools.info( message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at INFO level.
  lurek.devtools.isConsoleOpen( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the console is considered open.
  lurek.devtools.isProfilingEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the profiler is enabled.
  lurek.devtools.log( level, message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at the given level.
  lurek.devtools.newFileWatcher( path )  -> FileWatcher  -- Creates a standalone per-path file watcher. Call `:check()` once per frame
  lurek.devtools.newRepl( [max_history] )  -> ReplConsole  -- Creates an interactive Lua REPL console with a bounded history buffer.
  lurek.devtools.openConsole( )  -> boolean  -- Opens the console window (updates the console flag; returns true).
  lurek.devtools.profileFrame( )  -> nil  -- Seals the current frame of profiling data.
  lurek.devtools.profilePop( [] )  -> nil  -- Closes the most recent profiling zone.
  lurek.devtools.profilePush( name )  -> nil  -- Opens a named profiling zone on the stack.
  lurek.devtools.profilerReport( )  -> table  -- Returns a flat summary table of all recorded profiler zones across all stored
  lurek.devtools.recordFrameTime( dt_val )  -> nil  -- Records a frame-time sample (call each frame with delta time in seconds).
  lurek.devtools.removeWatch( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a watch by the id returned from exposeWatch. Returns true if removed.
  lurek.devtools.resetProfile( )  -> nil  -- Clears all profiling data and resets the zone stack.
  lurek.devtools.scan( )  -> table  -- Polls all watched paths and returns paths whose mtime changed.
  lurek.devtools.setFrameHistorySize( size )  -> nil  -- Sets the frame-history buffer capacity (clamped 10-10000).
  lurek.devtools.setLogConsole( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables console log output.
  lurek.devtools.setLogFile( path )  -> nil  -- Sets the log file path (empty string disables file output).
  lurek.devtools.setLogLevel( level )  -> nil  -- Sets the minimum log level.
  lurek.devtools.setProfilingEnabled( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the profiler.
  lurek.devtools.setWatchInterval( interval )  -> nil  -- Sets the file watch poll interval in seconds.
  lurek.devtools.snapshot( )  -> table  -- Takes a structured snapshot of all watches + frame stats + last profile frame.
  lurek.devtools.trace( message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at TRACE level.
  lurek.devtools.unwatch( path )  -> boolean  -- Removes a file path from the watch list.
  lurek.devtools.warn( message )  -> nil  -- Logs a message at WARN level.
  lurek.devtools.watch( path )  -> boolean  -- Adds a file path to the watch list. Returns false if already watched.
```

```lua
  LFileWatcher:getPath( )  -> string  -- Returns the watched path string.
```

```lua
  LPostFxEffect:setRadius( v )  -> nil  -- Sets the radius parameter of this effect.
  LPostFxEffect:setSaturation( v )  -> nil  -- Sets the saturation parameter of this effect.
  LPostFxEffect:setScanlineStrength( v )  -> nil  -- Sets the scanline strength parameter of this effect.
  LPostFxEffect:setStrength( v )  -> nil  -- Sets the strength parameter of this effect.
  LPostFxEffect:setThreshold( v )  -> nil  -- Sets the threshold parameter of this effect.
  LPostFxEffect:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LPostFxEffect:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the given name matches this object or a parent type.
```

**`LPostFxStack`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`PostFxStack`].

```lua
  LPostFxStack:add( effect_ud )  -> nil  -- Appends a PostFxEffect to the end of the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:apply( )  -> nil  -- Applies all enabled effects in the stack and composites the result to the screen.
  LPostFxStack:beginCapture( )  -> nil  -- Begins capturing the scene for post-processing.
  LPostFxStack:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all effects from the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:clearFeedback( )  -> nil  -- Resets the feedback intensity to `0.0` (disables feedback).
  LPostFxStack:dedup( )  -> integer  -- Removes duplicate effects from the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:endCapture( )  -> nil  -- Ends scene capture for post-processing.
  LPostFxStack:getDimensions( )  -> integer  -- Returns width and height of the render target.
  LPostFxStack:getEffect( index )  -> LPostFxEffect  -- Returns the effect at the given 1-based position, or nil.
  LPostFxStack:getEffectCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of effects in the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:getEnabledEffects( )  -> table  -- Returns a list of currently enabled effect objects.
  LPostFxStack:getFeedback( )  -> number  -- Returns the current feedback loop intensity `[0.0, 1.0]`.
  LPostFxStack:getHeight( )  -> integer  -- Returns the height of the render target.
  LPostFxStack:getWidth( )  -> integer  -- Returns the width of the render target.
  LPostFxStack:insert( position, effect_ud )  -> nil  -- Inserts a PostFxEffect at a specific 1-based position in the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:isCapturing( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the stack is currently capturing the scene.
  LPostFxStack:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the pipeline has no effect slots.
  LPostFxStack:isEnabled( position )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the effect at the given 1-based position is enabled.
  LPostFxStack:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of effect slots in the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:remove( effect_ud )  -> boolean  -- Removes the given PostFxEffect from the pipeline.
  LPostFxStack:resize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Resizes the render target to the given dimensions.
  LPostFxStack:setEnabled( position, enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the effect at the given 1-based position.
  LPostFxStack:setFeedback( factor )  -> nil  -- Sets the feedback loop intensity between `0.0` and `1.0`.
  LPostFxStack:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LPostFxStack:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the given name matches this object or a parent type.
```

**`LScreenTransition`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`crate::effect::ScreenTransition`].

```lua
  LScreenTransition:color( )  -> number  -- Returns the fill color as four numbers: `r, g, b, a`.
  LScreenTransition:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true while the transition is running.
  LScreenTransition:isDone( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true after the transition has completed.
  LScreenTransition:kind( )  -> string  -- Returns the transition kind name.
  LScreenTransition:play( )  -> nil  -- Starts the transition playing forward (scene fades/wipes out).
  LScreenTransition:progress( )  -> number  -- Returns the fractional progress of the transition.
  LScreenTransition:reverse( )  -> nil  -- Starts the transition in reverse (scene fades/wipes in).
  LScreenTransition:setColor( )  -> nil  -- Updates the fill color from `{r, g, b, a?}`.
  LScreenTransition:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LScreenTransition:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type name or a parent type.
  LScreenTransition:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the transition by `dt` seconds.
```

## lurek.engine {#engine}

```lua
  lurek.engine.fps( )  -> number  -- Returns the current measured frames-per-second.
  lurek.engine.frameCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of frames processed since engine start.
  lurek.engine.getFrameBudget( )  -> number  -- Returns the target frame budget in milliseconds (default: 1000 / 60 ~ 16.667 ms).
  lurek.engine.getResourceStats( )  -> table  -- Returns a table with resident resource memory statistics.
  lurek.engine.getVersion( )  -> string  -- Returns the engine version string (from `Cargo.toml`).
  lurek.engine.isDebug( )  -> boolean  -- Returns `true` if the engine was compiled in debug mode.

  lurek.engine.platform( )  -> string  -- Returns the host operating system name.
  lurek.engine.setResourceBudget( budget_bytes )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum resident texture memory budget in bytes.
  lurek.engine.uptime( )  -> number  -- Returns the total engine uptime in seconds (sum of all processed deltas).
```

## lurek.globe {#globe}

> `lurek.globe` - Geoscape globe simulation, province data, and world map helpers.

```lua
  lurek.globe.get( name )  -> LGlobe  -- Get an existing globe by name, or nil.
  lurek.globe.greatCircleDistance( la, lo, lb, lo2 )  -> number  -- Great-circle distance between two lat/lon points (in unit-sphere radians).
  lurek.globe.greatCirclePath( la, lo, lb, lo2, n )  -> table  -- Great-circle path as a table of {lat, lon} pairs.
  lurek.globe.latLonToUnit( lat, lon )  -> table  -- Convert lat/lon (degrees) to a unit-sphere Cartesian vector {x, y, z}.
  lurek.globe.loadFromTOML( name, toml_src, [spec_tbl] )  -> LGlobe  -- Load provinces from a TOML string and create a globe.
  lurek.globe.new( name, [spec_tbl] )  -> LGlobe  -- Creates a new globe instance with default settings and empty collections.
```

**`LGlobe`** methods:

> Lua-accessible handle to a `Globe` inside a `GlobeRegistry`.

```lua
  LGlobe:addArc( lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2, [steps] )  -> integer  -- Add an arc (great-circle path between two lat/lon points).

  LGlobe:addMarker( mtype, lat, lon, [label] )  -> integer  -- Add a marker. Returns marker ID.
  LGlobe:addProvince( p )  -> boolean  -- Adds a province from a table with id, centroid, vertices, neighbors, and base_color fie...
  LGlobe:findPath( from_id, to_id )  -> table  -- Find the shortest province path from `from_id` to `to_id`.
  LGlobe:getCamera( )  -> number  -- Get the current camera (lat, lon, zoom).
  LGlobe:getLod( )  -> string  -- Returns the current LOD tier as a string: "far", "mid", or "near".
  LGlobe:getMarkerAttr( id, key )  -> string  -- Get a string attribute from a marker.
  LGlobe:getName( )  -> string  -- Returns the string identifier name assigned to this globe instance.
  LGlobe:getNeighbors( id )  -> table  -- Returns the neighbor IDs of a province.
  LGlobe:getProvinceAttr( id, key )  -> string  -- Gets a string attribute from a province.
  LGlobe:getTimeOfDay( )  -> number  -- Gets the current simulated time of day for daylight computation.
  LGlobe:hideProvince( viewer, id )  -> nil  -- Hide a province for a viewer.
  LGlobe:isVisible( viewer, id )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the province is visible to the viewer.
  LGlobe:moveMarker( id, lat, lon )  -> nil  -- Move a marker to a new lat/lon.
  LGlobe:pan( dlat, dlon )  -> nil  -- Pan the orbit camera by delta-latitude and delta-longitude (degrees).
  LGlobe:pick( sx, sy )  -> integer  -- Returns the province ID under screen coordinates, or nil.
  LGlobe:pickLatLon( sx, sy )  -> number  -- Returns (lat, lon) of the screen point on the globe surface, or nil.
  LGlobe:provinceCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of provinces.
  LGlobe:reachable( start_id, max_cost )  -> table  -- Return all provinces reachable within `max_cost` steps from `start_id`.
  LGlobe:removeArc( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes an arc from the globe map by its unique string identifier.
  LGlobe:removeLabel( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a text label from the globe map by its unique string identifier.
  LGlobe:removeLayer( name )  -> boolean  -- Removes a texture layer from the globe map by its unique string identifier.
  LGlobe:removeMarker( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a marker from the globe map by its unique string identifier.
  LGlobe:removeProvince( id )  -> boolean  -- Removes a province by ID. Returns true if it existed.
  LGlobe:revealAll( viewer )  -> nil  -- Reveal all provinces for a viewer.
  LGlobe:revealProvince( viewer, id )  -> nil  -- Reveal a province for a viewer.
  LGlobe:setActiveViewer( [viewer] )  -> nil  -- Set the faction/viewer whose fog mask filters rendering.
  LGlobe:setBorders( show )  -> nil  -- Enable or disable province border rendering.
  LGlobe:setCamera( lat, lon, z )  -> nil  -- Set the camera position directly.
  LGlobe:setLabelText( id, text )  -> nil  -- Updates the visible text content of an existing globe label.
  LGlobe:setLabelVisible( id, vis )  -> nil  -- Sets whether this specific label is visible on the globe.
  LGlobe:setLayerAlpha( name, alpha )  -> nil  -- Set layer opacity (0.0–1.0).
  LGlobe:setLayerColor( layer, id, r, g, b, a )  -> nil  -- Set a per-province color override on a layer.
  LGlobe:setLayerVisible( name, vis )  -> nil  -- Sets whether this specific texture layer is visible on the globe.
  LGlobe:setMarkerAttr( id, key, val )  -> nil  -- Set a string attribute on a marker.
  LGlobe:setMarkerVisible( id, vis )  -> nil  -- Sets whether this specific marker is visible on the globe.
  LGlobe:setProvinceAttr( id, key, val )  -> boolean  -- Sets a string attribute on a province.
  LGlobe:setRotation( deg )  -> nil  -- Set planet rotation (degrees).
  LGlobe:setTimeOfDay( t )  -> nil  -- Set time of day (0.0–24.0 hours).
  LGlobe:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LGlobe:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LGlobe:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advance globe simulation by dt seconds.
  LGlobe:zoom( factor )  -> nil  -- Zoom the camera by a multiplier (>1 zooms in, <1 zooms out).
```

## lurek.html {#html}

> `lurek.html` — Lightweight pure-Rust HTML/CSS layout engine Lua bindings.

```lua
  lurek.html.isDefaultPrevented( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if `preventDefault` has been called on this event.
  lurek.html.loadDocument( path, [opts] )  -> LHtmlDocument  -- Placeholder for future sandboxed document loading.
  lurek.html.newDocument( [source], [opts] )  -> LHtmlDocument  -- Creates a detached HTML document from markup and optional CSS/viewport options.
  lurek.html.preventDefault( )  -- Prevents the default browser action associated with this event.
  lurek.html.stopPropagation( )  -- Stops the event from bubbling up to parent elements.
  lurek.html.supports( feature )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the active HTML facade supports a named feature.
```

**`LHtmlDocument`** methods:

> Lua wrapper around a shared `HtmlDocument` and its callback registry.

```lua
  LHtmlDocument:addCss( css )  -> nil  -- Appends stylesheet text after existing CSS rules.
  LHtmlDocument:clearCss( )  -> nil  -- Removes all stylesheet rules from this document.
  LHtmlDocument:draw( [x], [y] )  -> nil  -- Builds the current draw command list and discards it for now.
  LHtmlDocument:getElementById( id )  -> LHtmlElement  -- Finds the first element whose id attribute matches the given value, or nil.
  LHtmlDocument:getHtml( )  -> string  -- Returns the source markup used by this document.
  LHtmlDocument:getRoot( )  -> LHtmlElement  -- Returns the root element for this document.
  LHtmlDocument:getViewport( )  -> number  -- Returns the document layout viewport in UI pixels.
  LHtmlDocument:isDirty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether DOM, CSS, viewport, or layout state changed.
  LHtmlDocument:keypressed( key )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a key press and emits a keydown event.
  LHtmlDocument:mousemoved( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse move event.
  LHtmlDocument:mousepressed( x, y, [button] )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse press and emits a minimal click event.
  LHtmlDocument:mousereleased( x, y, [button] )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse release event.
  LHtmlDocument:off( handle )  -> nil  -- Removes a document-level event listener.
  LHtmlDocument:on( event, func )  -> integer  -- Registers a document-level event listener.
  LHtmlDocument:query( selector )  -> LHtmlElement  -- Finds the first element matching a supported selector.
  LHtmlDocument:queryAll( selector )  -> table  -- Returns all elements matching a supported selector in document order.
  LHtmlDocument:relayout( )  -> nil  -- Forces a layout pass immediately.
  LHtmlDocument:setCss( css )  -> nil  -- Replaces this document's stylesheet text.
  LHtmlDocument:setHtml( html )  -> nil  -- Replaces this document's markup and invalidates existing element handles.
  LHtmlDocument:setViewport( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the document layout viewport in UI pixels.
  LHtmlDocument:textinput( text )  -> boolean  -- Forwards text input and emits an input event for focused input elements.
  LHtmlDocument:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LHtmlDocument:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LHtmlDocument:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances document state and runs layout if needed.
  LHtmlDocument:wheelmoved( dx, dy )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse wheel event.
```

**`LHtmlElement`** methods:

> Lua wrapper that references a single element inside a shared `HtmlDocument`.

```lua
  LHtmlElement:addClass( name )  -> nil  -- Adds a CSS class to this element.
  LHtmlElement:appendHtml( html )  -> nil  -- Appends HTML inside this element.

  LHtmlElement:getId( )  -> string  -- Returns this element's id or nil.
  LHtmlElement:getRect( )  -> number  -- Returns this element's last computed layout rectangle.
  LHtmlElement:getStyle( name )  -> string  -- Returns an inline or stylesheet value for a property.
  LHtmlElement:getTagName( )  -> string  -- Returns this element's tag name.
  LHtmlElement:getText( )  -> string  -- Returns this element's text content.
  LHtmlElement:hasClass( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this element has a CSS class.
  LHtmlElement:off( handle )  -> nil  -- Removes an element event listener.
  LHtmlElement:on( event, func )  -> integer  -- Registers an element event listener.
  LHtmlElement:query( selector )  -> LHtmlElement  -- Finds the first descendant matching a selector.
  LHtmlElement:queryAll( selector )  -> table  -- Returns all descendants matching a selector.
  LHtmlElement:remove( )  -> nil  -- Removes this element from the document tree.
  LHtmlElement:removeAttribute( name )  -> nil  -- Removes the named attribute from this element; does nothing if absent.
  LHtmlElement:removeClass( name )  -> nil  -- Removes a CSS class from this element.
  LHtmlElement:setAttribute( name, [value] )  -> nil  -- Sets or removes an attribute value.
  LHtmlElement:setHtml( html )  -> nil  -- Replaces this element's inner HTML.
  LHtmlElement:setId( [id] )  -> nil  -- Sets or removes this element's id.
  LHtmlElement:setStyle( name, [value] )  -> nil  -- Sets or removes an inline style value.
  LHtmlElement:setText( text )  -> nil  -- Replaces this element's text content.
  LHtmlElement:toggleClass( name, [force] )  -> boolean  -- Toggles a CSS class and returns the final state.
  LHtmlElement:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LHtmlElement:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```
