## lurek.network {#network}

> `lurek.network` - Multiplayer networking with ENet, HTTP, TCP, WebSocket, and MessagePack.

```lua
  lurek.network.createLobby( name, port, [player_count], [max_players] )  -> table  -- Creates a LobbyInfo record and broadcasts it once on the local network.
  lurek.network.discoverLobbies( [timeout_ms] )  -> table  -- Listens for LAN lobby announcements for `timeout_ms` milliseconds (default 500).
  lurek.network.newClient( opts )  -> LNetworkHost  -- Creates a client host that connects to a remote server.
  lurek.network.newHost( opts )  -> LNetworkHost  -- Creates a new network host bound to the given address.
  lurek.network.newRuntime( )  -> LNetworkRuntime  -- Creates a background network runtime for async HTTP, TCP, and WebSocket.
  lurek.network.newServer( opts )  -> LNetworkHost  -- Creates a server host that binds to a port and accepts connections.
  lurek.network.pack( value )  -> string  -- Serializes a Lua value to a binary MessagePack string.
  lurek.network.syncEntity( )  -> nil  -- Convenience helper: packs an entity snapshot and broadcasts it to all peers.
  lurek.network.unpack( data )  -> any  -- Deserializes a MessagePack binary string back to a Lua value.
```

**`LNetworkHost`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`NetworkHost`].

```lua
  LNetworkHost:broadcast( channel_id, data, [reliable] )  -> nil  -- Broadcasts data to all connected peers on a channel.
  LNetworkHost:connect( addr_str, [channels], [data] )  -> integer  -- Initiates a connection to a remote host, returning the peer ID.
  LNetworkHost:destroy( )  -> nil  -- Destroys the host, closing the underlying socket.
  LNetworkHost:disconnect( peer_id, [data] )  -> nil  -- Gracefully disconnects a peer.
  LNetworkHost:disconnectLater( peer_id, [data] )  -> nil  -- Disconnects a peer after all queued packets have been sent.
  LNetworkHost:disconnectNow( peer_id, [data] )  -> nil  -- Immediately disconnects a peer without handshake.
  LNetworkHost:flush( )  -> nil  -- Flushes all pending sends immediately.
  LNetworkHost:getAddress( )  -> string  -- Returns the local bind address as a string.
  LNetworkHost:getBandwidthLimit( )  -> table  -- Returns the bandwidth limits as a table with incoming and outgoing fields.
  LNetworkHost:getChannelLimit( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum number of channels per connection.
  LNetworkHost:getConnectedPeerCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of currently connected peers.
  LNetworkHost:getConnectedPeerIds( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of connected peer IDs.
  LNetworkHost:getPeerAddress( peer_id )  -> string  -- Returns the remote address of a peer, or nil if unavailable.
  LNetworkHost:getPeerLimit( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum number of peer slots.
  LNetworkHost:getPeerState( peer_id )  -> string  -- Returns the connection state of a peer as a string.
  LNetworkHost:getPeerStats( peer_id )  -> table  -- Returns a statistics table for a peer.
  LNetworkHost:getRole( )  -> string  -- Returns the multiplayer role of this host ("server", "client", or "host").
  LNetworkHost:getRoundTripTime( peer_id )  -> number  -- Returns the round-trip time estimate for a peer in milliseconds.
  LNetworkHost:isClient( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this host was created as a client.
  LNetworkHost:isDestroyed( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the host has been destroyed.
  LNetworkHost:isServer( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this host was created as a server.
  LNetworkHost:ping( peer_id )  -> nil  -- Sends a ping to a peer to measure round-trip time.
  LNetworkHost:resetPeer( peer_id )  -> nil  -- Resets a peer connection immediately without notifying the remote side.
  LNetworkHost:send( peer_id, channel_id, data, [reliable] )  -> nil  -- Sends data to a specific peer on a channel.
  LNetworkHost:service( )  -> table  -- Polls the network for one event, returning an event table or nil.
  LNetworkHost:setBandwidthLimit( [incoming], [outgoing] )  -> nil  -- Sets the bandwidth limits in bytes per second.
  LNetworkHost:setChannelLimit( limit )  -> nil  -- Sets the channel limit for future connections.
  LNetworkHost:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LNetworkHost:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LNetworkRuntime`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`NetworkRuntime`] for async HTTP/TCP/WebSocket.

```lua
  LNetworkRuntime:httpGet( url, [headers] )  -> integer  -- Convenience: sends an HTTP GET request.
  LNetworkRuntime:httpPost( url, body, [headers] )  -> integer  -- Convenience: sends an HTTP POST request.
  LNetworkRuntime:httpRequest( opts )  -> integer  -- Sends an HTTP request asynchronously. Poll with `poll()` for the response.
  LNetworkRuntime:poll( )  -> table  -- Polls for completed async responses (HTTP, TCP events, WebSocket events).
  LNetworkRuntime:shutdown( )  -> nil  -- Shuts down the background network thread.
  LNetworkRuntime:tcpClose( id )  -> nil  -- Closes the TCP connection identified by the given connection handle.
  LNetworkRuntime:tcpConnect( addr )  -> integer  -- Opens a TCP connection to a remote address.
  LNetworkRuntime:tcpSend( id, data )  -> nil  -- Sends data over a TCP connection.
  LNetworkRuntime:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LNetworkRuntime:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LNetworkRuntime:wsClose( id )  -> nil  -- Closes a WebSocket connection.
  LNetworkRuntime:wsConnect( url )  -> integer  -- Opens a WebSocket connection.
  LNetworkRuntime:wsSend( id, data )  -> nil  -- Sends a text message over a WebSocket connection.
```

## lurek.parallax {#parallax}

> `lurek.parallax` - multi-layer scrolling background system.

```lua
  lurek.parallax.newLayer( opts )  -> LParallaxLayer  -- Creates a new parallax background layer from an options table.
  lurek.parallax.newSet( name )  -> LParallaxSet  -- Creates a new empty parallax set with the given name.
```

**`LParallaxLayer`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a single parallax background layer.

```lua
  LParallaxLayer:clearClamp( )  -> nil  -- Removes scroll clamping so the layer scrolls freely.
  LParallaxLayer:getAutoscroll( )  -> number  -- Returns the autoscroll velocity as `(vx, vy)`.
  LParallaxLayer:getBlendMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the current blend mode as a string.
  LParallaxLayer:getDepth( )  -> number  -- Returns the current floating-point depth.
  LParallaxLayer:getOffset( )  -> number  -- Returns the static offset as `(x, y)`.
  LParallaxLayer:getOpacity( )  -> number  -- Returns the current opacity.
  LParallaxLayer:getScrollFactor( )  -> number  -- Returns the scroll factor as `(x, y)`.
  LParallaxLayer:getTiling( )  -> boolean  -- Returns `true` if seamless infinite tiling is enabled.
  LParallaxLayer:getTint( )  -> number  -- Returns the current tint as `(r, g, b, a)`.
  LParallaxLayer:getZ( )  -> integer  -- Returns the draw-order depth.
  LParallaxLayer:isVisible( )  -> boolean  -- Returns `true` if the layer is currently visible.
  LParallaxLayer:render( cam_x, cam_y )  -> nil  -- Draws the layer using an explicit camera world position.
  LParallaxLayer:renderAuto( )  -> nil  -- Draws the layer using the engine active camera position automatically.
  LParallaxLayer:resetAutoscroll( )  -> nil  -- Resets the autonomous scroll accumulator to zero.
  LParallaxLayer:setAutoscroll( vx, vy )  -> nil  -- Sets the autonomous scroll velocity in world-pixels per second.
  LParallaxLayer:setBlendMode( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the GPU blend mode for this layer.
  LParallaxLayer:setClamp( min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -> nil  -- Clamps the scroll offset to a world-pixel range on each axis.
  LParallaxLayer:setDepth( z )  -> nil  -- Sets the floating-point draw depth for fine-grained layer ordering.
  LParallaxLayer:setOffset( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the static world-pixel position bias added on top of camera scroll.
  LParallaxLayer:setOpacity( a )  -> nil  -- Sets the layer-wide opacity override in `[0.0, 1.0]`.
  LParallaxLayer:setRepeat( rx, ry )  -> nil  -- Sets whether the layer tiles on the X and Y axes.
  LParallaxLayer:setScale( sx, sy )  -> nil  -- Sets the texture display scale factor on each axis.
  LParallaxLayer:setScrollFactor( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the scroll factor relative to camera movement on each axis.
  LParallaxLayer:setTileSize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets explicit tile dimensions in logical pixels.
  LParallaxLayer:setTiling( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables seamless infinite tiling on both axes simultaneously.
  LParallaxLayer:setTint( r, g, b, a )  -> nil  -- Sets the multiplicative RGBA tint applied to all pixels of this layer.
  LParallaxLayer:setVisible( v )  -> nil  -- Shows or hides this layer.
  LParallaxLayer:setZ( z )  -> nil  -- Sets the draw-order depth. Lower values render first (further back).
  LParallaxLayer:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LParallaxLayer:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the autonomous scroll accumulator by `dt` seconds.
```

**`LParallaxSet`** methods:

> Lua-side container that groups `LuaParallaxLayer` objects for scene-level management.

```lua
  LParallaxSet:addLayer( layer )  -> nil  -- Adds a layer to this set.
  LParallaxSet:getName( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of this set.
  LParallaxSet:isVisible( )  -> boolean  -- Returns `true` if the set is currently visible.
  LParallaxSet:layerCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of layers in this set.
  LParallaxSet:removeLayerAt( index )  -> boolean  -- Removes the layer at the given 1-based index.
  LParallaxSet:render( cam_x, cam_y )  -> nil  -- Draws all visible layers in ascending `z` order using an explicit camera position.
  LParallaxSet:renderAuto( )  -> nil  -- Draws all visible layers using the engine active camera position.
  LParallaxSet:setName( name )  -> nil  -- Sets the name of this set.
  LParallaxSet:setVisible( v )  -> nil  -- Shows or hides all layers in this set.
  LParallaxSet:sortByZ( )  -> nil  -- Re-sorts all layers by ascending `z` value.
  LParallaxSet:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LParallaxSet:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances the autoscroll accumulator of every layer by `dt` seconds.
```

## lurek.patterns {#patterns}

> `lurek.patterns` - Software design patterns API.

```lua
  lurek.patterns.newBlackboard( [name] )  -> LBlackboard  -- Creates a new Blackboard shared key-value store.
  lurek.patterns.newCommandStack( [max_size] )  -> LCommandStack  -- Creates a new CommandStack instance.
  lurek.patterns.newDebounce( wait )  -> LDebounce  -- Creates a trailing-edge debounce that fires after the input stream is idle for wait sec...
  lurek.patterns.newEventBus( [name] )  -> LEventBus  -- Creates a new EventBus instance.
  lurek.patterns.newFactory( )  -> LFactory  -- Creates a new Factory instance.
  lurek.patterns.newFunnel( window, [max_entries], [name] )  -> LFunnel  -- Creates a time-windowed event aggregator that flushes on every push when `window` is `0`.
  lurek.patterns.newList( )  -> LList  -- Creates an ordered, resizable list.
  lurek.patterns.newMediator( )  -> LMediator  -- Creates a new named-channel message broker.
  lurek.patterns.newObjectPool( )  -> LObjectPool  -- Creates a new ObjectPool instance.
  lurek.patterns.newObserver( [name] )  -> LObserver  -- Creates a new reactive property Observer.
  lurek.patterns.newPriorityQueue( [name] )  -> LPriorityQueue  -- Creates a stable priority-ordered task queue.
  lurek.patterns.newQueue( [capacity] )  -> LQueue  -- Creates a FIFO queue. capacity=0 means unlimited.
  lurek.patterns.newRelationshipManager( )  -> LRelationshipManager  -- Creates a new entity relationship manager.
  lurek.patterns.newRing( capacity, [name] )  -> LRing  -- Creates a fixed-capacity circular history buffer.
  lurek.patterns.newServiceLocator( )  -> LServiceLocator  -- Creates a new ServiceLocator instance.
  lurek.patterns.newSet( )  -> LSet  -- Creates an unordered set that rejects duplicate values (by string key).
  lurek.patterns.newSimpleState( )  -> LSimpleState  -- Creates a new SimpleState finite state machine instance.
  lurek.patterns.newStack( [capacity] )  -> LStack  -- Creates a LIFO stack. capacity=0 means unlimited.
  lurek.patterns.newStrategy( )  -> LStrategy  -- Creates a new strategy registry.
  lurek.patterns.newThrottle( interval )  -> LThrottle  -- Creates a leading-edge rate limiter that fires at most once per interval seconds.
```

**`LBlackboard`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Blackboard pattern.

```lua
  LBlackboard:clear( key )  -> nil  -- Removes a fact from the blackboard.
  LBlackboard:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Clears all facts from the blackboard.
  LBlackboard:get( key )  -> any  -- Gets a fact from the blackboard.
  LBlackboard:getRevision( )  -> integer  -- Returns the monotonic revision counter (incremented on every write).
  LBlackboard:has( key )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the key has a non-nil value.
  LBlackboard:keys( )  -> table  -- Returns all set fact keys as a table.
  LBlackboard:set( key, value )  -> nil  -- Sets a fact on the blackboard.
  LBlackboard:snapshot( )  -> table  -- Returns all facts as a flat key-value table.
  LBlackboard:unwatch( id )  -> nil  -- Removes a watcher subscription by id.
  LBlackboard:watch( key, callback )  -> integer  -- Subscribes to changes on a specific key (or "*" for all changes).
```

**`LCommandStack`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the CommandStack pattern.

```lua
  LCommandStack:canRedo( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if there is a command available to redo.
  LCommandStack:canUndo( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the most recent command can be undone.
  LCommandStack:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Clears all command history, releasing Lua registry values.
  LCommandStack:execute( name, exec_fn, [undo_fn] )  -> nil  -- Executes a named command and records it in undo/redo history.
  LCommandStack:getCurrentName( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the most recently executed command.
  LCommandStack:getHistorySize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of recorded commands (undo + redo).
  LCommandStack:redo( )  -> boolean  -- Re-executes the next undone command and returns whether it succeeded.
  LCommandStack:undo( )  -> boolean  -- Undoes the most recent command and returns whether it succeeded.
```

**`LDebounce`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Debounce pattern.

```lua
  LDebounce:cancel( )  -> nil  -- Cancels the pending trigger without firing.
  LDebounce:getFireCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of times this debounce has fired.
  LDebounce:isPending( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when a trigger is pending.
  LDebounce:onFire( f )  -> nil  -- Sets the callback invoked when the debounce fires.
  LDebounce:trigger( )  -> nil  -- Records an input event, resetting the idle timer.
  LDebounce:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the idle timer by dt seconds; fires the callback if idle wait expired.
```

**`LEventBus`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the EventBus pattern.

```lua
  LEventBus:clear( event )  -> nil  -- Removes all listeners for a specific event.
  LEventBus:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Removes all listeners on this EventBus.
  LEventBus:emit( ... )  -> nil  -- Dispatches an event, calling all registered listeners in priority order.
  LEventBus:getEvents( )  -> table  -- Returns all event names that have at least one listener.
  LEventBus:getListenerCount( event )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of listeners registered for an event.
  LEventBus:off( id )  -> nil  -- Removes a previously registered event listener by subscription ID.
  LEventBus:on( event, callback, [priority] )  -> integer  -- Registers a listener callback for an event.
```

**`LFactory`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Factory pattern.

```lua
  LFactory:alias( alias, canonical )  -> nil  -- Registers an alias pointing to an existing canonical type name.
  LFactory:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Removes all registered type constructors and aliases.
  LFactory:create( ... )  -> any  -- Creates an instance of the named type by invoking its constructor.
  LFactory:getTypes( )  -> table  -- Returns a table of all registered type names.
  LFactory:has( type_name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the named type (or alias) is registered.
  LFactory:register( type_name, ctor )  -> nil  -- Registers a named type constructor function.
  LFactory:remove( type_name )  -> nil  -- Unregisters a type constructor (and any aliases pointing to it).
```

**`LFunnel`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Funnel (event aggregator) pattern.

```lua
  LFunnel:discard( )  -> nil  -- Discards all buffered entries without flushing.
  LFunnel:flush( )  -> nil  -- Manually flushes all pending entries, invoking the onFlush callback.
  LFunnel:getFlushCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of flushes performed.
  LFunnel:onFlush( f )  -> nil  -- Sets a callback invoked when the funnel flushes. Receives a table of {tag, value} entries.
  LFunnel:pendingCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of buffered entries not yet flushed.
  LFunnel:push( tag, [value] )  -> nil  -- Adds an event to the funnel, flushing immediately when `max_entries` is reached or `win...
  LFunnel:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the window timer by dt seconds; flushes when window expires.
```

**`LList`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for an ordered, resizable list.

```lua
  LList:add( value )  -> nil  -- Appends a value to the end of the list.

  LList:contains( value )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the list contains a value equal to the given Lua value (string/number/b...
  LList:get( index )  -> any  -- Returns the value at a 1-based index.
  LList:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the list is empty.
  LList:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items in the list.
  LList:remove( index )  -> any  -- Removes and returns the value at a 1-based index.
  LList:set( index, value )  -> nil  -- Replaces the value at a 1-based index.
  LList:toArray( )  -> table  -- Returns all items as a Lua table.
```

**`LMediator`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Mediator pattern.

```lua
  LMediator:broadcast( ... )  -> nil  -- Dispatches a message to all handlers across all channels.
  LMediator:channels( )  -> table  -- Returns all registered channel names.
  LMediator:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all channels and handlers.

  LMediator:removeChannel( channel )  -> nil  -- Removes a channel and all its handlers.
  LMediator:send( ... )  -> nil  -- Dispatches a message to all handlers on a channel.
```

**`LObjectPool`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the ObjectPool pattern.

```lua
  LObjectPool:acquire( )  -> any  -- Acquires an available object from the pool.
  LObjectPool:add( value )  -> nil  -- Inserts a pre-built object into the available pool.
  LObjectPool:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Clears all objects from the pool, releasing Lua registry values.
  LObjectPool:getActiveCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of currently active (acquired) objects.

  LObjectPool:release( value )  -> nil  -- Returns an object to the available pool.
```

**`LObserver`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Observer pattern.

```lua
  LObserver:get( key )  -> any  -- Returns the current stored property value for the given observer key, or nil if it has ...

  LObserver:set( key, new_val )  -> nil  -- Sets a property value and fires subscribed watchers.
```

**`LPriorityQueue`** methods:

```lua
  LPriorityQueue:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Removes all items from the queue.

  LPriorityQueue:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items in the queue.

  LPriorityQueue:pop( )  -> any  -- Removes and returns the highest-priority item.
  LPriorityQueue:push( priority, value, [label] )  -> integer  -- Inserts an item with a priority. Higher priorities are dequeued first.
```

**`LQueue`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for a FIFO queue.

```lua
  LQueue:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all values from the queue.
  LQueue:dequeue( )  -> any  -- Removes and returns the front value.

  LQueue:front( )  -> any  -- Returns the front value without removing it.
  LQueue:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the queue is empty.
  LQueue:isFull( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the queue is at its capacity limit.
  LQueue:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items in the queue.
  LQueue:toArray( )  -> table  -- Returns all items as a Lua table (front to back).
```

**`LRing`** methods:

```lua
  LRing:average( )  -> number  -- Returns the average of all numeric values, or 0 if empty.
  LRing:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all entries from the ring.
  LRing:isFull( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the ring is at capacity.
  LRing:latest( )  -> table  -- Returns the most recently pushed entry.
  LRing:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of entries currently in the ring.
  LRing:push( value, [tag] )  -> integer  -- Pushes a number or string value with an optional tag, overwriting the oldest entry on o...
  LRing:sum( )  -> number  -- Returns the sum of all numeric values in the ring.
  LRing:toArray( )  -> table  -- Returns all entries (oldest first) as an array of {id, tag, value?, text?} tables.
```

**`LSimpleState`** methods:

```lua
  LSimpleState:addState( name, [callbacks] )  -> nil  -- Registers a named state with optional enter, exit, and update callbacks.
  LSimpleState:clearAll( )  -> nil  -- Removes all states and callbacks from this state machine.
  LSimpleState:getCurrent( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the current state.

  LSimpleState:transitionTo( name )  -> boolean  -- Transitions to a named state, calling exit/enter callbacks as needed.
  LSimpleState:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Calls the update callback of the current state with the given delta time.
```

**`LStack`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for a LIFO stack.

```lua
  LStack:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all values from the stack.
  LStack:isEmpty( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the stack is empty.
  LStack:isFull( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the stack is at its capacity limit.
  LStack:len( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items on the stack.
  LStack:peek( )  -> any  -- Returns the top value without removing it.
  LStack:pop( )  -> any  -- Removes and returns the top value.
  LStack:push( value )  -> boolean  -- Pushes a value onto the stack.
  LStack:toArray( )  -> table  -- Returns all items as a Lua table (bottom to top).
```

**`LStrategy`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Strategy pattern.

```lua
  LStrategy:clear( )  -> nil  -- Removes all strategies and clears the active selection.
  LStrategy:execute( ... )  -> any  -- Calls the currently active strategy function with the given arguments.
  LStrategy:getCurrent( )  -> string  -- Returns the name of the active strategy.
  LStrategy:has( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if a strategy with this name is registered.
  LStrategy:names( )  -> table  -- Returns all registered strategy names.
  LStrategy:register( name, callback )  -> nil  -- Registers a named strategy function.
  LStrategy:remove( name )  -> boolean  -- Removes a strategy by name.
  LStrategy:set( name )  -> boolean  -- Sets the active strategy by name.
```

**`LThrottle`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Throttle pattern.

```lua
  LThrottle:getFireCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of times this throttle has fired.
  LThrottle:getProgress( )  -> number  -- Returns the normalised progress through the current interval [0, 1].
  LThrottle:onFire( f )  -> nil  -- Sets the callback invoked when the throttle fires.
  LThrottle:reset( )  -> nil  -- Resets the elapsed counter without firing.
  LThrottle:setEnabled( v )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables the throttle.
  LThrottle:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the timer by dt seconds; fires the callback if the interval elapsed.
```

## lurek.pipeline {#pipeline}

> `lurek.pipeline` - DAG-based pipeline orchestrator for composing multi-step workflows.

```lua
  lurek.pipeline.fromTable( def )  -> LPipeline  -- Deserialises a pipeline from a definition table.
  lurek.pipeline.newPipeline( [name] )  -> LPipeline  -- Creates a new empty pipeline.
  lurek.pipeline.newStep( name, [callback] )  -> LPipelineStep  -- Creates a new pipeline step.
```

**`LPipeline`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Pipeline`] DAG.

```lua
  LPipeline:addConditional( name, deps_tbl, cb, cond )  -> LPipeline  -- Adds a conditional step to the pipeline.
  LPipeline:addStep( step_ud )  -> LPipeline  -- Adds a step to the pipeline.
  LPipeline:addSubPipeline( sub_ud, alias, [deps_tbl] )  -> nil  -- Inlines all steps from a sub-pipeline into this pipeline.
  LPipeline:cancel( )  -> nil  -- Cancels all pending and waiting steps.
  LPipeline:clear( )  -> nil  -- Clears all steps from the pipeline.
  LPipeline:getContext( )  -> table  -- Returns the stored asynchronous context table.
  LPipeline:getErrorMode( )  -> string  -- Returns the current error mode.
  LPipeline:getExecutionOrder( )  -> table  -- Returns the topological execution order.
  LPipeline:getName( )  -> string  -- Returns the pipeline name.
  LPipeline:getParallelGroups( )  -> table  -- Returns the pipeline's parallel execution groups.
  LPipeline:getResult( )  -> table  -- Returns the current result table.
  LPipeline:getStep( name )  -> LPipelineStep  -- Returns the step wrapper for the named step.
  LPipeline:getStepCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the total number of steps.
  LPipeline:getSteps( )  -> table  -- Returns all step wrappers in the pipeline.
  LPipeline:getStepsByTag( tag )  -> table  -- Returns all steps with a matching tag.
  LPipeline:isComplete( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether all steps have reached a terminal state.
  LPipeline:isRunning( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the pipeline is running asynchronously.
  LPipeline:onProgress( cb )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback invoked after every step.
  LPipeline:removeStep( name )  -> nil  -- Removes a step from the pipeline by name.
  LPipeline:reset( )  -> nil  -- Resets all step states and clears async pipeline state.
  LPipeline:run( [context] )  -> table  -- Executes the pipeline synchronously in topological order.
  LPipeline:runAsync( [context] )  -> nil  -- Starts an asynchronous pipeline run.
  LPipeline:setErrorMode( mode )  -> nil  -- Sets the pipeline error mode.
  LPipeline:setName( name )  -> nil  -- Renames the pipeline without changing its steps, dependencies, or current runtime state.
  LPipeline:setOnComplete( [cb] )  -> nil  -- Sets the callback invoked when the pipeline completes.
  LPipeline:setOnStepComplete( [cb] )  -> nil  -- Sets the callback invoked when a step completes successfully.
  LPipeline:setOnStepError( [cb] )  -> nil  -- Sets the callback invoked when a step fails.
  LPipeline:toAscii( )  -> string  -- Returns an ASCII diagram of the pipeline DAG.
  LPipeline:toTable( )  -> table  -- Serialises the pipeline definition to a Lua table.
  LPipeline:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua-visible type name for this pipeline.
  LPipeline:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given type name matches this pipeline.
  LPipeline:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the asynchronous pipeline by one tick.
  LPipeline:validate( )  -> boolean  -- Validates the pipeline dependency graph.
```

**`LPipelineStep`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a single [`PipelineStep`].

```lua
  LPipelineStep:dependsOn( dep )  -> LPipelineStep  -- Adds a dependency on another step.
  LPipelineStep:getAttempt( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of execution attempts so far.
  LPipelineStep:getData( key )  -> string  -- Returns a metadata value by key.
  LPipelineStep:getDelay( )  -> number  -- Returns the configured delay in seconds.
  LPipelineStep:getDependencies( )  -> table  -- Returns the dependency step names.
  LPipelineStep:getDependencyCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of declared dependencies.
  LPipelineStep:getDuration( )  -> number  -- Returns the total time spent executing this step.
  LPipelineStep:getError( )  -> string  -- Returns the error message from the last failed attempt.
  LPipelineStep:getName( )  -> string  -- Returns the unique name of this step.
  LPipelineStep:getRetryCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the configured retry count.
  LPipelineStep:getStatus( )  -> string  -- Returns the current execution status.
  LPipelineStep:getTag( )  -> string  -- Returns the tag on this step.
  LPipelineStep:getTimeout( )  -> number  -- Returns the timeout stored in metadata.
  LPipelineStep:isOptional( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether this step is marked as optional.
  LPipelineStep:setCallback( cb )  -> nil  -- Stores the execute callback for this step.
  LPipelineStep:setCondition( [cond] )  -> nil  -- Stores the run condition callback for this step.
  LPipelineStep:setData( key, value )  -> nil  -- Stores a metadata string value on this step.
  LPipelineStep:setDelay( seconds )  -> nil  -- Sets the delay to wait after dependencies finish.
  LPipelineStep:setOnError( [cb] )  -> nil  -- Stores the error callback for this step.
  LPipelineStep:setOptional( optional )  -> nil  -- Sets whether this step is optional.
  LPipelineStep:setRetryCount( count )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum number of retry attempts after failure.
  LPipelineStep:setRetryDelay( seconds )  -> nil  -- Sets the delay between retry attempts.
  LPipelineStep:setTag( tag )  -> nil  -- Sets the tag on this step.
  LPipelineStep:setTimeout( seconds )  -> nil  -- Stores a timeout value in this step's metadata.
  LPipelineStep:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua-visible type name for this step.
  LPipelineStep:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the given type name matches this step.
```

## lurek.procgen {#procgen}

> `lurek.procgen` - Stateless procedural generation utilities.

```lua
  lurek.procgen.bspDungeon( [opts] )  -> table  -- Generates a dungeon using Binary Space Partitioning.
  lurek.procgen.cellularAutomata( w, h, [opts] )  -> table  -- Generates a cave-like map using cellular automata.
  lurek.procgen.floodFill( )  -> table  -- BFS flood fill on a flat grid of bytes.
  lurek.procgen.generateName( )  -> string  -- Generates a single procedural name using a Markov chain.
  lurek.procgen.generateNames( )  -> table  -- Generates N procedural names using a Markov chain.
  lurek.procgen.heightmap( [opts] )  -> table  -- Generates a heightmap using fractal noise.
  lurek.procgen.lsystem( opts )  -> string  -- Generates an L-system string.
  lurek.procgen.lsystemSegments( opts, [angle_deg], [step] )  -> table  -- Generates L-system line segments for rendering.
  lurek.procgen.noiseMap( width, height, [opts] )  -> table  -- Generates a noise map using the configurable NoiseGenerator.
  lurek.procgen.noiseMapParallel( width, height, [opts] )  -> table  -- Generates a noise map using rayon parallel processing.
  lurek.procgen.perlinNoise( x, y, px, py )  -> number  -- Evaluates periodic Perlin noise at a point.
  lurek.procgen.poissonDisk( w, h, min_dist, [max_attempts], [seed] )  -> table  -- Generates Poisson disk sample points using Bridson's algorithm.
  lurek.procgen.roomsDungeon( [opts] )  -> table  -- Generates a rooms-and-corridors dungeon.
  lurek.procgen.simplex2d( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns a single Simplex noise value at the given 2-D coordinate.
  lurek.procgen.simplex3d( x, y, z )  -> number  -- Returns a single Simplex noise value at the given 3-D coordinate.
  lurek.procgen.voronoi( w, h, pts_tbl, [opts_tbl] )  -> table  -- Generates a Voronoi diagram for a set of seed points.
  lurek.procgen.wfcGenerate( opts )  -> table  -- Generates a tile grid using Wave Function Collapse.
  lurek.procgen.worldGraph( width, height, region_count, [seed] )  -> table  -- Generates a world graph with scattered regions and edges.
```

> `lurek.raycaster` - DDA grid raycasting for retro FPS and dungeon-crawler games.

```lua

  lurek.raycaster.newDoorManager( )  -> DoorManager  -- Creates a new empty door manager.

  lurek.raycaster.newPointLight( x, y, r, g, b, radius, intensity )  -> PointLight  -- Creates a point light for use in raycaster scene lighting.
```

```lua
  LDoorManager:getDoor( index )  -> table  -- Returns the state table for door at index, or nil if out of range.
  LDoorManager:openDoor( index )  -> nil  -- Begins opening the door at the given index.

  LDoorManager:update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances all door animations by dt seconds.
```

```lua
  LHeightMap:floorAt( x, y )  -> number  -- Returns the floor height at (x, y). Returns 0.0 for out-of-bounds.
```

**`LRaycaster`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Raycaster2D`] grid.

```lua
  LRaycaster:buildScene( )  -> nil  -- Builds a raycaster scene and stores it in SharedState for GPU rendering.
  LRaycaster:castFloorRow( )  -> table  -- Computes floor (or ceiling) texture UV coordinates for one horizontal screen row.
  LRaycaster:castRay( ox, oy, angle, max_dist )  -> table  -- Casts a single ray and returns a hit table, or nil if nothing was hit.
  LRaycaster:castRayMulti( ox, oy, angle, max_dist, [max_hits] )  -> table  -- Casts a ray collecting up to max_hits wall layers, continuing through
  LRaycaster:castRays( ox, oy, angle, fov, count, max_dist )  -> table  -- Casts multiple rays across a field of view, returns an array of hit tables.
  LRaycaster:castRaysFlat( ox, oy, angle, fov, count, max_dist )  -> table  -- Casts multiple rays and returns a flat array of 5 floats per ray.
  LRaycaster:drawCameraSweep( x, y, fov, max_dist, num_frames, fw, fh )  -> ImageData  -- Renders a mosaic of first-person views from evenly spaced angles to an ImageData.
  LRaycaster:drawDepthMap( )  -> ImageData  -- Renders a depth-map column view to an ImageData.
  LRaycaster:drawLineOfSight( ax, ay, bx, by, scale )  -> ImageData  -- Renders a line-of-sight test between two points to an ImageData.
  LRaycaster:drawTopDown( px, py, angle, scale )  -> ImageData  -- Renders a top-down grid view with player marker to an ImageData.
  LRaycaster:drawView( px, py, angle, fov, w, h, max_dist )  -> ImageData  -- Renders a first-person column view to an ImageData.
  LRaycaster:getCell( x, y )  -> integer  -- Returns the cell value at (x, y).
  LRaycaster:getWallAlpha( tile_type )  -> number  -- Returns the opacity for a wall tile type. Returns 1.0 if not set.
  LRaycaster:height( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid height in cells.
  LRaycaster:isBlocked( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Returns true when the cell at (x, y) is a wall (value > 0).
  LRaycaster:lineOfSight( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> boolean  -- Checks line of sight between two points using DDA traversal.
  LRaycaster:projectSprite( sx, sy, px, py, pa, fov, screen_w )  -> table  -- Projects a world-space sprite onto screen space.
  LRaycaster:setCell( x, y, val )  -> nil  -- Sets the cell value at grid position (x, y).
  LRaycaster:setCells( cells_tbl )  -> nil  -- Replaces all grid cells from a flat array of values in row-major order.
  LRaycaster:setWallAlpha( tile_type, alpha )  -> nil  -- Sets the opacity for a wall tile type. Alpha is clamped to [0, 1].
  LRaycaster:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LRaycaster:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LRaycaster:width( )  -> integer  -- Returns the grid width in cells.
```

```lua
  lurek.terminal.newButton( )  -> Widget  -- Creates a new button widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newLabel( col, row, [text] )  -> Widget  -- Creates a new label widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newList( col, row, width, height )  -> Widget  -- Creates a new scrollable list widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newPanel( col, row, [width], [height] )  -> Widget  -- Creates a new container panel widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newTerminal( [cols], [rows] )  -> Terminal  -- Creates a new terminal grid with the given dimensions.
  lurek.terminal.newTextBox( col, row, width )  -> Widget  -- Creates a new single-line text box widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.nextCmd( term_ud )  -> string  -- Steps one entry forward in command history (toward newer commands).
  lurek.terminal.nextCompletion( prefix )  -> string  -- Returns the next candidate for `prefix`, cycling on repeated calls.
  lurek.terminal.parseAnsi( text )  -> table  -- Parses `text` into colored span tables with optional foreground and background colors.
  lurek.terminal.prevCmd( term_ud )  -> string  -- Steps one entry back in command history (toward older commands).
  lurek.terminal.printAnsi( t_ud, col, row, text )  -> nil  -- Prints ANSI-escaped `text` onto terminal `t` starting at `(col, row)`.
  lurek.terminal.printHighlighted( )  -> nil  -- Prints text at 1-based `(col, row)` with per-keyword colour highlighting.
  lurek.terminal.pushCmdHistory( term_ud, cmd )  -> nil  -- Appends a command string to this terminal's history.
  lurek.terminal.pushScrollback( term_ud, line )  -> nil  -- Appends a line to this terminal's scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.removeCompletion( candidate )  -> nil  -- Removes a candidate string from the tab-completion engine.
  lurek.terminal.resetCompletion( )  -> nil  -- Resets the cycling cursor without clearing the candidate list.
  lurek.terminal.scrollbackLen( term_ud )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of lines currently in this terminal's scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.setScrollbackCap( term_ud, cap )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum number of lines retained in the scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.stripAnsi( text )  -> string  -- Strips all ANSI escape codes from `text` and returns the plain string.
```

**`LTerminal`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Terminal`] with widget binding management.

```lua
  LTerminal:addWidget( widget_ud )  -> nil  -- Attaches a widget to this terminal.
  LTerminal:autoResize( )  -> nil  -- Resizes the window to exactly fit the terminal grid at the current font size.
  LTerminal:clear( )  -> nil  -- Clears all cells to defaults.
  LTerminal:clearWidgets( )  -> nil  -- Detaches all widgets from this terminal.
  LTerminal:get( col, row )  -> nil  -- Returns the cell data at 1-based coordinates.
  LTerminal:getCellSize( )  -> table  -- Returns the active cell size override as `{w, h}`, or `nil` if none is set.
  LTerminal:getDimensions( )  -> integer  -- Returns the terminal grid dimensions.
  LTerminal:getFocused( )  -> nil  -- Returns the currently focused widget, or nil.
  LTerminal:getWidgetCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of attached widgets.
  LTerminal:keypressed( key )  -> boolean  -- Routes a key press to the focused widget and fires callbacks.
  LTerminal:mousepressed( px, py, [button] )  -> nil  -- Routes a mouse press to widgets using pixel coordinates.
  LTerminal:removeWidget( widget_ud )  -> nil  -- Detaches a widget from this terminal.
  LTerminal:render( [x], [y] )  -> nil  -- Renders the terminal grid and widgets as render commands.
  LTerminal:resetCellSize( )  -> nil  -- Removes the cell size override, restoring font-derived cell dimensions.
  LTerminal:set( ... )  -> nil  -- Sets a cell at 1-based coordinates with character FG and BG colours.
  LTerminal:setCellSize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets a per-terminal cell pixel size override, bypassing the font-derived size.
  LTerminal:setFocus( value )  -> nil  -- Sets the focused widget, or clears focus if nil is passed.
  LTerminal:setFont( height )  -> nil  -- Sets the terminal font by pixel height, snapping to the nearest built-in size.
  LTerminal:textinput( text )  -> boolean  -- Routes text input to the focused widget and fires callbacks.
  LTerminal:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTerminal:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LWidget`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Widget`] with attachment and callback state.

```lua
  LWidget:addChild( child_ud )  -> nil  -- Adds a child widget to a panel widget.
  LWidget:addItem( item )  -> nil  -- Adds an item to a list widget.
  LWidget:clearChildren( )  -> nil  -- Removes all children from a panel widget.
  LWidget:clearItems( )  -> nil  -- Removes all items from a list widget.
  LWidget:getChild( index )  -> nil  -- Returns a child widget from a panel by 1-based index, or nil.
  LWidget:getChildCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of children in a panel widget.
  LWidget:getColor( )  -> number  -- Returns the colour of a label or border widget.
  LWidget:getItem( index )  -> string  -- Returns a list item by 1-based index.
  LWidget:getItemCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of items in a list widget.
  LWidget:getMaxLength( )  -> integer  -- Returns the maximum character length of a text box widget.
  LWidget:getPosition( )  -> integer  -- Returns the widget position as 1-based coordinates.
  LWidget:getSelected( )  -> integer  -- Returns the selected item index (1-based) in a list widget, or nil.
  LWidget:getSize( )  -> integer  -- Returns the widget size in cells.
  LWidget:getStyle( )  -> string  -- Returns the border style name of a border widget.
  LWidget:getTag( )  -> string  -- Returns the free-form identification tag.
  LWidget:getText( )  -> string  -- Returns the text content of a label, button, or text box widget.
  LWidget:getTitle( )  -> string  -- Returns the title of a border widget.
  LWidget:isEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the widget accepts input.
  LWidget:isVisible( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the widget is visible.
  LWidget:removeChild( child_ud )  -> nil  -- Removes a child widget from a panel widget.
  LWidget:removeItem( index )  -> nil  -- Removes an item from a list widget by 1-based index.
  LWidget:setColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -> nil  -- Sets the colour of a label or border widget.
  LWidget:setEnabled( enabled )  -> nil  -- Sets whether the widget accepts input.
  LWidget:setMaxLength( max_length )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum character length of a text box widget.
  LWidget:setOnChange( [callback] )  -> nil  -- Registers a text change callback for a text box widget.
  LWidget:setOnClick( [callback] )  -> nil  -- Registers a click callback for a button widget.
  LWidget:setOnSelect( [callback] )  -> nil  -- Registers a selection change callback for a list widget.
  LWidget:setPosition( col, row )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget position from 1-based coordinates.
  LWidget:setSelected( [index] )  -> nil  -- Sets the selected item in a list widget by 1-based index.
  LWidget:setSize( width, height )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget size in cells.
  LWidget:setStyle( style_name )  -> nil  -- Sets the border style of a border widget.
  LWidget:setTag( tag )  -> nil  -- Sets the free-form identification tag.
  LWidget:setText( text )  -> nil  -- Sets the text content of a label, button, or text box widget.
  LWidget:setTitle( title )  -> nil  -- Sets the title of a border widget.
  LWidget:setVisible( visible )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget visibility.
  LWidget:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LWidget:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.tween {#tween}

> `lurek.tween` - Property tweening, sequencing, and spring animation helpers.

```lua
  lurek.tween.cancelAll( )  -> nil  -- Cancels all active tweens, sequences, parallels, and springs immediately.
  lurek.tween.delay( seconds, [cb] )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Creates a started delay sequence that waits and then optionally calls a callback.
  lurek.tween.getActiveCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of currently active tween objects.
  lurek.tween.getEasingNames( )  -> table  -- Returns all available built-in and custom easing names.
  lurek.tween.newState( duration, [easing] )  -> LTweenState  -- Creates a standalone tween state that is not registered with the engine.
  lurek.tween.parallel( )  -> LTweenParallel  -- Creates an empty parallel tween handle.
  lurek.tween.registerEasing( name, f )  -> nil  -- Registers a custom easing function under `name`.
  lurek.tween.sequence( )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Creates an empty tween sequence handle.
  lurek.tween.spring( target_tbl, fields_tbl, [opts] )  -> LSpring  -- Creates a spring animation that drives named table fields toward target values.
  lurek.tween.to( )  -> LTween  -- Creates a tween using `target` as the first argument.
  lurek.tween.tween( )  -> LTween  -- Creates a property tween and registers it for automatic updating.
  lurek.tween.update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances all active tweens, sequences, parallels, and springs by `dt` seconds.
```

**`LSpring`** methods:

> Lua-side spring handle: wraps [`SpringSystem`] and a registry reference to the target table.

```lua
  LSpring:cancel( )  -> nil  -- Stops the spring immediately, clears its settle callback, and leaves the current values...
  LSpring:getPosition( field )  -> number  -- Returns the current interpolated position for the named field.
  LSpring:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the spring is still active.
  LSpring:isSettled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether all spring axes have settled.
  LSpring:setDamping( value )  -> nil  -- Updates the damping coefficient on all axes.
  LSpring:setStiffness( value )  -> nil  -- Updates the stiffness constant on all axes.
  LSpring:setTarget( fields_tbl )  -> nil  -- Updates target values for all fields present in `fields_table`.
  LSpring:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LSpring:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  LSpring:update( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the spring by `dt` seconds.
```

**`LTween`** methods:

> A managed interpolation from start to end values over time.

```lua
  LTween:cancel( ud )  -> nil  -- Cancels this tween immediately; fires the `onCancel` callback if set.
  LTween:getProgress( )  -> number  -- Returns raw 0..1 playback progress (not eased, not accounting for yoyo).
  LTween:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the tween is still running (not completed or cancelled).
  LTween:onCancel( ud, f )  -> LTween  -- Sets a callback called when the tween is cancelled.
  LTween:onComplete( ud, f )  -> LTween  -- Sets a callback to fire when the tween finishes all cycles.
  LTween:onUpdate( ud, f )  -> LTween  -- Sets a callback called every tick with the current eased progress.
  LTween:pause( )  -> nil  -- Pauses this tween; time stops advancing but the tween is not cancelled.
  LTween:resume( )  -> nil  -- Resumes a paused tween, continuing from the position where it was paused.
  LTween:setRepeat( n )  -> nil  -- Sets the number of extra play cycles after the first (0 = play once, -1 = infinite).
  LTween:setYoyo( enabled )  -> nil  -- Enables or disables yoyo (ping-pong) on each repeat cycle.
  LTween:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTween:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LTweenParallel`** methods:

> A group of animations that run simultaneously over the same duration.

```lua
  LTweenParallel:add( par_ud, tw_ud )  -> nil  -- Adds an existing tween handle to the parallel group.
  LTweenParallel:cancel( )  -> nil  -- Cancels the parallel group immediately.
  LTweenParallel:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the parallel is running and not yet complete.
  LTweenParallel:onComplete( ud, f )  -> LTweenParallel  -- Sets a callback fired when all child tweens finish.
  LTweenParallel:start( ud )  -> LTweenParallel  -- Marks the parallel as active.
  LTweenParallel:tween( )  -> LTweenParallel  -- Creates and adds an inline tween entry to the parallel group.
  LTweenParallel:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTweenParallel:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LTweenSequence`** methods:

> A chained sequence of animations that run one after another.

```lua
  LTweenSequence:callback( ud, f )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Appends an immediate callback step to the sequence.
  LTweenSequence:cancel( )  -> nil  -- Cancels the sequence and stops all pending steps.
  LTweenSequence:delay( ud, seconds, [cb] )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Appends a delay step to the sequence.
  LTweenSequence:isActive( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the sequence has been started and has not yet completed.
  LTweenSequence:onComplete( ud, f )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Sets a callback fired when all steps complete.
  LTweenSequence:start( ud )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Marks the sequence as active so `lurek.tween.update(dt)` begins ticking it.
  LTweenSequence:tween( )  -> LTweenSequence  -- Appends a tween step to the sequence.
  LTweenSequence:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTweenSequence:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`LTweenState`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around the pure-Rust [`TweenState`] timing core.

```lua
  LTweenState:isComplete( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the tween state has completed.
  LTweenState:lerp( start, finish )  -> number  -- Interpolates from `start` to `finish` using the eased tween progress.
  LTweenState:reset( )  -> nil  -- Resets the tween state to elapsed time zero.
  LTweenState:t( )  -> number  -- Returns the raw 0..1 playback progress.
  LTweenState:tick( dt )  -> boolean  -- Advances the tween state by `dt` seconds.
  LTweenState:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  LTweenState:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.ui {#ui}

> `lurek.ui` - Retained-mode widget UI system for game HUDs, menus, and overlays.

```lua
  lurek.ui.addToast( toast_table )  -> nil  -- Queues a toast notification from a table.
  lurek.ui.clearFocus( )  -> nil  -- Removes keyboard focus from this widget so key events go to the next focusable.
  lurek.ui.draw( )  -> nil  -- Invokes all registered `on_draw` callbacks with a screen-space rect table.
  lurek.ui.drawToImage( w, h )  -> ImageData  -- Renders the UI widget tree to a CPU ImageData at the given resolution.
  lurek.ui.flushCache( )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if the widget tree changed since the last call, then resets the flag.
  lurek.ui.focusNext( )  -> nil  -- Moves focus to the next focusable widget.
  lurek.ui.focusPrev( )  -> nil  -- Moves focus to the previous focusable widget.
  lurek.ui.getFocus( )  -> number  -- Returns the focused widget index or nil.
  lurek.ui.getRoot( )  -> LPanel  -- Returns the root panel widget table.
  lurek.ui.getTheme( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether a theme is set.
  lurek.ui.getToastCount( )  -> number  -- Returns the number of active toasts.
  lurek.ui.getWidgetCount( )  -> number  -- Returns the total widget count in the context.
  lurek.ui.keypressed( key )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a key press event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.loadLayout( )  -> number  -- Loads a widget tree from a Lua definition table and attaches it to the UI root.
  lurek.ui.loadLayoutFile( path )  -> number  -- Loads a widget tree from a TOML layout file and attaches it to the UI root.
  lurek.ui.mousemoved( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse move event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.mousepressed( x, y, [btn] )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse press event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.mousereleased( x, y, [btn] )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse release event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.newAccordion( )  -> LAccordion  -- Creates a collapsible accordion widget.

  lurek.ui.newImageWidget( )  -> LImageWidget  -- Creates an image display widget.
  lurek.ui.newLabel( [text] )  -> LLabel  -- Creates a text label widget.
  lurek.ui.newLayout( [direction] )  -> LLayout  -- Creates a flexbox layout container.
  lurek.ui.newLineChart( opts )  -> LLineChart  -- Creates a new line chart.
  lurek.ui.newList( )  -> LListBox  -- Creates a selectable list widget.
  lurek.ui.newMenuBar( )  -> LMenuBar  -- Creates a menu bar widget.

  lurek.ui.newPanel( )  -> LPanel  -- Creates a container panel widget.
  lurek.ui.newPieChart( opts )  -> LPieChart  -- Creates and returns a new pie chart widget attached to this image widget.
  lurek.ui.newProgressBar( [min], [max] )  -> LProgressBar  -- Creates a progress bar widget.
  lurek.ui.newRadioButton( [text], [group] )  -> LRadioButton  -- Creates a grouped radio button widget.
  lurek.ui.newScatterPlot( opts )  -> LScatterPlot  -- Creates a new scatter plot.
  lurek.ui.newScrollBar( [vertical] )  -> LScrollBar  -- Creates a scroll bar widget.
  lurek.ui.newScrollPanel( )  -> LScrollPanel  -- Creates a scrollable panel widget.
  lurek.ui.newSeparator( [vertical] )  -> LSeparator  -- Creates a separator line.
  lurek.ui.newSlider( [min], [max] )  -> LSlider  -- Creates a value slider widget.
  lurek.ui.newSpacer( [w], [h] )  -> LSpacer  -- Creates a spacing filler widget.
  lurek.ui.newSpinBox( [min], [max] )  -> LSpinBox  -- Creates a numeric spin box widget with increment and decrement buttons.
  lurek.ui.newSplitPanel( [orientation] )  -> LSplitPanel  -- Creates a resizable split panel.
  lurek.ui.newStatusBar( )  -> LStatusBar  -- Creates a status bar widget.
  lurek.ui.newSwitch( [on] )  -> LSwitch  -- Creates a toggle switch widget.

  lurek.ui.newTextInput( )  -> LTextInput  -- Creates a text input widget.
  lurek.ui.newTheme( )  -> LTheme  -- Creates a new theme instance.

  lurek.ui.setDefaultTheme( )  -> nil  -- Installs the built-in dark theme as the active GUI theme.
  lurek.ui.setFocus( [widget] )  -> nil  -- Sets keyboard focus to a widget or clears it.
  lurek.ui.setTheme( theme_ud )  -> nil  -- Sets the active GUI theme.
  lurek.ui.setViewport( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the viewport dimensions used for anchor constraints and layout.
  lurek.ui.textinput( text )  -> boolean  -- Forwards text input to the focused text input widget.
  lurek.ui.update( dt )  -> nil  -- Advances toast timers, removes expired toasts, and dispatches pending GUI events.
  lurek.ui.update_bindings( )  -> nil  -- Updates widgets whose bound keys match values in the provided data table.
  lurek.ui.wheelmoved( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Forwards a mouse wheel event to the GUI.
```

**`LDialog`** methods:

> Creates a modal dialog widget.

```lua
  LDialog:addButton( text, [cb] )  -> integer  -- Adds a button entry to this Dialog widget.
  LDialog:close( )  -> nil  -- Closes and removes this dialog from the screen.
  LDialog:getContent( )  -> integer  -- Returns the content of this Dialog widget.
  LDialog:getTitle( )  -> string  -- Returns the title of this Dialog widget.
```

**`LUiWidget`** methods:

> Builds a Lua table with common base-widget methods bound to `idx`.

```lua
  LUiWidget:addChild( child )  -> nil  -- Adds a child widget to this container.
  LUiWidget:attachToEntity( entity_id )  -> nil  -- Anchors this widget to a world-space entity by its numeric ID.
  LUiWidget:bind( key )  -> nil  -- Registers a data-binding key on this widget.
  LUiWidget:clearAnchor( )  -> nil  -- Removes all anchor constraints.
  LUiWidget:containsPoint( x, y )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether (x, y) is inside this widget.
  LUiWidget:detachFromEntity( )  -> nil  -- Removes the entity anchor from this widget, restoring normal layout positioning.
  LUiWidget:fadeIn( )  -> nil  -- Instantly fades the widget in (sets alpha to `1.0`).
  LUiWidget:fadeOut( )  -> nil  -- Instantly fades the widget out (sets alpha to `0.0` and hides it).
  LUiWidget:findById( id )  -> table  -- Recursively searches for a widget by id starting from this widget.
  LUiWidget:getAlpha( )  -> number  -- Returns the widget's current alpha transparency.
  LUiWidget:getChildCount( )  -> integer  -- Returns the number of children in this container.
  LUiWidget:getChildren( )  -> table  -- Returns this container's children as widget-handle tables.
  LUiWidget:getFlexGrow( )  -> number  -- Returns the flex-grow factor.
  LUiWidget:getFlexShrink( )  -> number  -- Returns the flex-shrink factor.
  LUiWidget:getId( )  -> string  -- Returns the widget string identifier.
  LUiWidget:getMargin( )  -> number  -- Returns the widget margin (top, right, bottom, left).
  LUiWidget:getMaxSize( )  -> number  -- Returns the maximum widget size.
  LUiWidget:getMinSize( )  -> number  -- Returns the minimum widget size.
  LUiWidget:getPadding( )  -> number  -- Returns the widget padding (top, right, bottom, left).
  LUiWidget:getPosition( )  -> number  -- Returns the widget position.
  LUiWidget:getRect( )  -> number  -- Returns the computed screen-space rectangle after layout.
  LUiWidget:getSize( )  -> number  -- Returns the current width and height of the widget in UI pixels.
  LUiWidget:getState( )  -> string  -- Returns the widget interaction state name.
  LUiWidget:getTooltip( )  -> string  -- Returns the widget tooltip text.
  LUiWidget:getZOrder( )  -> integer  -- Returns the widget z-order.
  LUiWidget:isEnabled( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the widget is enabled.
  LUiWidget:isVisible( )  -> boolean  -- Returns whether the widget is visible.
  LUiWidget:removeChild( child )  -> nil  -- Removes a child widget from this container.
  LUiWidget:setAlpha( alpha )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget's alpha transparency (`0.0` fully transparent, `1.0` opaque).
  LUiWidget:setAnchor( )  -> nil  -- Sets anchor edges (left, top, right, bottom).
  LUiWidget:setAnchorCenter( [cx], [cy] )  -> nil  -- Sets center anchor offsets.
  LUiWidget:setEnabled( v )  -> nil  -- Sets whether the widget is enabled.
  LUiWidget:setFlexGrow( grow )  -> nil  -- Sets the flex-grow factor.
  LUiWidget:setFlexShrink( shrink )  -> nil  -- Sets the flex-shrink factor.
  LUiWidget:setId( id )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget string identifier.
  LUiWidget:setMargin( top, [right], [bottom], [left] )  -> nil  -- Sets widget margin (CSS-like: top, right?, bottom?, left?).
  LUiWidget:setMaxSize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the maximum widget size.
  LUiWidget:setMinSize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the minimum widget size.
  LUiWidget:setOnChange( f )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback invoked when this widget's value changes.
  LUiWidget:setOnClick( f )  -> nil  -- Registers a callback invoked when this widget is clicked.
  LUiWidget:setOnDraw( self, f )  -> nil  -- Stores a custom draw callback for later invocation.
  LUiWidget:setPadding( top, [right], [bottom], [left] )  -> nil  -- Sets widget padding (CSS-like: top, right?, bottom?, left?).
  LUiWidget:setPosition( x, y )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget position.
  LUiWidget:setSize( w, h )  -> nil  -- Sets the width and height of the widget in UI pixels.
  LUiWidget:setTooltip( text )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget tooltip text.
  LUiWidget:setVisible( v )  -> nil  -- Shows or hides the widget; hidden widgets are not rendered or interactive.
  LUiWidget:setZOrder( z )  -> nil  -- Sets the widget z-order for draw sorting.
  LUiWidget:slideIn( x, y )  -> nil  -- Instantly moves the widget to `(x, y)` and makes it visible.
  LUiWidget:slideOut( x, y )  -> nil  -- Instantly moves the widget to the off-screen position `(x, y)` and hides it.
  LUiWidget:type( )  -> string  -- Returns the Lua type name of this widget (e.g. "LButton").
  LUiWidget:typeOf( name )  -> boolean  -- Returns true if this widget is of the given type, "LWidget", or "Object".
```
